Abagize Inteko muri Peyi de Gale (AMs) bahangayikishijwe no 'kuba basa nk’ibipupe (muppets)'
Hari impungenge ku bagize Inteko bamwe na bamwe batanga igitekerezo cy’uko inyito yabo igomba guhinduka ikaba Abadepite (MWPs) (Abagize Inteko Ishinga Amategeko).
Byazamuwe ni uko hari gahunda yo guhindura izina ry’Inteko ikaba Inteko Ishinga Amategeko ya Peyi de Gale.
Abagize Inteko mu ruhando rwa politiki bahangayikishijwe ni uko byatuma bahabwa urw’amenyo.
Umwe mu bagize Inteko uhagarariye ishyaka ry’abakozi yavuze ko ishyaka ahagarariye rihangayikishijwe ni uko iyo nyito "yumvikana nka Twp na Pwp."
Ku basomyi batari abo muri Peyi de Gale: Mu kiwelishi twp bisobanura umusazi naho pwp bigasobanura amazirantoki.
Umwe mu bagize Inteko uhagarariye ishyaka ya Plaid yavuze ko ishyaka ahagarariye ryose uko ryakabaye "ritabyishimiye" kandi ryatanze ibindi byifuzo.
Uhagarariye ishyaka ry’abagendera ku mahame ya cyera muri Peyi de Gale yavuze ko ishyaka ahagarariye "ryiteguye kwakira ibitekerezo bitandukanye" ku byerekeye guhindura izina, ariko yashimangiye ko nta tandukaniro rinini riri hagati y’ijambo MWP (ugize Inteko Ishinga Amategeko) na Muppet (Igipupe).
Ni muri urwo rwego, inyuguti y’Ikiwelishi ya w ivugwa nk’uko abavuga icyongereza cyo muri Yorkshire bavuga inyunguti ya u.
Komisiyo y’Inteko, kuri ubu iri gutegura umushinga w’itegeko ryo guhindura izina yavuze ko: "Icyemezo ndakuka cy’ibisobanuro by’uko abagize Inteko bakwitwa kizifatirwa n’abagize Inteko ubwabo."
Itegeko rigenga leta yo muri Peyi de Gale ryo mu 2017 ryahaye ububasha abagize Inteko ya Peyi de Gale bwo guhindura izina ryayo.
Muri Kamena, Komisiyo yatangaje ibyavuye mu kugisha inama abaturage ku byifuzo aho abaturage benshi bashyigikiye ko Inteko yitwa Inteko Ishinga Amategeko ya Peyi de Gale.
Ku kibazo cyerekeye inyito y’abagize Inteko (AM), Komisiyo yahaye amahirwe menshi ko bakwitwa abagize Inteko Ishinga amategeko ya Peyi de Gale cyangwa WMP, ariko amahitamo ya MWP yarashyigikiwe cyane mu kugisha inama abaturage.
Abagize Inteko basa nk’aho bari gutanga andi mahitamo, ariko kumvikana bikagorana cyane ku Muyobozi ubakuriye, Elin Jones, witezweho gutanga umushinga w’itegeko ku mpinduka mu byumweru.
Itegeko ryerekeye ivugurura ririmo izindi mpinduka ku buryo Inteko ikoramo, harimo amategeko agenga iyirukanwa ry'abagize Inteko (AM) n’imiterere ya komite.
Abagize Inteko bazatora bya burundu ku kibazo cy’uko bakwiye kwitwa ubwo bazaba bungurana ibitekerezo ku itegeko.
Abanyamasedoniya bagiye mu matora ya kamparampaka ku guhindura izina ry’igihugu
Abatora bazatora ku Cyumweru niba bahindura izina ry’igihugu rikaba "Repubulika ya Masedoniya ya Ruguru."
Amatora y’abaturage yashyizweho kugira ngo hakemurwe impaka zimaze imyaka mirongo n’igihugu gituranyi cy’Ubugereki, gifite intara yacyo yitwa Masedoniya.
Leta y’Ubugereki ihereye mu mujyi wa Athens yagiye itsimbarara ivuga ko izina ry’igihugu gituranyi cyo mu majyaruguru risa neza n’izina ry’akarere kayo kandi bituma icyo gihugu cyangirwa kenshi kujya mu Muryango w’ibihugu by’ubumwe bw’Uburayi n’Umuryango wo gutabarana mu bya gisirikare uzwi nka OTAN.
Perezida wa Masedoniya, Gjorge Ivanov, utavuga rumwe ku itora rya kamarampaka ku guhindura izina, yavuze ko atazatora.
Icyakora, abashyigikiye kamarampaka, harimo Minisitiri w’Intebe, Zoran Zaev, bavuga ko guhindura izina ari cyo kiguzi gusa bakwishyura kugira ngo bajye mu Muryango w’ibihugu by’ubumwe bw’Uburayi n’Umuryango wo gutabarana mu bya gisirikare uzwi nka OTAN.
Inzogera zo kuri Kiliziya yitiriwe Mutagatifu Maritini ntizikivuzwa mu gihe kiliziya zo muri Harlem ziri guhura n’ingorane
Bwana Adams ati: "Hakurikijwe amateka, abantu bakuze naganiriye na bo bavuga ko hari akabari n’urusengero muri buri nguni.
"Uyu munsi, nta na kimwe gihari."
Yavuze ko ibura ry’utubari ryumvikana.
Ati: "Abantu basabana mu buryo butandukanye muri iyi minsi".
"Utubari ntabwo tukiri uruganiriro rwo muri karitsiye aho abantu bajyaga ku buryo buhoraho."
Ku byerekeye insengero, ahangayikishijwe n’uko amafaranga aturuka mu kugurisha imitungo atazamara igihe kirekire nk’uko abayobozi babyiteze, "kandi vuba bidatinze ibintu bizasubira aho byatangiriye."
Yongeraho ati: “Insengero zishobora gusimburwa na za aparitoma zirimo ibyumba byinshi zuzuyemo abantu b’amoko atandukanye batazafasha karitsiye gukuma ari ntagatifu.
Ati: "Umubare munini w’abaturage bagura ibyumba muri izo nyubako ari abazungu,"; "bityo, bizatuma iminsi izo nsengero zigenda zifunga igabanuka yose hamwe kubera ko ntibikunze kubaho ko abo bantu bimukiye muri ibyo byumba bazaba abayoboke b’izo nsengero."
Insengero zubatswe n’itorero rigizwe n’abazungu mbere y’aho Harlem iba umujyi wiganjemo abirabura - Abatuye mu mijyi mu 1870, Urusengero rwa Mutagatifu Maritini nyuma y’imyaka icumi.
Itorero ry’abametodisite rigizwe n’abazungu ryimutse mu myaka y’ 1930.
Itorero rigizwe n’abirabura ryasengeraga aho hafi ryahise ryiyitirira izina ry’iyo rusengero.
Urusenge rwitiriwe Mutagatifu Maritini rwagiyemo abo mu itorero ry’abirabura bayobowe na Pasiteri Mukuru John Howard Johnson, wigeze gukomanyiriza abacuruzi bato bakoreraga ku 125 Street, umuhanda munini uriho amaduka y’ubucurizi muri Harlem, akaba yaranze guha akazi cyangwa kuzamura mu ntera abirabura.
Inkongi y’umuriro yo mu 1939 yasize yangije bikomeye inyubako, ariko mu gihe abatuye kuri Paruwasi iyobowe na Pasiteri Johnson bari bafite gahunda yo kongera kubaka, bagurishije inzogera.
Pasiteri Mukuru David Johnson, umuhungu wa Pasiteri Johnson n’uwaragijwe urusengero rwa Mutagatifu Maritini, batewe ishema no kwita iyo nzogera "inzogera y’abakene."
Inzobere yavugije iyo nzogera muri Nyakanga yayise andi mazina: "umutungo mu by’umuco" n’"igikoresho ndangamateka ntasimburwa."
Inzobere, Tiffany Ng ya Kaminuza ya Michigan, nayo yavuze ko ari yo nzogera ya mbere ku isi yavugijwe n’umunyamuziki w’umwirabura, Dionisio A. Lind, akaba yaragiye kuvuza inzogera nini mu Rusengero rwa Riverside mu myaka 18 ishize.
Bwana Merriweather yavuze ko Mutagatifu Maritini atigeze amusimbura.
Ibyabaye kwa Mutagatifu Maritini mu mezi make ashize byari inkuru utapfa gusobanukirwa y’abahanga mu gushushanya inyubako n’abasinye amasezerano, bamwe bazanywe n’abayobozi b’abalayiki b’urusengero, abandi bazanwa na Diyoseze ya Episcopal.
Sakirisitiya: Inama iyoboye Paruwasi, igizwe n’abayobozi b’abalayiki bandikiye Diyoseze muri Nyakanga bayigaragariza impungenge z’uko Diyoseze "yashaka uko yashyikiriza ibiciro" sakirisitiya, nubwo sakirisitiya idafite aho ihuriye no guha akazi abahanga mu gushushanya inyubako n’abasinye amasezerano Diyoseze yohereje.
Bamwe mu baba muri Paruwasi bijujutiye kuba nta gukorera mu mucyo kurangwa ku ruhande rwa Diyoseze.
Ifi ndyanyama yakomerekeje umwana w’imyaka 13 aho bibirira bashakisha udusimba two mu mazi bita homari muri California
Abayobozi bavuze ko ifi ndyanyama yasagariye inakomeretsa umwana w’umuhungu w’imyaka 13 ku wa Gatandatu ubwo yarari kwibira ashakisha udusimba two mu mazi bita homari muri California ku munsi wo gufungura isizeni yahariye udusimba two mu mazi twitwa twa homari.
Uko gusagarirwa kwabaye neza mbere ya 7 z’igitondo hafi y’inkombe z’amazi zizwi nka Beacon muri Encinitas.
Chad Hammel yabwiye televiziyo ya KSWB-TV muri San Diego ko yarari kwibira n’inshuti ze hafi iminota mirongo itatu mu gitondo cyo ku wa Gatandatu ubwo yumvise uwo mwana w’umuhungu asakuza asaba ubufasha maze bagashya ari itsinda kugira ngo bamufashe kumukura mu mazi.
Hammel yavuze ko ubwa mbere yari yabanje gutekereza ko byari urusaku rw’ibyishimo byo gukurikirana udusimba two mu mazi tuzwi nka homari, ariko nyuma aza "kubona ko byari ugutaka, 'Irandiye!
Irandiye!'
Ibyo Hammel yabonye amaze kugera kuri uwo muhungu ati: “Igufa ry’urutugu ryose ryari riri kugaragara,”
Hammel akomeza agira ati: "Navugije induru mbwira buri wese kugira ngo ave mu mazi: 'Dore ifi ndyanyama mu mazi!'".
Umuhungu yajyanwe n’indege ku bitaro bivura abana bya Rady Children's Hospital muri San Diego aho arembeye kuri ubu.
Amoko y’ayo mafi ndyanyama yaba yaragabye icyo gitero ntabwo azwi.
Mu nama ihuza abanyamakuru na Kapiteni ushinzwe kurokora abantu mu mazi witwa Larry Giles yavuze ko ifi ndyanyama yabonywe muri ibyo bice mu byumweru bike byabanje, ariko byagaragajwe ko itari ubwoko bw’ifi ndyanyama ziteza ibibazo.
Giles yakomeje avuga ko uwariwe n’iyo fi yagize ibikomere bikabije mu gice cyo hejuru ku gatuza.
Abayobozi babujije abantu kugera ku nkengero z’inyanja guhera kuri Ponto Beach muri Casablad kugeza kuri Swami's muri Ecinitas mu gihe cy’amasaha 48 ku mpamvu z’iperereza n’umutekano.
Giles yavuze ko hari amoko arenga 135 y’amafi ndyanyama muri ako gace, ariko amenshi muri yo afatwa ko atateza ibibazo.
Gahunda za Sainsbury zo kwinjira ku isoko ry’ibikoresho by’ubwiza mu Bwongereza
Sainsbury iri gusatira Boots, Superdrug na Debenhams ikoresheje uburyo bwo gucururiza ibikoresho by’ubwiza mu maduka manini hamwe n’abafasha abaguzi b’inzobere.
Nka kimwe mu bigize igikorwa gikomeye cyo kujya ku isoko ry’ibikoresho by’ubwiza ryo mu Bwongereza rifite agaciro ka miriyari 2,8 z’amadorali, rikomeje gutera imbere mu gihe ubucuruzi bw’imideri n’ibikoresho byo mu rugo bukomeje gusubira inyuma, amaduka manini acuruza ibikoresho by’ubwiza azakorerwa igerageza mu maduka 11 ari mu ntara kandi bigere no ku yandi maduka umwaka utaha igihe bizaba bigaragaje ko byatanze umusaruro.
Ishoramari mu bikoresho by’ubwiza riza rimeze nko guhiga uko amasoko ya kijyambere akoresha umwanya wa za etajeri ukoresha hashyirwaho za televiziyo, mikorowonde n’ibikoresho byo mu rugo.
Sainsbury's yavuze ko ishobora gukuba kabiri ingano y’ibikoresho by’ubwiza icuruza bikagera ku bicuruzwa 3 000, harimo iby’inganda zikomeye nka Revlon, Essie, Tweezerman na Dr. PawPaw ku nshuro ya mbere.
Amoko asanzweho uhereye kuri L'Oreal, Maybelline na Burt's Bees na yo azabona umwanya uhagije w’ahashyirwa ibicuruzwa by’inganda zikomeye bimeze kimwe nk’uko bimeze mu maguriro nka Boots.
Isoko rya kijyambere na ryo riri kongera gushyira ahagaragara butiki y’ibikoresho by’ubwiza kugira ngo ibyinshi mu bicuruzwa bibe bibereye abatarya inyama; kikaba ari ikintu gikomeza gusabwa n’abagura ibicuruzwa bakiri bato.
Kandi, ucuruza imibavu yo mu iduka rya Fragrance Shop azasuzuma uko twakorera mu maduka abiri ya Sainsbury’s, irya mbere ryafunguye muri Croydon, mu majyepfo ya London, mu cyumweru gishize mu gihe irya kabiri rizafungura muri Selly Oak, Birmingham, mu mpera z’uyu mwaka.
Guhahira kuri interineti n’impinduka ku kugura ingano nto y’ibiribwa buri munsi mu maduka yo muri karitsiye bisobanuye ko amaduka manini agomba gukora ibirenze kugira ngo areshye abantu baza kuyahahiramo.
Mike Coupe, umuyobozi mukuru wa Sainsbury's, yavuze ko utwo tuduka tuziyongera nk’amaduka ya rutura mu gihe amaduka manini agerageza guhangana n’abaganya ibiciro barimo Aldi na Lidl batanga serivisi nyinshi kandi zitarimo iby’ibiribwa.
Sainsbury's yagiye ishyira amaduka mato ya Argos mu maduka menshi arenga amajana kandi yanafunguye amaduka yitwa Habitats kuko yaguze iryo zina ry’ayo maduka yombi mu myaka ibiri ishize, bika bivuze ko byongereye igurishwa ry’ibiribwa binatuma haboneka inyungu yisumbuyeho.
Igikorwa cyo kugerageza cyakozwe n’iduka rinini ryo guhindura amashami yaryo agurisha ibikoresho by’ubwiza na farumasi byarangiye ihombye.
Sainsbury's yagerageje uburyo bwo guhuza ibikorwa by’ubucuruzi na Boots mu ntangiriro za 2000s, ariko iyo mikoranire yarangiye mu bwumvikane buke ku buryo bagabana amafaranga yinjijwe avuye mu maduka acuruza imiti muri maduka manini yayo.
Ingamba nshya zije nyuma y’aho Sainsbury's yagurishije na Celesio amaduka ya farumasi angana na 281, akaba ari we nyiri maduka ya Lloyds Pharmacy, ku mafaranga agera kuri miriyoni 125 z’amapawundi, mu myaka itatu ishize.
Bivugwa ko Lloyds yagira uruhare muri gahunda, yongera andi moko ahenze y’amavuta yo ku mubiri harimo La Roche-Posay na Vichy akajya mu maduka ane.
Paul Mills-Hicks, umuyobozi ushinzwe ubucuruzi muri Sainsbury's, yagize ati: "Twahinduye uko ibintu bigaragara ni uko wumva bimeze mu gice cy’iduka cy’ibikoresho by’ubwiza mu rwego rwo kunoza aho abakiriya bacu bahahira.
Twanatumiye bagenzi bacu babihuguriwe by’umwihariko bazaba bari hafi kugira ngo batange inama.
Amoko yacu yakozwe mu rwego rwo kujyana na buri gikenewe no gukurura no kuba ari ahantu habereye bikaba bivuze ko ubu turi abo wahanaho ukeneye ibikoresho by’ubwiza bikaba bigira icyo bihindura ku buryo bwa kera bw’imihahire."
Peter Jones 'yarakaye cyane' nyuma y’aho Holly Willoughby yikuye mu bwumvikane bwa miriyoni 11 z’amapawundi
Uwakinnye muri filime ya Dragons Den ari we Peter Jones yasigaye 'yarakaye cyane' nyuma y’aho umunyamakuru wa televiziyo ari we Holly Willoughby yikuye mu bwumvikane bwa miriyoni 11 z’amapawundi bwo mu bucuruzi mu by’imibereho yo mu rwego rwo hejuru kugira ngo yibande ku masezerano ye mashya afitanye na Marks and Spencer na ITV
Willoughby nta gihe afite cy’imyambaro yabo yo mu rugo ndetse na sosiyete icuruza ibijyanye n’imirimbo izwi nka Truly.
Imikoranire mu bucuruzi y’abo bombi igereranywa na sosiyete ya Gwyneth Paltrow yitwa Goop.
Umunyamakuru w’ikiganiro cya This Morning, w’imyaka 37, yagiye kuri Instagram gutangaza ko asezeye.
Holly Willoughby yasize umukinnyi wa Dragons" Den ari we Peter Jones arakaye cyane nyuma yo kwikura mu bikorwa by’ubucuruzi bya sosiyete ikora iby’imibereho yo mu rwego rwo hejuru birimo amafaranga ku munota wa nyuma kugira ngo yibande ku masezerano ye bwite arimo amafaranga menshi yagiranye na Marks & Spencer na ITV.
Abatanze amakuru bavuga ko Jones yari "yarakaye cyane" ubwo umukobwa ukunzwe kuri TV yemeraga mu kiganiro gikomeye cyo ku wa Kabiri ku cyicaro gikuru cy’ibikorwa by’ubucuruzi bye muri Marlow, Buckinghamshire, ko amasezerano ye mashya afite agaciro kagera kuri miriyoni 1,5 z’amapawundi; bikaba bivuze ko atagifite igihe gihagije cyo kubonera umwanya isosiyete ikora imyenda yo kwambara mu rugo n’ibijyanye na yo izwi nka Truly.
Ibikorwa by’ubucuruzi bigereranywa nk’ibya sosiyete ya Gwyneth Paltrow yitwa Goop kandi yitezweho gukuba kabiri amafaranga ya Willoughby's abarirwa muri miriyoni 11 z’amapawundi.
Mu gihe Willoughby, w’imyaka 37, yajyaga kuri Instagram kugira ngo atangaze ko asezeye muri Truly, Jones yafashe indege ava mu Bwongereza ajya muri imwe mu mazu ye aruhukiramo.
Uwatanze amakuru yagize ati: "Truly ntabwo ya inegereye ibyo Holly yari yarashyize imbere.
Byari bigiye kuba ahazaza he h’igihe kirekire hari kumugeza mu myaka mirongo ikurikira.
Icyemezo yafashe cyo kubivamo cyatunguye abantu bose byarebaga.
Nta muntu wari kwizera ibyari bibaye ku wa Kabiri, kuko byari biri hafi gutangizwa.
Hari inzu y’ububiko yuzuyemo ibicuruzwa muri Marlow HQ biteguye ku buryo byagurishwa."
Inzobere zizera ko ukugenda k’umunyamakuru w’ikiganiro cya This Morning, akaba ari umwe mu bantu bazwi mu Bwongereza binjiza amafaranga, bishobora gutuma icyo kigo gihomba amamiriyoni bitewe n’ishoramari rikomeye mu bicuruzwa bihera ku misego na za buji bikagera ku myenda n’imyenda yo kwambara mu rugo ndetse no kuba byarushaho gutinza itangizwa ryayo.
Kandi bishobora kuba bisobanuye iherezo ry’ubucuti bw’igihe kirekire.
Willoughby ufite abana batatu n’umugabo we Dan Baldwin babaye inshuti za hafi za Jones n’umugore we Tara Capp imyaka icumi.
Willoughby yashinze Truly hamwe na Capp mu 2016 na Jones, w’imyaka 52, yaje nk’umuyobozi mukuru muri Werurwe.
Iyo miryango yombi ikorera ibiruhuko hamwe naho Jones akaba afite 40 ku ijana by’imigabane muri sosiyete itunganya ibiganiro bya televiziyo ya Baldwin.
Byitezwe ko Willoughby aba ambasaderi wa sosiyete ya M&S maze agasimbura Ant McPartlin nk’uyobora ikiganiro cya ITV cyitwa I'm A Celebrity.
Mu ijoro ryakeye, uwatanze amakuru uba bya hafi na Jones yagize ati: "Ntidushobora kugira icyo tuvuga ku bikorwa by’ubucuruzi bye."
Twagiranye ikiganiro gikomeye 'maze turakundana'
Yateye urwenya ku byo yanengwa mu itangazamakuru atanze igitekerezo cy’uko bamwe babifata avuze ko "bitabereye perezida" ndetse no kuba yemera cyane umuyobozi wa Koreya ya Ruguru.
Kubera iki Perezida yatanze byinshi cyane?
Trump yavuze mu buryo bwo kunenga mu ijwi ry’"usoma amakuru".
"Ntacyo nigeze ntanga."
Yavuze ko Kim ashishikajwe n’inama ya kabiri nyuma y’inama yabanje yabereye muri Singapuru muri Kamena yashimwe na Trump ko ari intambwe nini itewe mu gutuma Koreya ya Ruguru ireka umugambi wo gukora ibisasu bya kirimbuzi.
Ariko ibiganiro byo kureka gukora ibisasu bya kirimbuzi bigenda gahoro.
Amezi arenga atatu nyuma y’inama yo muri Kamena yo muri Singapuru, umuporomate wo mu rwego hejuru witwa Ri Yong Ho wa Koreya ya Ruguru yabwiye abayobozi b’isi mu Nteko Rusange y’Umuryango w’abibumbye ku wa Gatandatu ko Koreya ya Ruguru itabona "igisubizo kijyanye" cy’Amerika ku bikorwa bya Koreya ya Ruguru byo kureka intwaro za kirimbuzi hakiri kare.
Ahubwo yavuze ko Amerika ikomeje ibihano bigamije gukomeza igitutu.
Trump yatanze igitekerezo kirimo icyizere mu ijambo yavuze ari kwiyamamaza.
"Koreya ya Ruguru tumeranye neza," ni ko yavuze.
"Twari tugiye kurwana na Koreya ya Ruguru.
Abantu amamiriyoni bakabaye barapfuye.
None ubu, dufitanye uyu mubano mwiza."
Yavuze ko ibikorwa bye byo kunoza umubano na Kim byatanze ibisubizo byiza, bigatuma kugerageza ibisasu bya misire bihagarara, bifasha mu kubohora imbohe no gutuma abanyamerika b’abakozi bari basigaye basubira mu rugo.
Kandi yavuganiye uburyo bwe budasanzwe akoresha mu kuvuga ibyerekeye umubano we na Kim.
"Biroroshye cyane kuba perezida, ariko aho kugira abantu 10 000 bari hanze bagerageza kwinjira muri iki cyumba cyuzuye, twagira abantu nka 200 bahagarara hano," byavuzwe na Trump atunga urutoki ku kivunge cy’abantu bari bamuhagaze imbere.
Tsunami n’umutingito byo muri Indoneziya byashegeshe ikirwa maze bihitana abantu barenga amajana
Urugero, nyuma y’umutingito wa Lombok, imiryango mpuzamahanga itegamiye kuri leta yabwiwe ko idakenewe.
Nubwo abaturage barenga 10 ku ijana bo muri Lombok bavuye mu byabo, nta kiza ku rwego rw’igihugu kigeze gitangazwa, bikaba ari byo bibanza gusabwa kugira ngo hatangwe inkunga mpuzamahanga.
Bwana Sumbung ati: "Ikibabaje ni uko ahanini byagaragaraga neza ko batari gusaba inkunga mpuzamahanga, rero biragoye.”
Mu gihe umuryango wa Save the Children uri gushaka itsinda ryo kujya muri Palu, ntabwo uramenya neza niba abakozi b’abanyamahanga bashobora gukorera muri ako gace.
Bwana Sutopo, umuvugizi w’ikigo cy’igihugu gishinzwe kurwanya ibiza yavuze ko abayobozi ba Indoneziya bari gusuzuma uko ibintu bimeze muri Palu kugira ngo barebe niba imiryango mpuzamahanga yakwemererwa gutanga umusanzu w’inkunga.
Bitewe ni uko muri Indoneziya hakunda kuba umutingito, igihugu gikunda guterwa n’ibiza kititeguye.
Mu gihe hubatswe aho guhingira tsunami muri Aceh, si ko bigaragara ku cyindi gice cy’inkombe.
Kuba nta majwi aburira ko tsunami igiye kuza muri Palu, nubwo hari uburyo bwo kuburira buhari, birashoboka cyane ko byagize uruhare mu gutuma abantu bapfa.
Akenshi, gukorera ingendo hagati y’ibirwa byinshi bya Indoneziya biragorana.
Ibiza bituma ibikoresho bigorana kurushaho.
Ubwato burimo ibitaro bwaparitswe muri Lombok kugira ngo buvure abakomerekejwe n’umutingito buri mu nzira bugana Palu, ariko bizafata byibuze iminsi itatu kugira ngo bugere ahantu hashya hari ibiza.
Mu kwiyamamaza, Perezida Joko Widodo yagize iturufu ibikorwa byo kunoza ibikorwaremezo bya Indoneziya byangiritse kugira ngo azatorwe kandi yakoresheje nabi amafaranga yubaka imihanda n’inzira za gari ya moshi.
Ariko kutabona amafaranga yo gukoresha imishinga itandukanye ni byo byaranze ubutegetsi bwa Bwana Joko mu gihe ahanganye no kuba yakongera gutorwa umwaka utaha.
Bwana Joko anafite igitutu gituruka ku ntambara z’amadini atandukanye muri Indoneziya aho abagize umubare munini w’abayisilamu barushijeho kugendera ku mahame ya kera mu myizerere yabo.
Abantu barenga 1 000 barishwe ndetse n’ibihumbi by’abantu bata ingo zabo ubwo insoresore z’abakirisitu n’abayisilamu zarwaniraga ku mihanda, zikoresha imihoro, imiheto n’imyambi n’izindi ntwaro gakondo.
Reba: Umukinnyi wa Liverpool witwa Daniel Sturridge yatsinze igitego cyo kwishyura ubwo bahuraga na Chelsea
Daniel Sturridge yarokoye Liverpool muri Shampiyona yo mu Bwongereza atuma idatsindwa na Chelsea aho yatsinze igitego ku munota wa 89 ku wa Gatandatu kuri sitade ya Stamford Bridge muri Londere.
Sturridge yaherejwe umupira na Xherdan Shaqiri mu gihe yarari mu ntera ya metero 27 uvuye ku izamu rya Chelsea aho ikipe ye yari yatsinzwe 1-0.
Umupira awuganisha ibumoso bwe mbere yo gutera ishoti rigana ku ipoto rya kabiri.
Iryo shoti yariteye rigana ku nguni y’iburyo hejuru bw’izamu.
Umupira wageze aho uramanuka unyura kuri Kepa Arrizabalaga maze unyeganyeza urushundura.
Sturridge aganira na LiverpoolFC.com ati: "Narindi kugerageza kujya muri uwo mwanya kugira ngo mbone umupira kandi abakinnyi nka Shaq bahora bakina basatira uko bishoboka, rero nagerageje gushaka uko nabona umupira ku buryo bushoboka.”
"Nabonye Kante aza maze nkora ku mupira rimwe, sinigeze mbitekerezaho cyane maze ntera ishoti."
Chelsea yari iyoboye n’igitego 1-0 mu kiruhuko cy’igice cya mbere nyuma yo gutsinda ku munota wa 25 igitego gitsinzwe n’umubiligi w’icyamamare Eden Hazard.
Umukinnyi ukina usatira izamu w’abambara ubururu yatanze pase y’agatsitsino ahereza Mateo Kovacic muri uwo mukino, mbere yo kwiruka agana mu kibuka hagati ajya mu gice cya Liverpool.
Kovacic yakiye ahita atanga umupira mu kibuga hagati.
Noneho atera ishoti ryiza cyane rigana kuri Hazard waruri mu rubuga rw’amahina.
Hazard yarirutse asiga abarinda izamu maze umupira awutera mu rushundura akoresheje ikirenge cy’ibumoso unyura kuri muzamu wa Liverpool ari we Alisson Becker.
Liverpool ihanganye na Napoli mu mikino y’amatsinda y’Irushanwa ry’amakipe yabaye aya mbere iwayo mu Burayi rizwa inka Champions League saa 3 z’umugoroba ku wa Gatatu kuri sitade ya Stadio San Paolo muri Naples, mu Butaliyani.
Chelsea izahura na Videoton mu Irushanwa rya UEFA Europa League saa 3 z’umugoroba ku wa Kane i Londere.
Umubare w’abamaze guhitanwa na tsunami muri Indoneziya wazamutse ugera kuri 832
Umubare w’abahitanwe n’umutingito na tsunami muri Indoneziya wazamutse ugera kuri 832, ikigo cy’igihugu gishinzwe kurwanya ibiza cyabitangaye mu masaha ya kare yo ku Cyumweru.
Byavuzwe ko abantu benshi baheze mu bisigazwa by’inzu yashennywe n’umutingito uri ku gipimo cya 7,5 wabaye ku wa Gatanu maze utera umuvumba ufite uburebure bwa metero 6, umuvugizi w’ikigo ari we Sutopo Purwo Nugroho yabivugiye mu nama n’abanyamakuru.
Umujyi wa Palu, utuwemo n’abantu barenga 380 000, wuzuyemo ibisigazwa byaguye bivuye ku nyubako.
Polisi yafashe umugabo, w’imyaka 32, ukekwaho ubwicanyi nyuma y’aho umugore atwe icyuma agapfa
Iperereza ku bwicanyi ryaratangiye nyuma y’aho umubiri w’umugore wabonetse muri Birkenhead, Merseyside muri iki gitondo.
Umugore w’imyaka 44 yabonywe saa 7:55 z’igitondo afite ibikomere by’umuntu watewe icyuma muri Grayson Mews ku muhanda wa John Street, aho umugabo w’imyaka 32 yafashwe akekwaho kuba ari we wamwishe.
Polisi yasabye abantu batuye muri ako gace babonye cyangwa bumvise ikintu icyo ari cyo cyose kuza bagatanga amakuru.
Umupolisi ushinzwe gukora ipeerereza ku byaha ari we Insipegiteri Brian O'Hagan yagize ati: 'Iperereza ni bwo rigitangira ariko nasaba buri wese waruri muri ako gace k’umuhanda wa John muri Birkenhead wabonye cyangwa wumvise ikintu akeka kubitumenyesha.
Nanashimishwa igihe umuntu wese; by’umwihariko, abatwara tagisi, bashobora kuba bagize amashusho bafata na kamera zo kuri dashibodi zabo kubitumenyesha kuko bashobora kuba bafite amakuru y’ingenzi mu iperereza turi gukora.'
Umuvugizi wa Polisi yemeje ko umurambo w’uwo mugore wabonetse mu gace ka Birkenhead uboneka mu mu nzu.
Nyuma ya saa sita uyu munsi, inshuti zizera ko zizi uwo mugore zageze ahabereye icyaha kugira ngo zibaze ibibazo ku byerekeye aho yabonetse muri iki gitondo.
Iperereza riracyakomeje mu gihe Polisi yavuze ko hari gutegurwa uburyo bwo kumenyesha abavandimwe ba hafi ba nyakwigendera.
Umushoferi wa tagisi utuye muri Grayson Mews yagerageje gusubira muri etaje atuyemo ariko ari kubwirwa na Polisi ko nta muntu n’umwe wemerewe kwinjira cyangwa gusohoka muri iyo nyubako.
Yavuze icyo avuga ubwo yamenyaga ibyabaye.
Ubu, abahatuye babwiwe ko bizafata amasaha menshi kugira ngo bemererwe kongera kwinjiramo.
Humvikanye umupolisi abwira umuntu ko ako gace kose ubu kari gufatwa nk’agace kabereyemo icyaha.
Umugore yagaragaye aririra ahabereye icyaha.
Yakomeje kuvuga ngo: 'Biteye ubwoba cyane'.
Saa 2 z’umugoroba, abapolisi babiri bari imbere y’agace kabereyemo icyaha n’indi kamyoneti iparitse hanze.
Abapolisi benshi bari bahagaze imbere y’ahabereye icyaha bagenzura za etaje zitandukanye.
Umuntu wese ufite amakuru yasabwe guhita yandikira @MerPolCC, agahamagara 101 cyangwa akabimenyesha Urwego rushinzwe gukumira ibyaha ruzwi nka Crimestoppers atavuze amazina ye kuri 0800 555 111, havuzwe ibyanditse muri raporo 247 yo ku wa 30 Nzeli.
Ikibumbano cya Cromwell kiri ku Nteko Ishinga Amategeko cyabaye urwibutso ruheruka rwagezweho n’ikibazo cyo 'kongera kwandika amateka'
Uko kubuza kumanika icyo kibumbano bizafatwa nko guhana kubera gusenya ibikoresho by’umuco n’iby’idini by’abongereza bimeze nk’ibyakozwe n’aba taliban bikozwe n’abafana n’abayoboke ba Puritan.
Ariko Sosiyete ya Cromwell yasobanuye icyifuzo cya Bwana Crick nk’icy’"ubusazi" kandi ko ari "kugerageza kongera kwandika amateka."
John Goldsmith, umuyobozi wa Sosiyete ya Cromwell yagize ati: "Ntaho byari guhungirwa muri iki kiganiro ku byerekeye kuvanaho ibibumbano bigaragaza ishusho ya Oliver Cromwell hanze y’Ingoro ya Westminster na byo byakwibasirwa.
Ni ikibumbano kigaragaza ishusho y’intambara z’imbere mu gihugu mu Bwongereza kanti nta n’imwe yigeze isabwa gushorwa cyangwa yarwanywe na Cromwell.
Ahari ikibi Cromwell yabambirwa ni ibikorwa y’umukurambere we Thomasi wo mu kinyejana cyabanje.
Uko nyakubahwa William Hamo Thorneycroft agaragazamo Cromwell ni ikimenyetso cy’ibyo mu kinyejana cya 19 mu bijyanye n’ibitekerezo na kimwe mu bigize amateka y’ibibumbano aho benshi bizera ko bigikwiye kwishimirwa.
Bwana Goldsmith yabwiye ikinyamakuru cya The Sunday Telegraph ko: "Cromwell afatwa nka benshi, ahari mu mpera z’ikinyejana cya 19 kurusha uyu munsi, nk’uwahariye ubusugire bw’Inteko Ishinga Amategeko ntihure n’igitutu cy’abo hanze mu kujya ku ngoma ya cyami.
Yaba ari ko bigaragazwa uko byakabaye ni ingingo ikomeza kuganirwaho mu ruhando rw’amateka.
Ikiri cyo ni uko amakimbirane yo hagati mu kinyejana cya 17 yatewe n’iterambere ry’ibihugu byacu kandi Cromwell ni umuntu ku giti cye uzwi ugaragaza uruhande rumwe rw’ayo macakubiri.
Ibyo yagezeho nka Lord Protector na byo bikwiye kwishimirwa no kwibukwa."
Ingurube y’inyicanyi yarire umworozi w’umushinwa kugeza ashizemo umwuka
Umworozi yasagariwe anicwa n’ingurube mu isoko ryo mu majyepfo y’uburengerazuba bw’Ubushinwa, hakurikijwe amakuru aturuka mu bitangazamakuru.
Uwo mugabo, uzwi gusa ku rindi zina rya "Yuan," yasanzwe yapfuye aho umutsi w’umujyana wacitse, yuzuye amaraso yafi y’ikiraro cy’ingurube muri Liupanshui mu ntara ya Guizhou, ikinyamakuru cya South China Morning Post cyabitangaje ku Cyumweru.
Umworozi w’ingurube ari kwitegura gukingira ingurube mu kiraro cy’ingurube tariki ya 30 Gicurasi 2005 muri Xining mu ntara ya Qinghai Province, mu Bushinwa.
Bivugwa ko yari yagiye kwa mubyara we wo mu ntara ya Yunna baturanye ku wa Gatatu kugira ngo agurishe ingurube 15 ku isoko.
Igitondo cyakurikiyeho, mubyara we yamusanze yapfuye maze asanga urugi rw’ikiraro cy’ingurube cyari kihegereye rufunguye.
Yavuze ko mu kiraro cy’ingurube harimo ingurube y’isekurume y’ingurube ifite amaraso mu munwa wayo.
Isuzuma ry’ibimenyetso hakoreshejwe siyansi ryemeje ko ingurube y’ibiro 226 yariye uwo mworozi kugeza apfuye, hakurikijwe ibyo raporo yagaragaje.
Mubyara we wamuvugaga ku rindi zina rya: "Amaguru ya mubyara wanjye yari ariho amaraso kandi yarumwe bikomeye,", nk’uko amagambo ye yakoreshejwe n’ikinyamakuru cya Guiyang Evening News.
Videwo yafashwe na kamera y’umutekano yerekanye Yuan yinjira mu isoko saa 4:40 z’igitondo ku wa Kane kugira ngo agaburire ingurube ze.
Umubiri we wabonetse hafi nyuma y’isaha.
Inyamaswa yishe uwo muntu ntabwo yari iya Yuan cyangwa mubyara we.
Umuyobozi w’isoko yabwiye ikinyamakuru cya Evening News ko inguruye yafungiranywe kugira ngo hirindwe ko igira undi yibasira mu gihe polisi iri gukusanya ibimenyetso by’ahabereye icyaha.
Umuryango wa Yuan n’ubuyobozi bw’isoko byavuze ko buri kuganira ku mpuzamarira y’urupfu rwe.
Nubwo bidakunze kubaho, ibibazo by’ingurube zibasira abantu byabayeho na mbere.
Mu 2016, ingurube yibasiye umugore n’umugabo we mu kiraro cyazo muri Massachusetts, aho yasize umugabo yakomeretse bikomeye.
Mu myaka icumi yabanje, ingurube y’ibiro 295 yafatishije umworozi wo muri Peyi de Gale ku modoka ye kugeza umugore akanze iyo ngurube ikamurekura.
Nyuma y’aho umwirozo wo muri Oregon aririwe n’ingurube ze mu 2012, umworozi wo muri Manitoba yabwiye ikinyamakuru cya CBC News ko ingurube zidasanzwe ko zigira amahane ariko kurya ku maraso bishobora gutuma ari byo "bituma zigira amahane."
Ati: "Ziba zishaka gukina.
Zikunda kuryama, zigira amatsiko cyane ... ntabwo zibereyeho kukubabaza.
Uba ugomba kuzubaha uko bikwiye," ni ko yavuze.
Imiyaga yasizwe na serwakira ya rutura yihuta yitwa Rosa yazanye imvura nyinshi yakwiye henshi mu majyepfo y’uburengerazuba bw’Amerika
Ku byerekeye iteganyagihe, serwakira ya rutura yihuta yitwa Rosa iri kugenda icika intege uko igenda inyura ku mazi akonje yo ku nkombe y’amayaruguru ya Mexico.
Icyakora, serwakira ya rutura yihuta yitwa Rosa izazana imvura itera imyuzure mu majyaruguru ya Mexico no mu majyepfo y’uburengerazuba bwa Amerika mu minsi iri imbere.
Serwakira ya rutura yihuta yitwa Rosa yari ifite umuyaga uri ku muvuduko wa kirometero 136 ku isaha, ukaba ari serwakirwa ya rutura yihuta iri mu cyiciro cya 1 kugeza saa 5:00 z’igitondo. Ku isaha y’uburasirazuba ku Cyumweru, kandi yabonywe iri ku bitometero 620 mu majyepfo y’uburengerazuba bwa Punta Eugenia, muri Mexico.
Rosa yitezweho kujya mu mayaruguru ku Cyumweru.
Hagati aho, umuvumba utangiye kuba mwinshi mu nyinja ya Pasifika kandi uri kugana mu burengerazuba bwa West Coast muri Amerika. Mu gihe Rosa yegera umwigimbakirwa wa Baja California ku wa Mbere nk’umuyaga wo muri toropike uzatangira kugeza ubuhehere bwo muri toropike mu majyaruguru no mu majyepfo y’uburengerazuba bw’Amerika.
Rosa izazana imvura ishobora kugwa ikaba ireshya na cm 25 mu bice bya Mexico ku wa Mbere.
Noneho, ubuhehere bwo muri toropike buzahura n’umuvumba uri gusatira bikore imvura y’umuvumbi ikwire henshi mu majyepfo y’uburengerazuba mu minsi iri imbere.
Muri ako gace, imvura ishobora kugwa ikaba ireshya na cm kuva kuri cm 2,5 kugeza kuri cm 10 ibe yateza umwuzure ukaze, ibisigazwa by’ibyangiritse bitembe kandi ibe yanateza inkangu mu butayu.
Ubuhehere bwo muri toropike bukomeye buzatera imvura ishobora kugwa ikava kuri cm 5 ikagera kuri cm 7 ku isaha ako kanya; by’umwihariko mu bice by’amajyepfo ya Nevada na Arizona.
Mu gihe imvura yagwa ikaba na cm kuva kuri 5 ukagera ku 10 yitezwe mu bice by’amajyepfo, ahanini muri Arizona.
Imyuzure yihuta irashoboka aho ishobora kugenda igabanuka bitewe ni uko imvura yo muri toropike igwa itatanye.
Bishobora kuba atari igitekerezo cyiza cyo kujya mu butayu n’amaguru ahashobora kugwa imvura yo muri toropike.
Imvura nyinshi ishobora gutuma imibande ihinduka imigezi ikaze n’imvura irimo inkuba ishobora guzana umuyaga ukomeye maze ugatumura ivumbi.
Umuvumba ugiye kuza uzaza imvura ikomeye mu duce tw’amajyepfo ya California twegereye inkombe z’inyanja.
Imvura izagwa ishobora kugera ku cm 1, bikaba byatuma ibyangiritse bike bitemba maze bigatuma imihanda inyerera.
Ibi byaba imvura iguye bwa mbere muri ako karere mu gihe cy’imvura.
Zimwe mu mvura zo muri toropike zigwa ahantu hatandukanye zizatangira kwegera Arizona mu masaha akuze yo ku Cyumweru no mu masaha ya kare ku wa Mbere, mbere y’uko imvura ikwira kenshi mu masaha akuze yo ku wa Mbere no mu masaha ya kare ku wa Kabiri.
Imvura ikaze izagera mu bice bya Four Corners ku wa Kabiri no ku wa Gatatu.
Ukwakira gushobora kuba hari ihindagurika rikomeye ry’ubushyuhe muri Amerika kuko Arigitika iri gukonja kurushaho, ariko toropike igakomeza gushyuha.
Rimwe na rimwe bituma habaho impinduka zikomeye mu bushyushye harimo intera nto.
Hari urugero rukomeye rw’itandukaniro rinini ry’ubushyuhe hagati muri Amerika ku Cyumweru.
Hari hafi itandukaniro rya dogere 20 z’ubushyuhe hagati y’Umujyi wa Kansas, Missouri na Omaha, Nebraska no hagati ya St. Louis na Des Moines, Iowa.
Mu minsi mike ikurikira, ubushyuhe bwo mu mpeshyi buzagerageza kuza no kongera kugera henshi.
Ahenshi mu bice byo hagati n’uburasirazuba bw’Amerika hitezwe ko hagera ubushyuhe guhera mu Ukwakira bukagera ahandi bukagera nko kuri dogere Celcius 26 uhereye mu kibaya cy’amajyepfo ukagera mu bice by’amajyaruguru y’uburasirazuba.
Umujyi wa New York City ushobora kugera kuri dogere Celcius 26 ku wa Kabiri, bikaba ari hafi dogere 10 ziyongeye ku mpuzandengo.
Iteganyagihe ryacu ry’igihe kirekire riri kugaragaza ko hari amahirwe menshi y’uko ubushyuhe buri hejuru y’impuzandengo bushobora kugera mu bice by’uburasirazuba bw’Amerika kugeza mu gice cya mbere cy’ukwezi k’Ukwakira.
Abantu b arenga miriyoni 20 barebye iburanisha rya Brett Kavanaugh
Abantu barenga miriyoni 20 barebye ubuhamya bushishikaje bw’uwatanzwe nk’uzaba perezida w’Urukiko rw’ikirenga ari we Brett Kavanaugh n’umugore umushinja kumusagarira bishingiye ku gitsina uvuga ko byakozwe muri za 80, Christine Blasey Ford, bunyura ku mashene ya televiziyo atandatu.
Hagati aho, ukutumvikana mu ruhando rwa politiki byarakomeje, aho abatangaza amakuru kuri televiziyo barogoye ikiganiro gisanzwe cyo ku wa Gatanu ku munota wa nyuma: Ni amasezerano yakozwe na Senateri wa Arizona ari we Jeff Flake kugira ngo FBI ikore iperereza ry’ibyaha ashinjwa mu cyumweru kimwe.
Ford yabwiye Komiti ya Sena ishinzwe ubutabere ko yizeye neza 100 ku ijana ko Kavanaugh yamukabakabye yanyoye inzoga maze akagerageza kumukuramo imyenda mu birori byo ku ishuri ryisumbuye.
Kavanaugh, utanga ubuhamya agaragaza amarangamutimal, yavuze ko azi neza 100 ku ijana ko ibyo bitigeze biba.
Birashoboka cyane ko abantu barenga miriyoni 20,4 batangajwe n’isosiyete ya Nielsen ku wa Gatanu ko baburebye.
Isosiyete yariri kubara impuzandengo y’abareba televiziyo za CBS, ABC, NBC, CNN, Fox News Channel na MSNBC.
Imibare ntiyahise iboneka yo ku zindi televiziyo zerekanye ubuhamya harimo PBS, C-SPAN na Fox Business Network.
Kandi ubusanzwe Nielsen igira ibibazo byo kubara abantu barebera ibiganiro mu biro.
Kugira ngo byumvikane neza, ni abantu baba bangana n’abari mu mukino wo kwishyura cyangwa batanga ibihembo bya Academy Awards.
Nielsen iti: “Fox News Channel, ifite abakira abatumirwa yishyigikiye ku buryo bukomeye igenwa rya Kavanaugh, ikaba iyoboye izindi televiziyo ku mpuzandengo ya abayireba bangana na miriyoni 5,69 mu iburanisha ryabaye umunsi wose.”
ABC ni yo yaje ku mwanya wa mbere n’abarebye iburanisha bangana na miriyoni 3,26.
Nielsen iti: “CBS yo yarebwe na miriyoni 3,1, NBC irebwa na miriyoni 2,4, MSNBC yarebwe na miriyoni 2,89 naho CNN irebwa na miriyoni 2,52.”
Ibishishikaje biracyari byinshi nyuma y’iburanisha.
Flake ni we wari uhanzwe amaso mu byabaye byo ku wa Gatanu.
Nyuma y’aho ibiro by’abarepubulikani bigize icyo bitangaza cy’uko bizatora bishyigikira Kavanaugh, yafashwe amashusho na kamera za CNN na CBS mu gitondo cyo ku wa Gatanu akankamirwa n’abigaragambya mu gihe yageragezaga kwinjira muri asanseri ajya mu iburanisha rya Komite ishinzwe ubutabera.
Yahagaze amaso ye areba hasi iminota myinshi ubwo yanengwaga, bitambuka ako kanya kuri televiziyo ya CNN.
Umugore umwe ati: "Mpagaze hano imbere yanyu," umugore ni ko yavuze.
"Muratekereza ko ari kubwira ukuri abaturage b’igihugu cyose?
Yabwiwe ko, "ugira imbaraga nyinshi iyo abagore benshi cyane nta mbaraga bafite.""
Flake yavuze ko ibiro bye byagize icyo bitangaza maze avuga ko mbere y’uko asanseri ifunga, yakabaye yaravuze byinshi mu iburanisha rya komite.
Amashene ya televiziyo na televiziyo bari biri kunyuzaho ako kanya nyuma y’amasaha make, ubwo Komite ishinzwe iburanisha yatoye kugira ngo igeze igenwa rya Kavanaugh ku rundi rwego kugira ngo bigere kuri Sena habe amatora.
Ariko Flake yavuze ko yabikora gusa mu gihe azi ko FBI yashaka kugenzura ibyo birego biregwa uwagenwe mu cyumweru gitaha, bikaba ari byo abatemokarate bake basabaga ko bikorwa.
Flake yumvishijwe ko ari umwe mu bagizei kiganiro n’inshuti ye, umutemokarate Senateri Chris Coons.
Nyuma y’ikiganiro na Coons n’abandi basenateri nyuma yaho, Flake yafashe icyemezo.
Uguhitamo kwa Flake kwari gufite imbaraga, kubera ko byagaragaraga ko abarepubulike batagomba gutora kugira ngo bemeze Kavanaugh hadakozwe iperereza.
Perezida Trump yatangije iperereza rya FBI ku byaha bishinjwa Kavanaugh.
Minisitiri w’Ubwongereza, May, ashinja abamunenga ibyo 'gukina politiki' ku byerekeye Brexit
Minisitiri W’Intebe, Theresa May, yashinje abanenga gahunda ze zo kuva mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi "gukina politiki" y’ahazaza h’Ubwongereza no gutesha agaciro inyungu z’igihugu mu kiganiro yagiranye n’ikinyamakuru cya Sunday Times.
Minisitir w’Intebe w’Ubwongereza, Theresa May, yageze mu Nama y’ishyaka ry’abakonserivateri i Birmingham, mu Bwongereza, tariki ya 29 Nzeli 2018.
Mu kindi kiganiro gikurikira icyo yagiranye n’ikinyamakuru kuri paji ibanza, uwahoze ari minisitiri w’ububanyi n’amahanga we, Boris Johnson, yibasiye mu binyamakuru gahunda ye y’umubano w’Ubwongereza n’Umuryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi igamije icyitwa Brexit, avuga ko igitekerezo cy’uko Ubwongereza n’Umuryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi byombi bigomba kwishyurana imisoro ari "ibintu bidasanzwe na gato."
Iraswa rya Wayde Sims: Polisi yataye muri yombi ukekwa, Dyteon Simpson, mu rupfu rw’umukinnyi wa LSU
Polisi yataye muri yombi ukekwaho kurasa bikaviramo urupfu Wayde Sims, umukinnyi wa basiketi w’imyaka 20 wakiniraga ikipe ya LSU.
Ishami rya Polisi rya Baton Rouge ryavuze ko Dyteon Simpson, w’imyaka 20, yatawe muri yombi maze ashyirwa muri gereza akurikiranyweho icyaha cy’ubwicanyi bwo mu rwego rwa kabiri.
Abapolisi bashyize ahagaragara videwo y’ubushyamirane hagati ya Sims na Simpson maze Polisi ivuga ko Sims yataye amataratara ye muri iyo mirwano.
Ishami rya televiziyo ya CBS ari ryo WAFB rivuga ko Polisi yatoye ayo mataratara ahabereye icyaha maze ivuga ko yayasanzeho ADN ya Simpson.
Nyuma yo guhata ibibazo Simpson, Polisi yavuze ko yemeye kuba yararashe agahitana Wayde.
Umwavoka we avuga ko ingwate yatanga kugira ngo arekurwe by’agateganyo ari amadorari 350 000.
Ibiro bishinzwe gusuzuma icyishe umuntu bya East Baton Rouge Parish Coroner byasohoye raporo y’ibanze ku wa Gatanu, bivuga ko yishwe n’ibikomere by’amasasu yarashwe mu mutwe no ku ijosi.
Ishami rya Polisi rirashimira Sitasiyo ya Polisi ya Louisiana ishinzwe gukurikirana abakoze ibyaha bagahunga, laburatwari ishinzwe kurwanya ibyaha ya sitasiyo ya Polisi, Polisi ikorera muri kaminuza ya Southern University n’abaturage bo muri ako gace kurifasha mu iperereza ryatumye ukekwaho icyaha afatwa.
Umuyobozi ushinzwe abakinnyi mu ikipe ya LSU, Joe Alleva, yashimiye abapolisi bo muri ako gace ku bw’"ubushishozi bwabo no gukurikirana kugira ngo hatangwe ubutabera nyabwo."
Sims yari afite imyaka 20.
Umukinnyi wareshyaga na metero 2 yakuriye muri Baton Rouge, aho se umubyara, Wayne, na we yakinnye basiketi mu ikipe ya LSU.
Afite impuzandengo yo kwinjiza amanota 5,6 no kugarira imipira 2,6 itinjiye mu gatebo kuri buri mukino muri shampiyona ishize.
Ku wa Gatanu mu gitondo, umutoza w’ikipe ya basiketi ya LSU, Will Wade, yavuze ko ikipe "yashenguwe" kandi "kandi ibabajwe cyane" n’urupfu rwa Waydeh.
Wade ati: "Iki ni cyo kiduhangayikisha igihe cyose".
Ikirunga cyasutse ku Mujyi wa Mexico
Ivu ryasutswe n’ikirunga cya Popocatepetl ryageze kuri karitsiye y’amajyepfo y’umujyi wa Mexico.
Ku wa Gatandatu, Ikigo cy’igihugu gishinzwe kurwanya ibiza ryaburiye abanyamegizike kibabuza kwirinda kwegera ikiraunga nyuma y’aho cyongeye kwaka ku gasongero kacyo maze hagaragazwa ko cyasohoye imyuka 183 n’ivu mu masaha arenga 24.
Icyo kigo cyari kiri gukurikirana uguhinda n’imitingo myinshi.
Amashusho yo ku mbuga mpuzambaga yerekanye ivu ryagiye ritwikira ibirahure by’imbere by’imodoka muri karitsiye y’umujyi wa Mexico nka Xochimilco.
Inzobere mu by’ubumenyi bw’isi babonye ko hari ubwiyongere bwo kwaka k’ikirunga kiri mu birometero 72 mu majypefo y’uburasirazuba bw’umujyi mu gihe umutingo uri ku gipimo cya 7,1 wibasiye agace ko hagati ka Mexico muri Nzeli 2017.
Ikirunga kizwi nka "Don Goyo" cyatse kuva mu 1994.
Polisi yiraye mu baharanira ko intara ya Catalan ibona ubwigenge mbere y’isabukuru y’amatora y’ubwigenge
Ku wa Gatandatu, abantu batandatu bafunzwe i Barcelona nyuma y’aho abigaragambya bashyigikiye ubwigenge basakiranye na Polisi ishinzwe guhosha imyigaragambyo, naho abantu ibihumbi basanze abandi bari mu myigaragambyo yo kwizihisa isabukuru y’amatora yo kwigenga kw’intara ya Catalonia.
Itsinda ry’abantu bambaye masike bashyigikiye ukwigenga kw’intara basubijwe inyuma na Polisi ishinzwe guhosha imyigaragambyo aho babateye amagi n’amarangi, bituma hacura igicu cyijimye cy’ivumbi mu mihanda, ubusanzwe iba yuzuyemo ba mukerarugendo.
Imirwano yaje kuvuka mu masaha yigiye imbere y’uwo munsi aho Polisi yariri gukoresha indembo kugira ngo ihoshe iyo mirwano.
Amatsinda ashyigikiye ubwigenge yamaze amasaha menshi aririmba "Ntituzibagirwa, ntituzababarira" bahangana n’abigaragambya baharanira ko ubwo bwigenge butahaho bo baririmbagango "Esipanye irakabaho iteka."
Ikinyamakuru cyo muri ako gace cyavuze ko abantu cumi na bane bavuwe ibikomere bidakanganye bakuye mu myigaragambyo.
Ukutumvikana gukomeje kuba kwinshi hagati y’igice gishaka ubwigenge nyuma y’umwaka umwe nyuma ya kamparampaka yo ku itariki ya 1 Ukwakira yafashwe nk;idakurikije amategeko na Madrid ariko bikishimirwa n’abanyakatara bifuza kubona ubwigenge.
Abatoye bahisemo kwigenga, nubwo abitabiriye amatora bari mbarwa aho abarwanya uko kwigenga baje ari benshi kugira ngo baburizemo amantora.
Hakurikijwe ibitangazwa n’ubuyobozi bwa Catalan, hafi abantu 1 000 bakomerekejwe umwaka ushize nyuma y’aho Polisi yabujije ko amatora akomeza ku biro b’itora bitandukanye mu karere mu mirwano ikaze.
Ku wa Gatanu, amatsinda ashyigikiye ubwigenge yari yakambitse ijoro kugira ngo yirinde ko habaho imyigaragambyo yo gushyigikira Polisi y’igihugu.
Imyigaragambyo yarabaye ariko ihatirwa gukorerwa ahandi.
Narcis Termes, w’imyaka 68, ukora iby’amashanyarazi yagiye mu myigaragambyo y’abashaka kwigenga ari kumwe n’umugore we, akaba yaravuze ko nta cyizere kigihari ku byerekeye kuba intara ya Catalonia yabona ubwigenge.
Ati: "Umwaka ushize twabaye mu bihe byiza.
Nabonye ababyeyi banjye barira amarira y’ibyishimo kubera ko babashije gutora ariko ubu twabuze icyo dukora."
Nubwo habonetse intsinzi nubwo yari nto mu mataro y’akarere Ukuboza umwaka ushize, amashyaka ashyigikiye ubwigenge bw’intara ya Catalonia yagowe no gukomera kuri iyo ntsinzi uyu mwaka, aho abayobozi benshi bazwi bijyanye mu buhungiro cyangwa bafunzwe bategereje kuburana ku ruhare rwabo mu gutegura kamparamaka no gutangaza ubwigenge.
Joan Puig, umukanishi w’imyaka 42-yafashwe amashusho y’imyigaragambyo ashyigikiye Polisi akoresheje telefone ye, yavuze ko amakimbirane yatejwe n’abanyapolitiki b’impande zombi.
Ati: "biri kurushaho gukomera."
Ku wa Gatandatu, Oriol Junqueras, imwe mu bayobozi icyenda b’intara ya Catalan ufunzwe by’agateganyo kuva umwaka ushize, yatangaje ko aziyamamaza mu matora y’Intego Ishinga Amategeko y’Uburayi umwaka utaha.
Ati: "Kuba umukandida mu matora y’Uburayi ni bwo buryo bwiza bwo kwamagana ugusubira inyuma kw’indangagaciro za demokarasi no gukandamizwa twabonye ku buyobizi bwa Esipanye."
Londonderry: Abagabo bafashwe nyuma y’aho inzu igongewe n’imodoka
Abagabo batatu, bafite imyaka 33, 34 na 39, barafashwe nyuma y’aho imodoka byavuzwe ko yagonze inzu muri Londonderry.
Iyo mpanduka yabereye muri Ballynagard Crescent ku wa Kane hafi saa 19:30 z’isaha yo mu Bwongereza.
Insipegiteri wungirije witwa Bob Blemmings yavuze ko hangiritse amarembo n’inyubako ubwayo.
Hashobora no kuba hararashwe umwambi ku modoka.
Igitego cyatsinzwe na Menga cyatumye Livingston itsinda 1-0 bwa Rangers
Igitego cya mbere cya Dolly Menga akinira Livingston cyayihesheje intsinzi
Ikipe yazamutse mu cyiciro cya mbere yitwa Livingston yatunguye Rangers akaba ari bwo bwa kabiri Steven Gerrard atsinzwe mu mikino 18 nk’umutoza w’ikipe ya Ibrox.
Igitego cya Dolly Menga cyagaragaje itandukaniro ubwo uruhande rwa Gary Holt rwagiye ku mwanya wa kabiri ruyisanzeho Hibernian.
Uruhande rwa Gerrard rwakomeje kutabonera itsinzi ku kibuga cy’ikipe yasuye muri Shampiyona uyu mwaka w’imikino kandi izahura n’ikipe iyoboye urutonde rwa shampiyona ari yo Hearts, bakaba bayikurikiye ibarusha amanota umunani, bazahura ku Cyumweru.
Mbere y ‘aho, Rangers izakira Rapid Vienna mu mikino y’irushanwa rya Europa League ku wa Kane.
Hagati aho, Livingston, yakomeje kongera imikino idatsindwa muri shampiyona igera ku mikino itandatu, aho umutoza wayo mukuru Holt ategereje gutsindwa kuva yasimbura Kenny Miler mu kwezi gushize.
Livingston yabuze amahirwe yo gutsinda ikipe idakomeye yari yabasuye
Ikipe ya Holt yakagombye kuba iri imbere cyane mbere yo gutsinda, mu gihe ubusaritiza bwayo buri guteza ibibazo byose bibaho ikipe ya Rangers.
Scott Robinson yabashije kurenga abarinda izamu ariko umupira yateye unyura iruhande rw’izamu noneho Alan Lithgow we abasha gutera umupira aro ujjya hanze nyuma yo guserebeka kugira ngo ahure n’umupira wari utewe n’umutwe wa Craig Halkett.
Abari bakiriye umukino bishimiye kureka ngo Rangers ikinire imbere yabo, bazi neza ko bashobora gutera ibibazo ababasuye ku mipira y’imiterekano.
Ni muri ubwo buryo igitego cya ngombwa cyabonetse.
Rangers yatsinzwe umupira wa kufura maze Livingston iba ifunguye amazamu, Declan Gallagher na Robinson bahuje uburyo bwo gushaka uko Menga atsinda igitego, akaba ari we wakoze ku mubiri ari hagati mu rubuga rw’amahina.
Kuri urwo rwego, Rangers yari yihariye umupira cyane ariko iza gusanga urukuta rw’inyuma ry’ikipe basuye rudapfa kumenwa ndetse n’umuzamu, Liam Kelly, akaba ataragiye akuramo imipira ikomeye,
Umukino wakomeje utyo no mu gice cya kabiri, nubwo Alfredo Morelos yateye umupira ukagarurwa na Kelly.
Umupira watewe na Scott Pittman wakuwemo n’ibirenge by’umuzamu wa Rangers witwa Allan McGregor naho Lithgow we atera hejuru nyuma y’undi mupira w’umuterekano watewe na Livingston.
Amashoti agana imbere y’izamu yakomeje kuza mu rubuga rw’amahina rw’ikipe ya Livingston ariko anakomeza kugarirwa ku buryo atageze ku izamu, mu gihe bavuze ko hari penaliti zagombaga gutangwa zigera kuri ebyiri, nyuma y’aho Halkett akoreye ikosa kuri Glenn Middleton waje asimbuye ndetse n’umupira wakoreshejweho intoki, zombi ntizatanzwe.
Isesengura rivuga ko ikipe ya Livingston yakinnye mu 'buryo budasanzwe'
Umunyamakuru wa BBC Scotland ari we Alasdair Lamont uri ku kibuga cya Tony Macaroni Arena
Imikinire idasanzwe n’umukino urangiye neza kuri Livingston.
Nta gushidikanya ko bakinnye neza cyane, bakomeza kugenda bakina mu buryo bwiza cyane uko umukino wagenda ukura.
Imikinire yabo n’ubuhanga bwa buri mukinnyi bahindutse gake kuva bagarutse mu ruhando rw’amakipe akomeye, ariko amanota menshi yahabwe Holt ku buryo yashyize ikipe ku murongo kuva yahagera.
Afite abakinnyi benshi beza.
Kapiteni Halkett yakinnye neza, ashyira ku murongo abakinnyi bugarura, mu gihe Menga yafashe Connor Goldson na Joe Worrall mu mukino wose.
Naho Rangers nta byinshi yakoze mu kibuga.
Igihe cyose bakina neza kuva batangira gutozwa na Gerrard, ariko ubu ntacyo bakoze gihambaye.
Umupira wa nyuma ntiwageraga mu izamu, gusa inshuro imwe basatiriye izamu ry’ikpe yabakiriye, ariko ibyo byatumye ikipe ya Rangers, ubu bakaba bari hagati ku rutonde rwa shampiyona.
Erdogan yakiriwe mu buryo butavuzweho rumwe muri Kolonye
Ku wa Gatandatu, hari abari bari guseka n’abatari bishimye (tariki ya 29 Nzeli) mu gihe abayobozi ba Turikiya n’Ubudage bahuriye ku ifunguro rya mugitondo i Berlin.
Ni wo munsi wa nyuma Perezida Erdogan yagiriye uruzinduka rutavuzweho rumwe mu Budage, rukaba rwari rugamije kuzahura umubano hagati y’ibihugu biri mu Muryango wo gutabarana mu bya gisirikare wa OTAN.
Ntibumvikanye ku bibazo birimo uburenganzira bwa muntu, ubwisanzure bw’itangazamakuru no kuba Turikiya yekwemererwa kujya mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi.
Ubwo, Erdogan yagiye muri Kolonye kugira ngo ahafungure umusigiti munini mushya.
Uwo mujyi ni wo ubamo abanyaturikiya benshi baba hanze ya Turikiya.
Polisi yavuze impamvu z’umutekano akaba ari byo byatumye abagera ku bihumbi 25 000 babuzwa guteranira imbere y’uwo musigiti, ariko abenshi mu bamushyigikiye baje aho hafi kugira ngo barebe perezida wabo.
Abantu bagera mu majana bigaragambije bamagana Erdogan; abenshi muri bo bakaba ari abakurude bakaba baratumye ijwi ryabo ryumvikana, bamagana politiki za Erdogan n’icyemezo cya leta y’Ubudage cyo kumuha ikaze mu gihugu.
Imyigaragambyo yajemo n’imirwano igaragaza ukutumvikana bw’umushyitsi ufatwa nk’intwara na bamwe mu banyaturikiya b’abadage naho abandi bakamufata nk’umunyagitugu.
Impanuka yo mu muhanda wa Deptford: Umunyegare yapfiriye mu mpanuka yagonganyemo n’imodoka
Umunyegare yapfiriye mu mpanuka y’imodoka i Londere.
Impanuka yabereye hafi y’isangano ry’imihanda ya Bestwood Street na Evelyn, umuhanda uba urimo imodoka nyinshi muri Deptford, mu majyepfo y’uburasirazuba bw’umujyi hafi saa 10:15 zo ku isaha yo mu Bwongereza.
Umushoferi wari utwaye imodoka yahagaze maze abatabara abakomeretse baramufasha, ariko uwo munyegare yapfiriye ahabereye impanuka.
Impanuka ibya nyuma y’amezi hari undi munyegare wagonzwe n’imodoka itaramanyekanye ku muhanda wa Childers, mu kirometero kimwe n’igice uvuye aho impanuka yo ku wa Gatandatu yabereye.
Polisi yo mu muhanda yavuze ko abapolisi bari gukora kugira ngo bamenye uwo mugabo maze bamenyeshe abavandimwe be.
Umuhanda wapfunzwe kandi hashyizweho ahandi bisi zinyura n’abagendera kuri moto bagiriwe inama yo kwirinda aho hantu.
Gereza ya Long Lartin: Aba ofisiye batandatu bakomerekeye mu mirwano
Umuyobozi wa gereza yatangaje ko abacungagereza batandatu bakomerekeye mu mirwano yo muri gereza ifungirwamo abagabo irinzwe cyane.
Iyo mirwano yatangiriye kuri HMP Long Lartin muri Worcestershire hafi ya 09:30 ku isaha yo mu Bwongereza ku Cyumweru kandi irakomeje.
Inzobere z’aba ofisiye zitwa ba "Tornado" barazanyawe kugira ngo bahangane n’iyo mirwano, bikaba irimo imfungwa umunani kandi zikaba zagumishijwe mu gice kimwe.
Aba ofisiye bavuriwe ahari kubera imirwano ibikomere byo mu maso bidakanganye.
Umuvugizi wa gereza yagize ati: "Abacungagereza bahawe amafunzo yihariye barazanywe kugira ngo bahangane n’imirwano iri kubera muri HMP Long Lartin.
Abantu batandatu bagize abacungagereza bavuwe ibikomere.
Ntabwo twihanganira imirwano muri gereza zacu kandi twabisobanuye neza ko ababigizemo uruhare bazagezwa kuri Polisi kandi igihe cyo gufungwa bari bafite gishobora kwiyongera."
Gereza ya HMP Long Lartin ifungiwemo imfungwa zirenga 500, harimo bamwe bakoze ibyaha bazwi cyane ku rwego rw’igihugu.
Muri Kamena, byavuzwe ko umuyobozi wa gerereza yavuriwe mu bitaro kubera ko yasagariwe n’imfungwa.
Naho mu Ukwakira umwaka ushize, aba ofisiye bashinzwe guhosha imyigaragambyo barahamagawe kugira ngo bahangane n’imirwano ikomeye muri gereza aho abakozi bibasiwe hakoreshejwe imipira ya biyari.
Serwakira ya rutura yihuta yitwa Rose ihangayikishije Phoenix, Las Vegas, Salt Lake City kubera imyuzure yihuta (Uduce twibasiwe n’amapfa dushobora kubyungukiramo)
Ntibisanzwe ko serwakira zo muri toropike zibasira Arizona, ariko ni byo neza bishobora kuba mu ntangiriro z’icyumweru gitaha aho imbaraga zari zisigaye za serwakira ya rutura yitwa Rosa zirigeze mu butayu bw’amajyepfo y’uburengerazuba, bigatuma haza imyuzure yihuta.
Ikigo cy’igihugu cy’iteganyagihe cyamaze kuburira abantu ko bitondera imyuzure yihuta ku wa Mbere no ku wa Kabiri uhereye mu burengerazuba bwa Arizona ukageza mu majyepfo no mu burasirazuba bwa Nevada, amajypefo y’uburasirazuba bwa California na Utah, harimo imijyi ya Phoenix, Flagstaff, Las Vegas na Salt Lake City.
Rosa yitezweho gufata inzira itaziguye ijya muri Phoenix ku wa Kabiri, ihegera mu masaha akazu yo ku wa Mbere iteza imvura.
Ikigo cy’igihugu gishinzwe iby’iteganyagihe muri Phoenix cyavuze ko hari za serwakira "icumi zituruka muri toropike zatumye haza umuyaga ukomeye cyangwa serwakira zo muri toropike mu birometero 320 muri Phoenix kuva mu 1950!
Serwakira yiswe Katrina (1967) ni yo serwakira yaje ivuye mu birometero 64 uvuye ku mupaka wa AZ."
Ikigo cy’igihugu gishinzwe gukurikirana imiyaga ya serwakira cyakoze moderi igaragaza ko hashobora kugwa imvura yatuma amazi agera kuri cm ivuye kuri 5 ukagera ku 10, hari aho ishobora kugera kuri cm 15 mu gice cya Mogollon Rim muri Arizona.
Ibindi bice by’ubutayu bw’amayepfo y’uburengerazuba harimo igice cyo hagati cya Rockies na Great Basin bikaba bishobora kubona imvura ifite amazi yagera muri cm uvuye kuri 2 ukagera kuri 5, hari aho ishobora kugera kuri cm 10.
Ku badafite ibyago byi kwibasirwa n’imyuzure yihuta, imvura iterwa na Rosa ishobora kuba ari umugisha nyuma y’aho akarere kibasiwe n’amapfa.
Nubwo imyuzuye iteye impungenge zikomeye, zimwe muri izi mvura zishobora kuzana inyungu mu gice cy’amajyepfo y’uburengerazuba kuri kiri mu mapfa.
Weather.com itangaza ko hakurikijwe ibivugwa n’Ikigo cy’igihugu gishinzwe gukurikirana amapfa, aharenga 40 ku ijana muri Arizona byibuze hari amapfa akomeye, bikaba ari cyo cyiciro cyo hejuru."
Icya mbere, inzira inyurwamo na serwakira ya Rosa ituma ugera ku butaka ku mwigimbakirwa wa Baja California muri Mexico.
Rosa, iracyafite ingufu za serwakira ku Cyumweru aho ifite umuyaga ufite umuvuduko wo hejuru wa kirometero 136 ku isaha, ikaba iri ku muvuduko wa kirometero 620 mu majyepfo ya Punta Eugenia, Mexico igenda mu majyaruguru ku muvuduko wa kirometero 20 ku isaha.
Umuyaga uri guhura n’amazi akonje yo mu nyanja ya Pasifika maze bigatuma ugabanura umuvuduko.
Bityo, byitezwe ko ugera ku butaka muri Mexico ufite imbaraga z’umuyaga wo muri toropike nyuma ya saa sita cyangwa nimugoroba ku wa Mbere.
Imvura mu bice bya Mexico ishobora kuba ikomeye, ibikaba yateza imyuzure yazana ibibazo bikomeye.
Weather.com igira iti: "Imvura yose yagwa ishobora guteza amazi yagera kuri cm uvuye kuri 7 ukagera kuri 15 uhereye muri Baja California ukagera mu majyaruguru y’uburasirazuba bwa Sonora, aho no kugira imvura igera kuri cm 25 bishoboka."
Noneho, Rosa izakomeza ijye mujyaruguru inyuze muri Mexico nk’umuyaga wo muri toropike mbere yo kugera ku mupaka wa Arizona mu masaha ya mugitondo ku wa Kabiri mu gihe serwakira yo muri toropike, yo izakomeza inzira ikanyura muri Arizona igana mu majyepfo ya Utah mu masaha akuze yo ku wa Kabiri nijoro.
Ikigo cy’igihugu gishinzwe gukurikirana za serwakira kiti: "Ibibazo by’ibanze byitezwe kuri serwakira ya Rosa cyangwa imiyaga izanwa na yo ni imvura ikomeye iri bugwe muri Baja California, amajyaruguru y’uburengerazuba bwa Sonora no mu butayu bw’amajyepfo y’uburengerazuba."
Iyo mvura yitezweho kuzana imyuzure yihuta yahitana ubuzima bw’abantu ikanakumumba ibisigazwa ibijyana mu butayu, ikanateza inkangu mu bice by’imisozi.
Igitero cyo muri Midsomer Norton: Abantu bane bakwekwaho kugerageza kwica barafashwe
Ingimbi eshatu n’umugabo w’imyaka 20 barafashwe bakekwaho kugerageza kwica nyuma y’aho umuntu w’imyaka 16 bamusanze afite ibikomere by’uwatewe ibyuma muri Somerset.
Iyo ngimbi bayisanze yakomeretse mu gace ka Excelsior Terrace muri Midsomer Norton, hafi sa 04:00 z’isaha yo mu Bwongereza ku wa Gatandatu.
Yajyanwe ku bitaro aho akomereje kuvurirwa ariko akaba "atarembye".
Polisi ivuga ko ingimbi imwe ifite imyaka 17, izindi ebyiri zifite imyaka 18 n’umugabo w’imyaka 20 barafashwe mu ijoro muri Radstock area, Avon na Somerset.

Trump avuga ko Kavanaugh 'yahuye n’umujinya n’ubugome’ by’ishyaka ry’abademokarate
Trump ubwo yiyamamazaga muri Wheeling, Virginia y’uburengerazuba yagize ati: "Gutora Umucamanza Kavanaugh ni ugutora wamagana tagitike z’ubugome kandi zifite ibyo zangiza z’ishyaka ry’abademokarate."
Trump yavuze ko Kavanaugh "yahuje n’umujinya n’ubugome" bw’ishyaka ry’abademokarate mu gikorwa cye cyo kugenwa cyose.
Ku wa Kane, Kavanaugh yatangiye ubuhamya imbere ya Kongere ahakana ku buryo bukomeye kandi burimo amarangamutima ku byo aregwa na Christine Blasey Ford ko yamusagariye bishingiye ku gitsina mu myaka mirongo ishize ubwo bari ingambi n’abangavu.
Ford na we atanga ubuhamya mu iburanisha ku byo arega.
Ku wa Gatandatu, Perezida yagize ati: "Abanyamerika babonye ubuhanga, ubwiza n’ishyaka" bya Kavanaugh kuri uwo munsi.
Abwira ikivunge cy’abantu bamushyigikiye muri Virginia y’uburengerazuba ati: "Gutora mu rwego rwo kwemeza Umucamanza Kavanaugh ni ugutora kugira ngo twemeze ibyinshi byagezweho n’umuhanga ukomeye mu by’amategeko twagize mu gihe cyacu, umucamanza wakoreye ibikorwa ntagereranywa rubanda."
Perezida yavuze ku buryo butaziguye igenwa rya Kavanaugh mu gihe yarari kuvuga ku kamaro ko kuba abarepuburikani babazaza ari benshi mu matora yo mu gihembwe hagati.
Ati: "Harabura ibyumweru bitanu ngo amwe mu matora y’ingenzi mu gihe cyacu abe.
Sindi kwiyamamaza, ariko ndi kwiyamamaza."
"Ni yo mpamvu ndi ahantu hose ndwanira abakindida bakomeye."
Trump yavuze ko abademokarate bafite gahunda yo "kwinangira no kubuza ibikorwa."
Umwe mu bayobozi b’ishyaka ry’abarepubulike yabwiye ikinyamakuru cya CNN ko igikorwa cya mbere cy’ingenzi mu matora ari uko hitezwe ko Sena yemeza igenwa rya Kavanaugh bikaba bizakorwa bitarenze ku wa Gatanu.
Abantu amajana bipfiriye mu mutungito, tsunami byabereye muri Indoneziya, aho imibare y’abapfuye ikomeje kwiyongera
Ku wa Gatandatu, abayobozi bavuze ko byibuze abantu 384 barishwe, abenshi bajywa n’umuvumba wakubise ku nkombe, ubwo umutingito ukomeye na tsunami byakubise ikirwa cya Indoneziya cya Sulawesi.
Ku wa Gatanu, abantu barenga amajana bateraniye ku iserukiramuco ryabereye ku nkombe z’inyanja mu mujyi wa Palu ubwo umuvumba urehsya na metero esheshatu (fiti 18) wakubise ku nkombe ku mugoroba, ujyana uhitana abantu benshi unangiza ikintu cyose wasanze mu nzira wanyuzemo.
Tsunami yakurikiwe n’umutingito ufite ubukana bwa 7,5.
Sutopo Purwo Nugroho, umuvugizi w’Ikigo gishinzwe kurwanya ibiza muri Indoneziya cyitwa BNPB, mu kiganiro cyabere i Jakarta agira ati: "Ubwo ikibazo cya tsunami kiyongeraga ejo, abantu bari bakiri gukora ibikorwa byabo ku nkengero z’inyanja kandi ntabwo bahise biruka maze irabahitana."
Nugroho ati: "Tsunami ntiyigeze iza ubusa, yaje yakururanye imodoka, inginga z’ibiti, amazi, ikubura ikuntu cyose isanze ku butaka;" akomeza avuga ko tsunami yageze mu nyanja ku muvuduko w’ibirometero 800 ku isaha (mayiro 497 ku isaha) mbere yo kwibasira inkengero z’inyanja.
Avuga ko abantu bamwe na bamwe bagiye burira ibiti kugira ngo bacike tsunami maze abarokoka.
Hafi abantu 16 700 bakuwe ahabereye ikiza bajyanwa mu bigo 24 byo muri Palu.
Amafoto yafashwe n’indege yashyizwe ahagaragara n’ikigo gishinzwe kurwanya ibiza yerekanye ko inyubuko nyinshi n’amaduka byasenyutse, ibiraro birangirika ibindi biragwa n’imisigiti isengurukwa n’amazi.
Ku wa Gatandatu, umutingito muto uza nyuma y’ukomeye wakomeje gushegesha imijyi iri ku nkengero z’inyanja.
Imitingito itandukanye yagiye yumvikana mu bice bituyemo abantu bagera kuri miriyoni 2,4.
Ikigo cya Indoneziya gishinzwe isuzuma n’ikoreshwa ry’ikoranabuhanga (BPPT) cyatangaje ko umutingito wo ku wa Gatanu wari ufite hafi imbaraga zikubye inshuro 200 bombe atomike yatewe muri Hiroshima mu ntambara ya kabiri y’isi.
Icyo giko gikomeza kivuga ko kubera imiterere y’umujyi, uri ku gice gikikije inyanja bishobora kongera ubukana bwa tsunami.
Nugroho yasobanuye ibyangiritse nk’"ibikomeye" kandi avuga ko amazu, amavuriro, amaduka n’amahoteri ibihumbi yasenyutse.
Imirambo y’abahitanwe n’ibiza yagaragaye yaheze mu bisigazwa by’inzu zaguye, avuga ko biyongera ku bantu 540 bakomeretse n’abandi 29 baburiwe irengero.
Nugroho yavuze ko abakomeretse n’ibyangiritse bishobora kuba byinshi ku nkengero z’inyanja zingana na km 300 (mayiro 190) mu majyaruguru ya Palu, mu gace kitwa Donggala, kakaba kegereye aho umutingito waturutse.
Nugroho avuga ko guhabwa no gutanga amakuru "byabangamiwe bikomeye aho nta makuru yabashaga gutambuka" avuye muri Donggala.
Mu byatangajwe n’umuryango utabara imbabare wa Croix Rouge uvuga ko muri ako gace hatuye abantu 300 000," wongeraho ko abakozi bawo n’abakorerabushake bari kugana mu duce twahuye n’ibiza.
Uti: "Byamaze kuba akaga, ariko bishobora kuba bibi kurushaho."
Ku wa Gatandatu, ikigo cyatangaje ko cyanenzwe bikomeye kubera ko nta makuru cyatanze y’uko tsunami yari yibasiye Palu, ariko abayobozi bavuze ko imivumba yaje mu gihe bari batangiye kuburira abaturage.
Mu mafoto yafashwe n’abatarabigize umwuga yasangijwe ku mbuga mpuzambaga, yerekana umugabo ari hejuru mu nyubako aho yumvimana ari gusakuza aburira abantu ababwira ko tsunami iri kugerera abantu bari mu muhanda uri munsi ye.
Mu minota mike amazi menshi yikubise ku nkombe, utwara inyubako n’imodoka.
Ikinyamakuru cya Reuters ntabwo cyabashije guhita cyemeza ayo mashusho.
Umutingito na tsunami byatumye umuriro ubura bikoma mu nkokora kwakira no gutanga amkuru muri Palu, bituma abayobozi bagorwa no guhuza ibikorwa by’ubutabazi.
Abasirikare batangiye kohereza indege z’imizigo zirimo ubufasha buvuye muri Jakarta no mu yindi mijyi, abayobozi bavuze ko n’abantu bakuwe ahabereye ibiza bakeneye ibiribwa ku buryo bukomeye n’ibindi bikenerwa ku buryo bw’ibanze.
Ikibuga cy’indege cy’umujyi cyongewe gufungurwa mu rwego rwo gutanga ubufasha no kuguma gifunzwe kugeza mu Ukwakira.
Ku Cyumweru, byari byitezwe ko Perezida Joko Widodo asura ibigo byakira abakuwe ahabereye ibiza muriPalu.
Umubare w’amabaze guhitanwa na tsunami yo muri Indoneziya wazamutse ugera ku bantu 800.
Ni bibi cyane.
Bwana Doseba yavuze ko mu gihe abakozi b’umuryango wa World Vision baturutse muri Donggala bageze mu mujyi wa Palu, aho abakozi bacumbitse mu macumbi ya Tarpaulin kugira ngo bashyire ibiro byabo mu gikari, banyuze ahantu hageshejwe n’ibiza bagera muri ako gacea.
Ati: "Bambwiye ko babonye amazu menshi yangiritse."
Ni bibi cyane.
Nubwo amatsinda y’ubutabazi yatangiye ibikorwa byo gufasha, bamwe binubira ko abakozi batanga inkunga zo mu mahanga bafite ubunararibonye bukomeye bari kubuzwa kujya muri Palu.
Hakurikijwe ibigenwa n’amabwiriza yo muri Indonezihya ku byerekeye amafaranga, ibikoresho n’abakozi bavuye hanze bashobora gutnagira gukora igihe ahatangirwa ubufasha ku biza hatangajwe ko hita ku biza byo ku rwego rw’igihugu.
Ntabwo byari byaba.
Umuvugizi wa Croix Rouge yo muri Indoneziya yagize ati: "Biracyari ikiza cyo ku rwego rw’intara."
"Igihe leta ivuze ko nta, "Nta kibazo, ari ikiza cyo ku rwego rw’igihugu," dushobora gufungura ubufasha bwo ku rwego mpuzamahanga ariko rangamimerere ryari ryaboneka."
Ubwo ijoro rya kabiri ryageraga kuri Palu nyuma y’umutingito na tsunami byo ku wa Gatanu, inshuti n’imiryango y’abo babuze bari bafite icyizere cy’uko abo bakunda bazaboneka ku bw’igitangaza bakarokoka ibiza.
Ku wa Gatandatu, umwana muto w’umuhungu yakuwe muri ruhurura.
Ku Cyumweru, abatanga ubutabazi bakijije umugore wari wafatiwe mu bisigazwa by’inzu mu ghe cy’iminsi ibiri aruhande rwe hari umurambo wa mama we.
Gendon Subandono, umutoza w’ikipe y’igihugu cya Indoneziya y’umukino wo kugendera mu mitaka, yari yaratoje abakinnyi babiri baburiwe irengero bagombaga gukina Imikino nyaziya, iyo mikino yarangiye mu ntangiriro z’uku kwezi yari yabereye muri Indoneziya.
Bwana Mandagi yavuze ko abandi bari bafatiwe muri hoteri ya Roa Roa Hotel, bari abanyeshuri be.
Ati: "Nk’umutoza mukuru mu mukino wo kugendera mu mutaka, nanjye mfite amarangamutima yanjye yihariye."
Bwana Gendon yavuze uko, nyuma y’amasaha hatangajwe amakuru y’uko hoteri ya Roa Roa Hotel yaguye mu bakina umukino wo kugendera mu mutaka, yoherereje n’akababaro kenshi ubutumwa kuri WhatsApp abwoherereza abari mu marushanwa bakomoka muri Palu, bari mu iserukiramuco ryaberaga ku nkombe z’inyanja.
Gusa ubutumwa bwe, bwagaragaje ko bwoherejwe ariko butasomwe.
Ati: "Ndatekereza ko ubutumwa butasomwe."
Abajura bibye amadorali 26 750 mu gihe yakurwaga mu cyuma cya ATM kuri Newport muri Levee
Mu gitondo cyo ku wa Gatanu, abajura bibye amadorali 26 750 umukozi wa Brink aho yarari gukura amafaranga mu cyuma cya ATM kuri Newport muri Levee, hakurikijwe amakuru yatangajwe n’Ishami rya Polisi ryo muri Newport.
Umushoferi w’imodoka yarari gukura amafaranga mu cyuma cya ATM mu nyubako y’imyidagaduro, ari no kwitegura gutanga anadi mafaranga, ibyo bikaba bikubiye mu byo ushinzwe gukora iperereza witwa Dennis McCarthy yanditse mu makuru yatangajwe.
Mu gihe yari ahuze, undi mugabo "yahise aza aturutse inyuma y’umukozi wa Brink" maze amwiba igikapu kirimo amafaranga yagombaga gutanga.
Abatangabuhamya babonye abakekwaho ibyaha benshi bahunga ahabereye icyaha, hakurikijwe amakuru yatangajwe, ariko Polisi ntiyigeze isobanura neza umubare w’abantu bari muri ubwo bujura.
Umuntu wese ufite amakuru yerekeye imyirondoro y’abo bantu yahamagara Polisi ya Newport kuri 859-292-3680.
Kanye West: Umuraperi yahinduye izina rye yitwa Ye
Umuraperi Kanye West agiye guhindura izina rye yitwe Ye.
Ku wa Gatandatu, atangaza izo mpinduka kuri Twitter yagize ati: "Nzi mu buryo bwemewe ko nitwa Kanye West."
West, ufite imyaka 41, hashize igihe yihaye akazina k’akabyiniriro ka Ye kandi yitiriye iryo zina rihimbano arubumu ye ya munani, ikaba yarasohotse muri Kamena.
Izo mpinduka zije mbere y’uko agaragara mu kiganiro cyitwa Saturday Night Live, aho biteganyijwe ko asohotera arubumu ye yitwa Yandhi.
Uwahimbye ikiganiro yavuze ko asimbuje uwo muhanzi Ariana Grande mu kiganiro aho we yavuze ko atakije "ku mpamvu z’amarangamutima."
Ndetse no kuba ari impine y’izina rye akoresha mu buryo bw’umwuga, West yigeze kuvuga ko iryo jambo rifite igisobanuro kijyanye n’idini kuri we.
Mu ntangiriro z’umwaka Wese yavuze ari kuganira kuri arubumu ye n’uwakira abatumirwa kuri radiyo witwa Big Boy ko "yizera ko 'ye' ari ijambo rikunda gukoreshwa cyane muri Bibiliya kandi muri Bibiliya rikaba risobanura 'you (wowe)'".
"Rero, ndi wowe, ndi twe, ni twe.
Byavuye kuri Kanye, bikaba bisobanura umwe rukimbi, bikaba ari Ye; bikaba bigaragaza ishusho y’ibyiza, ibibi dukora, ibidutera urujijo, buri kimwe.
Arubumu igaragaza ishusho y’abo turi bo."
Ni umwe mu baraperi bazwi wigeze uhindura izina rye.
Sean Combs waruzwi nka Puff Daddy, P. Diddy cyangwa Diddy, ariko uyu mwaka yatangaje ko akunda izina rya Love na Brother Love.
Uwahoze akorana na West, JAY-Z, na we yandika iryo zina akoresheje akarongo cyangwa akaryandika mu nyuguti nkuru.
Perezida wa Megizike witwa AMLO yarahiriye kudakoresha igisirikare gihangana n’abasivire
Perezida watowe wa Megizike witwa Andres Manuel Lopez Obrador yarahiriye ko atazigera akoresha abasirikare ahangana n’abasivire mu gihe igihugu kiri gusatira isabukuru y’imyaka 50 hibukwa ukwihimura kwamenetsemo amaraso menshi y’abanyeshuri.
Ku wa Gatandatu, Lopez Obrador ari ku nyubako ya Tlatelolco Plaza yijeje ko "atazigera akoresha abasirikare mu gucecekesha abanyamegizike."
Abasirikare barashe ku bari mu myigaragambyo y’amahoro ku ngoro tariki ya 2 Ukwakira 1968, hapfa abantu 300 muri icyo gihe ubwo muvoma y’abanyeshuri batavuga rumwe na leta yari iri gukomera muri Amerika yo hagati.
Lopez Obrador yijeje ko hagiye gufashwa urubyiruko rw’abanyamegizike atanga inkunga y’amafaranga ku banyeshuri no gufungura kaminuza za leta nyinshi.
Yavuze ko kutagira akazi no kubura amahirwe yo kwiga bituma urubyiruko rwishora mu mitwe y’abagizi ba nabi.
Amerika igomba gukuba kabiri amafaranga yatangwaga mu bwenge buhangano
Mu gihe Ubushinwa buri gukora ibikorwa byinshi bijyanye n’ubwenge buhangano, Amerika igomba gukuba kabiri amafaranga ikoresha mu bushakashatsi bwo muri uru rwego, ibyo bikaba byaravuzwe n’umushoramari n’ukora mu by’ubwenge buhangano witwa Kai-Fu Lee, wakoreye Google, Microsoft na Apple.
Ibyo bitekerezo bije nyuma y’aho ibice byinshi bya leta y’Amerika byagize icyo bitangaza ku by’ubwenge buhangano; nubwo muri rusange Amerika idafite ingamba zizwi zerekeye iby’ubwenge buhangano.
Hagati aho, Ubushinwa bwatangije gahunda yabwo umwaka ushize: Bugamije kuba ubwa 1 mu guhanga udushya mu by’ubwenge buhangano mu mwaka wa 2030.
Lee ati : "Gukuba kabiri ingengo y’imari ikoreshwa mu bushakashatsi bw’ubwenge buhangano byaba ari intangiriro nziza, bitewe ni uko ibindi bihugu bikiri inyuma cyane ya Amerika kandi turi gushaka uko twagera ku buhanga buhambaye mu by’ubwenge buhangano."
Gukuba kabiri amafaranga y’inkunga bishobora gukuba kabiri amahirwe y’ibikorwa by’indashyikirwa mu by’ubwenge buhangano bikomeye bagerwaho muri Amerika, bikaba ari byo Lee yabwiye televiziyo ya CNBC mu kiganiro cyo muri iki cyumweru.
Lee, wanditse igitabo cyitwa "AI Superpowers: China, Silicon Valley and the New World Order" cyashyizwe ahagaragara muri uku kwezi na Houghton Mifflin Harcourt, akaba ari Umuyobozi Mukuru wa Sinovation Ventures, ikaba ari sosiyete yashoye amafaranga mu ma sosiyete akomeye mu by’ubwenge buhangano yo mu Bushinwa, Face++.
Muri za 1980 muri kaminuza ya Carnegie Mellon University yakoze ku buryo bukoresha ubwenge buhangano burusha ubwenge umukinnyi ufite amanota menshi w’umunyamerika witwa Othello, nyuma y’aho aza kuba Umuyobozi nshingwabikorwa w’ishami ry’ubushakashatsi rya Microsoft anaba umuyobozi wa Google ishami ryo mu Bushinwa.
Lee yemeje amarushanwa rya leta y’Amerika mu by’ikoranabuhanga nk’amarushanwa ya Defense Advanced Research Projects Agency's Robotics Challenge maze abazwa igihe amarushanwa y’ubutaha azabera kugira ngo abafashe kumenya abahanga bo mu minsi iri imbere.
Lee avuga ko akenshi abashakashatsi bo muri Amerika bagenda bakora cyane kugira ngo batsindire inkunga ya leta.
Lee ati: "Ubushinwa si bwo buri gutwara abarimu b’abahanga, ahubwo bari gutwara n’amasosiyete."
Facebook, Google n’andi masosiyete y’ikoranabuhanga yahaye akazi abahanga bazwi bo muri za kaminuza kugira ngo bakore ku mishinga y’iby’ubwenge buhangano mu myaka mike ishize.
Lee yavuze ko impinduka mu ngamba z’ubwimukira zinashobora gufasha Amerika kongera imbaraga mu by’ubwenge buhangano.
Ati: "Ntekereza ko uburenganzira bwo gutura burundu muri Amerika buzwi nka green card bugomba guhita buhabwa abafite impamyabumenyi y’ikirenga mu by’ubuhanga karemano."
Akanama ka leta y’Ubushinwa katanze Gahunda y’iterambere mu by’ubwenge buhangano mu bisekuru bikurikira muri Nyakanga 2017.
Lee avuga ko umuryango nterankunga mu bya siyansi mu Bushinwa utera inkunga abantu bo mu bigo by’amashuri mu buryo bumwe busa nk’ubwo Umuryango nterankunga mu bya siyansi n’indi miryango ya leta iha amafaranga abashakashatsi bo muri Amerika, ariko imirimo yo mu rwego rw’uburezi ifite ireme riri hasi mu Bushinwa.
Mu ntangiriro z’uyu mwaka, Minisiteri y’ingabo z’Amerika y ashyizeho Ikigo gihuriweho n’izindi nzego mu by’ubwenge buhangano, bikaba bisobanuye ko hari kunozwa imikoranire hagati y’inganda n’amashuri kandi Perezidansi y’Amerika ikaba yaratangaje ko hagiye gushyirwaho Komite yihariye igenzura iby’ubwenge buhangano.
Kandi uku kwezi DARPA yatangaje ko igiye gushora miriyari 2 z’amadorali mu gikorwa cyitwa AI Next.
Naho ku byerekeye Umuryango wa NSF, kuri ubu uri gushora imari irenga miriyoni 100 z’amadorali ku mwaka mu bushakashatsi mu by’ubwenge buhangano.
Hagati aho, abashinga amategeko muri Amerika bifuje ko hashyirwaho Komisiyo y’igihugu ishinzwe umutekano mu by’ubwenge buhangano, hashize amezi menshi ntacyo bakoze.
Abanyamasedoniya batoye kamparamaka harebwa niba bahindura izina ry’igihugu
Ku Cyumweru, abaturage ba Masedoniya batoye kamparampaka harebwa niba hahindurwa izina ikitwa "Repubulika ya Masedoniya y’amajyaruguru," kikaba ari igikorwa gishobora gukemura amakimbirane amaze imyaka mirongo ari hagati yayo n’Ubugereki akaba yarayibujuje gutanga ubusabe bwo kuba umunyamuryango mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi n’Umuryango wo gutabarana mu bya gisirikare uzwi nka OTAN.
Ubugereki, bufite intara yitwa Masedoniya, buvuga ko izina ry’igihugu gituranyi cyo mu majyaruguru kitiranwa n’intara yayo kandi bukaba bwarahagaritse ubusabe bw’icyo gihugu bwo kwinjira mu Muryango wo gutabarana mu bya gisirikare uzwi nka OTAN n’Umuryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi.
Leta zombi zagiranye amasezerano muri Kamena hashingiwe izina rishya ryatanzwe, ariko abatabishyigikiye bakunda igihugu bavuga ko iyo mpinduka ishobora gutesha agaciro ikiranga ubwoko bw’abaturage nyamwinshi b’abasalivici bo muri Masedoniya.
Perezida Gjorge Ivanov yavuze ko atazatora iyo kamparampaka kandi gukomanyiriza ibikorwa byo kuyamamaza byatumye habaho urujijo niba abantu bake bashoboka bazaza gutora bazagera kuri 50 ku ijana by’abakenewe kugira ngo kamparampaka igire agaciro.
Ikibazo kiri mu gasanduka gashyirwamo amajwi ya kamparampaka kigira kiti: "Wemera ko tuba abanyamuryango b’Umuryango wo gutabarana mu bya gisirikare wa OTAN n’Umuryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi hakurikijwe amasezerano twagiranye n’Ubugereki."
Abashyigikiye ko izina rihindurwa, harimo Minisitiri w’Intebe Zoran Zaev, bavuga ko ni ikiguzi gikwiye kwishyurwa kugira ngo bakomeze barebe ko bakwinjira mu miryango ikomeye nk’Umuryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi na OTANI ku bwa Masedoniya, kimwe mu bihugu byashibutse mu ihirima rya Yugosalaviya.
Olivera Georgijevska, w’imyaka 79, uturuka muri Skopje agira ati: "Naje uyu munsi gutora ahazaza h’igihugu, ku rubyiruko rwa Masedoniya; kugira ngo babeho mu bwisanzure bari mu Muryango w’Ubumwe bw’Uburayi kubera ko bisobanuye ko twabaho ubuzima butekanye kurushaho ku bwacu twese."
Nubwo bitari mu rwego rw’amategeko, abadepite bahagije bavuze ko bazubahiriza ibizava mu matora kugira ngo hagire icyemezo gifatwa.
Guhindura izina bisaba ko byemezwa na bibiri bya gatatu by’abagize Inteko Ishinga Amategeko.
Komisiyo y’igihugu ishinzwe amatora yavuze ko nta bidasanzwe byatangajwe kugeza saa 1 z’umugoroba.
Icyakora, abitabiriye amatora bageze gusa kuri 16 ku ijana, ugereranyije na 34 ku ijana mu mataro y’abadepite aheruka mu 2016 ubwo 66 ku ijana by’abatora biyandikishije ari bo batoye.
Uwatoreye mu murwa mukuru wa Skopje witwa Tanevski, w’imyaka 62, yagize ati: "Naje nje gutora kubera ko abana banjye, aho tugomba gutura ni mu Burayi."
Minisitiri w’Intebe wa Masedoniya, Zoran Zaev, umugore we Zorica n’umuhungu we Dushko batoreye kamparampaka muri Masedoniya kuguhindura izina ry’igihugu bikaba byafungura amayira yo kujya mu Muryango wa OTAN n’Umuryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi muri Strumica, muri Masedoniya tariki y a 30 Nzeli 2018.
Imbere y’Inteko Ishinga Amategeko ya Skopje, Vladimir Kavardarkov, w’imyaka 54, yari gutegura podiyumu nto arambura intebe imbere y’amahema yashinzwe n’abashaka gukoma mu nkokora kamparampaka.
Kavadarkov ati: "Dukeneye kujya mu Muryango wa OTAN no mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi, ariko turifuza kuyinjiramo twemye, tutanyuze mu gikari."
"Turi igihugu gikennye, ariko dufite icyubahiro.
Niba batifuza kudufata nka Masedoniya, tushobora kwerekeza ku bindi bihugu nk’Ubushinwa n’Uburusiya maze tukajya mu Muryango w’ubumwe uhuza Uburayi n’Aziya."
Minisitiri w’Intebe, Zaev, yavuze ko abanyamuryango ba OTAN bazana ishoramari rinini rikenewe muri Masedoniya, aho abatagira akazi barenga 20 ku ijana.
Nyuma yo gutora, Zaev yagize ati: "Nizera ko abaturage benshi bazatora neza kubera ko abarenga 80 ku ijana by’abaturage bacu bafuza kujya mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi n’Umuryango wa OTAN."
Yavuze ko "yego" igomba kuba "kwemeza ahazaza hacu."
Ubushakashatsi bwakozwe ku wa Mbere ushizwe n’Ikigo cya Masedoniya gikora ubushakashatsi mu bya politiki bwagaragaje ko hagati ya 30 na 43 ku ijana by’abatora bashobora gutora kamparampaka, bikaba ari umubare utageze k’usabwa kugira ngo amatora yemerwe.
Ubundi bushakashatsi, bwakozwe na televiziyo ya Telma yo muri Masedoniya, bwabonye ko 57 ku ijana by’abasubije bateganya gutora ku Cyumweru.
Muri abo, 70 ku ijana bavuze ko bazatora yego.
Kugira ngo kamparampaka yemerwe hekenwe kuza abagera kuri 50 ku ijana kongeraho ijwi rimwe.
Iyo bitagezweho, kamparampaka yafatwa nk’ikibazo kuri politiki y’abashyigikiye leta y’uburengerazuba kuva yafata ubutegetsi muri Gicurasi umwaka ushize.
Reba: Umukinnyi w’ikipe y a Manchester City yacenze abakinnyi b’inyuma bose b’ikipe ya Brighton atsinda igitego
Sergio Aguero na Raheem Sterling bajujubije abakinnyi b’inyuma ba Brighton mu mukino Manchester City yatsinzemo ibitego 2-0 ku wa Gatandatu kuri sitade ya Etihad i Manchester, mu Bwongereza.
Aguero yakoze ku buryo bigaragara nk’ibyoroshye cyane ubwo yatsindaga igitego ku munota wa 65.
Umusatirizi w’umunyarijantina yahawe umupira mu kibuga hagati guhanahana umupira bigitangira.
Yirukanse hagati y’abakinnyi b’inyuma bagera kuri batatu bakinira Brighton, mbere yo kwiruka akabasiga.
Ubwo Aguero yisanze akikijwe n’abakinnyi bane b’imipira y’icyatsi.
Acenga umukinnyi wugarira umwe mbere yo kwiruka agasiga abandi benshi ku ruhande rw’urubuga rw’amahina y’ikipe ya Brighton.
Noneho atanga umupira ibumoso bwe, awuhereza Sterling.
Rutahizamu w’umwongereza yakoresheje umupira yakozeho bwa mbere kugira ngo yongere ahereze umupira Aguero, wakoresheje ikirenge cy’iburyo cye maze atsinda umunyezamu w’ikipe ya Brighton witwa Mathew Ryan aho yamuteye umupira ugana mu gice cy’iburyo cy’izamu.
Umutoza w’ikipe ya City, Pep Guardiola yabwiye abanyamakuru ati: "Aguero ari kugorwa n’ibibazo afite mu maguru ye."
"Twavuze ko dushobora kumukinisha iminota, 55, 60.
Ni uko byagenze.
Twagize amahirwe kuba yaratsinze igitego muri icyo gihe."
Ariko ni Sterling wahaye ikipe yambara ubururu bwerurutse amahirwe ya mbere yo gutsinda umukino wo muri Shampiyona yo mu Bwongereza.
Igitego cyabonetse ku munota wa 29.
Aguero yahawe umupira wari utewe mu rubuga rw’amahina rw’ikipe ya Brighton muri uwo mukino.
Noneho yohereza umupira mwiza ku gice cy’ibumoso uhasanga Leroy Sane.
Sane acenga gake mbere yo kuwuterera imbere ngo Sterling awusange aho yawuteye ku ipoto ryo ku rundi ruhande.
Umusatirizi w’ikipe yambara ubururu bwerurutse yateye umupira mu rushundura mbere yo kwinyereza agashyira mu izamu umupira wari ugarutse.
Ikipe ya City izahura na Hoffenheim mu itsinda ry’Irushanwa ry’amakipe yabaye aya mbere iwayo mu Burayi saa 12:55 z’umugoroba ku wa Kabiri kuri sitade ya Rhein-Neckar-Arena muri Sinsheim, mu Budage.
Scherzer yifuza ko ikipe itavuzwe izina ikina na Rockies
Mu gihe ikipe ya Nationals yasezerwe mu mikino yo kwishyura, nta mpamvu nini yari ihari yo guhatiriza gutangira andi marushanwa.
Ariko umukinnyi uhora yifuza kujya mu marushanwa witwa Scherzer yizera ko azajya mu kibuga ku Cyumweru agahura n’ikipe ya Colorado Rockies, ariko mu gihe hari imikino yo kwishyura ari gukinira Rockies, ikaba irusha umukino umwe w’itsinzi ikipe ya Los Angeles Dodgers muri NL West.
Rockies yabonye byibuze umwanya wo gukina imikino yo kwishyura aho yatsinze 5-2 ikipe ya Nationals ku wa Gatanu, ariko iracyashaka gutwara igikombe cyayo cya mbere mu itsinda irimo.
"Nubwo ntacyo turi gukinira, byibuze dushobora kubasha kujya mu kibuga tuzi uko byifashe hano muri Denver aho abantu benshi n’andi makipe bizaba bikinira ahari ku rwego rwo hejuru rw’imikino yose ishobora gukinwa uyu mwaka.
Kubera iki ntakwifuza gukina muri uwo mukino?"
Ikipe ya Nationals igiye gutangaza umukino wa mbere ku Cyumweru, ariko byavuzwe ko izareka Scherzer agakina muri uwo mukino.
Scherzer, uzaba atangiye umukino we wa 34, yavuye mu mwanya yari asanzwe akinamo ku wa Kane ariko azongera akine mu mwanya yari asanzwe akinamo ku Cyumweru.
Umukinnyi wo ku ruhande rw’iburyo wa Washington afite 18-7 n’amanota 2.53 ERA no gutera imipira 300 agahamyamo 220 2/3 muri uyu mwaka w’imikino.
