"Ibyo twakoze byose bizaba biri mu kaga mu Ugushyingo.
Harabura ibyumweru bitanu ngo amwe mu matora y’ingenzi mu gihe cyacu abe.
Ati: “Iki ni ikintu gikomeye cyane, ntabwo ndi kwiyamamaza ariko ndi kwiyamamaza mu by’ukuri bikaba ari yo mpamvu ntaho ntari kugera ndwanira abakandida bakomeye."
Trump yakomeje agira ati: "Urabona iri tsinda ribi cyane, ribi ariko ry’abahezanguni ry’abademokarate, urabona ibiri kuba ubu ngubu.
Kandi biyemeje ko bagomba kwisubiza imbaraga bakoresheje uburyo bwose bushoboka, ubona ubugome bwabo, ububi bwabo.
Ntabwo bita ku wo bababaza, uwo bagomba guhutaza kugira ngo babone imbaraga n’ibyo bagenzura, icyo bifuza n’imbaraga n’icyo bagenzura, ntabwo tuzabibaha."
Abademokarate bafite gahunda yo "kwinangira no kubuza ibikorwa."
Ati: "Kandi urabona ko mu minsi ine ishize," avuga ku bademokarate "barakaye, b’abagome kandi babi ndetse batari n’abo kwizerwa."
Yavuze kuri Komite ya Sena ishinzwe ubutabera avuga ku mudemokarate witwa Senateri Dianne Feinstein, aho yahise avugirizwa indurua mu bari aho.
"Muribuka igisubizo yatanze?

Uh, uh, ngwiki?

Risigaye ritihanganira abavuga ibyo batekereza
Ubwo abarwanashyaka ba Momentum b’ishyaka ryo mu gace ntuyemo batoraga kugira ngo banyamagane, byari bitunguranye cyane.
Muri make, ni njye ugezweho mu badepite b’ishyaka ry’abakozi wabwiwe ko ntahawe ikaze ryo kuvuga icyo ntekereza.
Mugenzi wanjye wo mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko, Joan Ryan, na we yafashwe muri ubwo buryo kubera ko yamaganye ku buryo bwumvikana abanga abayahudi.
Ku kibazo cyanjye, igikorwa cyo kunyamagana cyari icyo kunenga kubera ko ntumvikana na Jeremy Corbyn.
Ku kamaro k’ingamba z’ubukungu zirimo kubazwa ibyo abantu bakora, ku mutekano w’igihugu, ku Burayi, ku buryo bujimije bikaba ari ibibazo bisa n’ibyo Jeremy atemeranyagaho n’abayobozi babanje.
Itangazo ryamamaza inama y’ishyaka rya Nottingham East Labour yo ku wa Gatanu ryavugaga ko "twifuza ko inama idaheza kandi itanga umusaruro."
Hafi imyaka umunani nk’umudepite w’ishyaka ry’abakozi, mu ijoro ryo ku wa Gatanu inama ya GC ni ko yagenze neza.
Ikibabaje ni uko uyu munsi, ari uko inama nyinshi atari ko ziri gukorwamo kandi isezerano ry’ishyirwaho rya politiki "yuje urukundo n’urugwiro" ryaribagiranye na mbere y’uko ritangira.
Byagiye birushaho kugaragara ko ibitekerezo bitandukanye bitihanganirwa mu ishyaka ry’abakozi kandi buri gitekerezo kigomba kugenwa niba cyemewe n’ubuyobozi bw’ishyaka.
Ibi byatangiye nyuma gato y’aho Jeremy abereye umuyobozi, mu gihe mu gihe abo turi mu ishyaka rimwe natekerezaga ko twari dusangiye ibitekerezo bya politiki batangiye kwitega ko mfata ikindi cyerekezo maze nkerekeza ibitekerezo byanjye mu bindi ntagakwiye kuba nemera; yaba ari ku mutekano w’igihugu cyangwa ku isoko rimwe ry’Ubumwe bw’ibihugu by’Uburayi.
Igihe cyose mvugiye mu ruhame; kandi si ngombwa icyo naba mvuga icyo ari cyo cyose, hakurikiraho kunsagarira ku buryo bukabije ku mbuga mpuzambaga basaba ko nirukanwa, mva mu bya politiki iharanira imibereho myiza ya rubanda, bambwira ko ntakagombye kuba ndi mu ishyaka ry’abakozi.
Kandi ngo si bwo bunararibonye mfite.
Ni byo koko, ndabizi ko mfite amahirwe kurusha bagenzi banjye kuko ibitekerezo bintangwaho biba bijyanye na politiki.
Ntangazwa cyane n’ubunyamwuga n’ubwitange bwa bagenzi banjye bibasirwa bishingiye ku gitsina cyangwa ibara ry’uruhu buri munsi ariko ntibacike intege.
Ikintu kimwe gitenguha muri uru ruhando rwa politiki ni urwego rwo kwibasirwa aho byafashwe nk’ibintu bisanzwe.
Mu cyumweru gishize, Jeremy Corbyn yavuze ko ishyaka ry’abakozi rigomba kugira umuco wo koroherana.
Igihari ni uko twese tutari abarangwa n’ibitekerezo bitandukanye kandi igikorwa cyo gutora cyangwa gushinja umuntu ko "yatererwa icyizere" ku mategeko amwe n’amwe y’ishyaka bituma ishyaka ritaguka.
Nagiye ngirwa inama nyinshi mu myaka ibiri ishize nsabwa ko nakomeza kutazamura umutwe, no kutavuga byinshi cyane, bityo ko "nta kibazo nzagira."
Ariko ibyo si byo byanzanye muri politiki.
Hashize imyaka 32 ninjiye mu ishyaka ry’abakozi ubwo narindi umunyeshuri, mbitewe n’uburangare bwa guverinoma ya Thatcher bwatumye nsigara naratakarije icyizere ubumenyi bwose bwatangwaga mu mashuri, nashatse uko narinda kurushaho serivisi zihabwa rubanda ku bazikeneye cyane; yaba nkora nk’umujyanama w’urwego rwa leta rw’ibanze cyangwa minisitiri muri leta.
Sinigeze mpisha politiki yanjye, harimo no mu gihe cy’amatora aheruka.
Nta n’umwe muri Nottingham East wakabaye aterwa urujijo na politiki yanjye ndetse n’aho tutumvikana n’ubuyobozi buriho.
Ku bakoze igikorwa cyo ku wa Gatanu, icyo navuga ni uko mu gihe igihugu kiri kugana muri gahunda yo kuva mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi izwi nka Brexit ikaba izabangamira ingo, abakora ibikorwa by’ubucuruzi na serivisi zihabwa rubanda, sinumva ko hari ubushake bwo guta umwanya n’ingufu ku bunyangamugayo bwanjye mfitiye umuyobozi w’ishyaka ry’abakozi.
Mu by’ukuri, ubutumwa mfite ntabwo bugenewe Nottingham Momentum, ahubwo bugenewe abo mu gace kanjye batora, yaba ari mu ishyaka ry’abakozi cyangwa ataririmo: Ntewe ishema no kubakorera kandi ndabasezeranya ko nta bikangisho byo kunyirukana cyangwa ibyitezwe mu rwego rwa politiki bizambuza gukora cyane mu byo nizera ari byo nyungu zanyu mwese.

Ayr 38 - 17 Melrose: Ayr itaratsindwa yagiye ku mwanya wa mbere
Ibitego bibiri byageragejwe gutsindwa byari bigiye guhindura uko umukino warangiye, ariko nta gushidikanya ko Ayr yari ikwiye gutsinda muri uyu mukino uryoheye ijisho ukaba wanakwitwa umukino w’umunsi w’irushanwa rya Tennent.
Ubu ni bo bayoboye urutonde, akaba ari yo kipe yonyine itaratsindwa mu makipe icumi.
Hanyuma, byagaragaje ko ari ikipe ifite uburinzi bukomeye, ndetse no kugira amahirwe, bikaba byaratumye ikipe yakiriye umukino n’umutoza wayo Peter Murchie babona impamvu yo kwishima.
Ati: "Twageragejwe mu mukino kugeza ubu kandi ntitwari twatsindwa, rero ngomba kwishima."
Robyn Christie wa Melrose ati: "Harashimirwa Ayr, babyaje umusaruro amahirwe babonye kuturusha."
Ishoti ryatewe na Grant Anderson ku munota wa 14, ryabyajwemo igitego na Frazier Climo, bituma Ayr iyobora, ariko, ikarita y’umuhondo yahawe kapiteni w’ikipe ya Ekose witwa Rory Hughes, yatanzwe n’ikipe ya Warriors kugira ngo akinire ikipe y’igihugu, yemerewe na Melrose kugira ngo ajye mu ikipe na Jason Baggot agerageza gutera umupira utwarabyajwemo igitego.
Climo yongeye igitego ku cyari gifitwe na Ayr atsinze penaliti, mbere y’aho, habura gato ngo igice cya mbere kirangire, yatsinze igitgo ari wenyine maze biba ibitego 17-5 bya Ayr mu kiruhuko cy’igihe cya mbere.
Ariko Melrose yatangiye neza igice cya kabiri maze umupira watewe na Patrick Anderson ubyatazwamo igitego na Baggot, bigabanya amanota babarushaga agera kuri atanu.
Ubwo hazamo ibyo gutinda mu kibuga ku bw’imvune ikomeye ya Ruaridh Knott, watawe mu ngombi akurwa mu kibuga, noneho umukino urongera uratangira, aho Ayr yakomeje gusatira ku mupira watewe na Stafford McDowall ubyazwamo igitego na Climo.
Kaptieni wungirije w’ikipe ya Ayr witwa Blair Macpherson yahawe ikarita y’umuhondo noneho, Melrose ituma undi mukinnyi babarushaga abyaza igitego umupira watewe na Bruce Colvine, nyuma y’umukino warurimo igitutu cyinshi.
Ikipe yari yakiye yishyuye igitego yatsinzwe, ni mu gihe Struan Hutchinson yari yahawe ikarita y’umuhondo ku byo gutera takere Climo adafite umupira, inyuma gato y’umurongo w’urubuga rw’amahina, MacPherson yakojeje umupira hasi inyuma kugira ngo yatake ikipe ya Ayr.
Climo yatsinze igitego nk’uko yabigenje umukino ucyongera gutangira, nyuma y’aho Kyle Rowe yafatiye David Armstrong mu rubuga rw’amahina maze akoherereze umupira umukinnyi w’iruhande witwa Gregor Henry mu kugerageza ku nshuro ya gatanu kw’ikipe yari yakiriye umukino.
Umukinnyi w’ikipe ya Still Game yiteguye umwuga mushya mu rwego rw’amaresitora
Umukinnyi w’ikipe ya Still Game witwa Ford Kieran asa nk’aho yiteguye kujya mu rwego rwo kwakira abashyitsi nyuma y’aho yabonye ko yahamagawe n’umuyobozi ubifitiye uruhushya muri sosiyete ikora mu bya resitora.

'Inyanja ni iyacu': igihugu kidakora ku nyanja cya Boliviya cyizera ko kizongera gufungura inzira ikigeza kuri Pasifika
Abashinzwe kurinda umutekano wo mu mazi bakaba ari abo mu mazi bakaze bafite icyacaro muri La Paz.
Inyubako za leta zifite idarapo ry’ubururu bwerurutse.
Ibirindiro by’abarwanira mu mazi bo mu kiyaga cya Titicaca baturutse muri Amazon bafite intego ibaranga: "Dufite uburenganzira ku nyanja.
Tuyifata nk’inshingano."
Mu gihugu cyose kidakora ku nyanja cya Boliviya, magingo aya hibukwa intambara cyatsinzwe barwanira inkengero z’inyanja na Shili mu makimbirane yetembyemo imivu y’amaraso mu kinyejana cya 19; mu gihe hifuzwa cyane kongera kugendera mu bwato mu nyanja ya Pasifika indi nshuro.
Ahari icyo cyizere ni cyo cyinshi bagize mu myaka mirongo, mu gihe Boliviya itegereje umwanzuro w’urukingo mpuzamahanga ku itariki ya 1 Ukwakira nyuma y’imyaka itanu higwa ku mwanzuro wafatwa.
Roberto Calzadilla, umudipolomate w’umunyaboliviya ati: "Boliviya ifite imbaraga, ishyaka ry’ubumwe n’umutuzo kandi yiteze ko hazafatwa umwanzuro uyinogeye."
Abanyaboliviya bazareba umwanzuro w’urukiko mpuzamahanga rwa ICJ kuri za ekara za rutura mu gihugu cyose, bizera ko urwo rukiko rw’i Lahe ruzasanga ikirego cyatanzwe na Boliviya gifite ishingiro; nyuma y’imyaka mirongo y’ibiganiro bitatangaga umusaruro, aho Shiri yahatirijwe kuganira ku buryo yaha Boliviya uburenganzira bwo kugera ku nyanja.
Evo Morales, Perezida ufite impano unakunda igihugu wa Boliviya, uhanganye kugira ngo azongere atorwe umwaka utaha; nawe yizeye cyane ko umwanzuro wo ku wa Mbere uzagenda neza.
Mu mpera za Kanama yarahiye agira ati: "Turabura gato cyane ngo dusubire ku nyanja ya Pasifika."
Ariko bamwe mu basesenguzi bizera ko urukiko rutapfa gufata umwanzuro wagwa neza Boliviya kandi ni yo yawufata hahinduka bike.
Ishami ry’Umuryango w’abibumbye riri muri Buholandi nta bubasha rifite bwo gutanga akarere ka Shiri kandi rivuga ko ritagena ibizava mu biganiro bishobora kuba.
Paz Zárate, impuguke mu by’amategeko mpuzamahanga ikomoka muri Shiri ivuga ko: “Uwo mwanzuro w’urukiko rwa ICJ uje nyuma y’amezi atandatu gusa nyuma y’aho iburanisha ryagaragaje ko ikirego "kitari kigoranye."
Mu rwego rwo kurushaho kugaragaza icyo Boliviya iharanira, imyaka ine ishize ishobora kuba yaratumye ibyagezweho bisubira inyuma.
Zárate ati: "Ikibazo cyo gukora ku nyanja cyafashwe bugwate na leta ya Boliviya iriho."
Avuga ko amagambo agamije gushoza intambara ya Morales yatumye n’umutima mwiza abanyashiri bari basigaranye uyoyoka.
Boliviya na Shiri bakomeje igibaniro, ariko bizagorana cyane kuba bakomeza kuganira nyuma y’ibi.
Ibihugu byombi ntabwo byigeze bihana ba ambasaderi kuva mu 1962.
Uwahoze ari Perezida Eduardo Rodríguez Veltzé, uhagararaiye Boliviya i Lahe, yanze igitekerezo kivuga ko ifatwa ry’ibyemezo by’urukiko byihuse bitari ngombwa.
Ati: “Ku wa Mbere, hazatuma Boliviya "ibona amahirwe adasanzwe yo kugirana umubano mushya na Shiri" n’amahirwe yo "gushyira akadomo k’amakimbirane yari amaze imyaka 139 kandi impande zombi zizabyungukiramo."
Calzadilla na we yahakanye ko Morales, ukiri umwe mu ba perezida bo muri Amerika yo hagati ukunzwe cyane, yarari gukoresha ikibazo cyo gukora ku nyanja mu nyungu za politiki.
Ati: "Boliviya ntabwo izigera yiyambura uburenganzira bwo gukora ku nyanja ya Pasifika."
"Uwo mwanzuro ni amahirwe yo kureba niba dukwiye kwibagirwa ahahise."
Koreya ya ruguru ivuga ko kureka gukora ibisasu kirimbuzi bitazakorwa kugeza igihe ishobora kwizerera Amerika
Minisitiri w’ububanyi n’amahanga wa Koreya ya ruguru, Ri Yong Ho, avuga ko igihugu cye kitazigera kireka gukora ibisasu kirimbuzi igihe kitizeye leta ya Washington.
Ri yabivuze ku wa Gatandatu mu Nama rusange y’Umuryango w’abibumbye.
Yasabye ko Umuryango w’abibumbye ukurikiza isezerano watanze mu nama yabereye muri Singapuru hagati y’abayobozi batumvikana.
Ayo magambo ayavuze mu gihe Umunyamabanga wa leta, Mike Pompeo, asa nk’aho ari hafi yo kongera gutangira ibiganiro ku by’ibisasu kirimbuzi bisa nk’ibyari byarahagaze nyuma y’amezi atatu y’ibiganiro byabereye muri Singapuru hamwe na perezida wa Koreya ya ruguru, Kim Jong Un.
Ri avuga ko "bitapfa gushoboka" hakomeje gutangwa ibihano byashyizweho kandi Amerika igakomeza kwanga kuvuga ku mugaragaro ko irangije intambara na Koreya, ibyo bikaba bitashyira Koreya ya ruguru ishyirwa ku mavi.
Washington irashyidikanya ku kwemera gusohora itangaza mu gihe leta ya Pyongyang itabanje gutera intambwe ya mbere mu kureka gukora ibisasu bya kirimbuzi.
Yaba Kim na Perezida w’Amerika, Donald Trump, bifuza ko habaho inama ya kabiri.
Ariko Pyongyang inengwa henshi ko ikomeje ku byo kureka gukora intwaro za kirimbuzi kuko igihugu kibona ko ari bwo buryo bwonyine yakwizeramo umutekano wacyo.
Pompeo ari guteganya gusura Pyongyang mu kwezi gutaha kugira ngo hategurwa inama ya kabiri izahuza Kim na Trump.
Igitaramo cy’imideri i Paris kigaragaza imyenda mishya igiye kugezwa ku mihanda ikomeye hafi yawe
Niba wifuza kongeresha ingofero zawe utunze cyangwa wifuza kwikingira izuba ntujye kure.
Abakora imyenda bitwa Valentino na Thom Browne bamuritse ingofero nini cyane mu itsinda ry’imyenda ryitwa SS19 ku muhanda aho iyo myambaro ari yo yatangije icyumweru cyahariwe imideri i Paris.
Ingofero z’urugara runini zagaragajwe henshi kuri rubuga rwa Instagram muri iyi mpeshyi kandi abo bazikoze bagaragaraije ibyo bahanze bitangaje mu birori byo kwerekana imideri.
Iyo ngofero yihariye yakozwe na Valentino ifite ibara rya beje ifite urugara rumeze nk’ibaba rugera imbere ahajya umutwe.
Ibindi biherekeza imyambaro binini cyane harimo, imirimbo imeze nka wotameroni, ingofero ifite urugara runini ndetse n’inanasi, ariko ntabwo zakorewe ku buryo zatuma umutwe wawe ukomeza gushyuha.
Thom Browne yanagaragaje itsinda rya masike zitangaje kandi mu gihe kijya kwegera umunsi mukuru wa Halloween.
Inyinshi muri masike zifite amabara zadozwe zashyizweho iminwa iza nk’iya Hannibal Lecter kurusha uko zadozwe ku buryo bwihariye.
Imwe muri masike yakozwe isa nk’iyo bambara bagiye kwibira munsi y’inyanja iriho n’agahombo bahumekeramo n’amataratara, mu gihe indi yasaga nk’ayisikirimu yayonze.
Kandi nukomeza kuvuga ibyerekeye iby’imideri ikomeye uraba ufite amahirwe.
Abareba iby’imideri bateganya ko izo ngoferi nini zishobora kugera ku mihanda ikomeye hafi yawe.
Izo ngefero nini zijya kumera nka 'La Bomba', ikaba ari ingofero ikoze mu byatsi bikomeye ifite urugara rwa cm 60 aho yagiye yambarwa n’abantu bakomeye guhera kuri Rihanna ukagera kuri Emily Ratajkowski.
Uruganda ruzwi rwakozwe ingofero nini cyane rwamamajwe ku mbuga mpuzambaga rwongeye kwerekana ibyo rwakoze mu gitaramo cyo kwerekana imideri, isakoshi ikoze mu byatsi bikomeye yo kujyana ku mucanga nini cyane ingana n’uwerekana imideri wambaye umwenda wo kogana waruri kuyerekana.
Isakoshi ikoze mu bibabi by’igiti cya raffia ya oranje yabanje gutwikwa, ikoreshejwe ibibabi by’icyo giti kandi hajuru hakaba hariho aho gufata hakozwe mu ruhu rw’umweru, ukaba ari cyo kijyana n’imenya cyari mu itsinda ry’imyambaro rya Jacquemus rizwi nka La Riviera SS19 mu cyumweru cyahariwe imideri i Paris.
Uwambika ibyamamare nka Luke Armitage yabwiye ikinyamakuru cya FEMAIL ati: 'Niteze ko ingofero nini n’amasakoshi yo ku mucanga bizagera ku mihanda ikomeye mu mpeshyi tahaa; mu gihe uwakoze ibyo bijyana n’imyenda yagize icyo ahindura gikomeye ku buryo habaho kwirengagiza ibijyana n’imyenda bifite ubunini bukabije.'
John Edward: Ubumenyi mu by’indimi ni ingenzi ku batuye isi
Amashuri yigenga muri Ekose akomeje kuza imbere mu ruhando rw’uburezi kandi bikaba byarakomeje mu 2018 ahagaragaye ibindi byavuye mu bizamini byiza cyane, bikaba byarashimangiye kurushaho ibyo abanyeshuri ku giti cyabo no muri rusange bagezeho muri siporo, ubugeni, umuziki n’ibindi bikorwa bijyanye n’abaturage.
Mu banyeshuri bagera ku 30 000 muri Ekose yose, ayo mashuri, ahagarariwe n’Akanama k’amashuri yigenga muri Ekose (SCIS), baharanira kugera ku rugero rwo hejuru rwo gutanga serivi zo ku rwego rwo hejuru yaba ku banyeshuri bahiga n’ababyeyi.
Amashuri yigenga agamije gutegura abanyeshuri bayo kurushaho no kugira ngo bajye mu mashuri yisumbuye, bakore umwuga bihitiyemo ndetse banagira umwanya mu baturage b’isi.
Nk’urwego rw’uburezi rushobora gushyiraho no gushyira mu bikorwa integanyanyigisho y’amashuri inogeye abanyeshuri, turi kubona indimi nshya zikomeza gukundwa no kuba ari isomo abanyeshuri bahitamo mu mashuri.
Nelson Mandela ati: "Iyo uvugishije umuntu mu rurimi yumva, ibyo umubyiye bijya mu mutwe.
Iyo umuvugishije mu rurimi kavukire rwe, ibyo umubwiye bijya mu mutima we."
Aya ni amagambo akomeye atwibutsa ko tutagomba kugendera ku Cyongereza gusa iyo twifuza kugirana umubano n’icyizere n’abantu bo mu bindi bihugu.
Uhereye mu bisubizo by’ibizamini biheruka by’uyu mwaka, dushobora kubona ko indimi ari zo ziri imbere ku mbonerahamwe aho zagiye zitsindwa cyane ku rugero rwo hejuru mu mashuri yigenga.
Igiteranyo cya 68 ku ijana by’abanyeshuri bize mu rurumi rw’amahanga babonye inota ryao hejuru rya A.
Amakuru yakusanyijwe n’akanama ka SCIS mu mashuri ari muri ako kanama agera ku 74, yagaragaje ko 72 ku ijana by’abanyeshuri babonye inota ryo hejuru rya A mu kimandare, mu gihe 72 ku ijana by’abo biga mu kidage, 69 ku ijana by’abo biga mu gifaransa naho 63 by’abiga mu cyesipanyoro babonye inota rya A.
Bigaragaza ko amashuri yigenga muri Ekose ari gushyigikira indimi zo mu mahanga hnk’ubumenyi by’ingenzi abana n’urubyiruko nta gushidikanya bazakenera mu minsi iri imbere.
Ubu indimi, kimwe nk’isomo wihitiyemo, rifatwa n’andi masomo wihitiramo ya STEM (siyansi, ikoranabuhanga, injiniyaringi n’imibare) mu nteganyanyigisho zo mu mashuri yigenga cyangwa ahandi.
Ubushakashatsi bwakozwe na Komisiyo y’Ubwongereza ku byerekeye akazi n’ubumenyi mu 2014, bwasanze ko impamvu abakoresha bagorwa no kubona abajya mu myanya y’akaziz, 17 ku ijana byaterwaga no kutagira ubumenyi buhagije mu ndimi.
Bityo, ubumenyi mu ndimi biru kuba itegeko kugira ngo hategurwe urubyiruko mu mwuga wabo w’ahazaza.
Mu gihe imyanya y’akazi myinshi isaba ururimi, ubwo bumenyi ni ingenzi mu isi yabaye umudugudu.
Hatitawe ku mwuga uwo ari we wese yanyuramo, iyo yize ururimi rwa kabiri, aba afite amahirwe nyayo y’ahazaza he yo kugira ubumenyi bw’ubuzima bwe bwose nk’ubu.
Kubasha kuvugana n’abandi bantu mu buryo butaziguye bo mu bihugu by’amahanga bihita bituma uwo muntu uzi indi myinshi imbere y’abandi bahanganye ku isoko.
Hakurikijwe ubushakashatsi bwa YouGov bwakorewe ku bantu barenga 4 000 bakuze mu Bwongereza mu 2013, 75 ku ijana ntibabasha kuvuga ururimi rw’amahanga neza ku buryo bagirana ikiganiro, mu gihe Igifaransa ari rwo rurimi rwonyine rivugwa n’abantu bari ku ijanisha rirenga icumi, 15 ku ijana.
Ni yo mpamvu gushora imari mu kwigisha indimi ubu ari ingenzi ku bana bo muri iki gihe.
Kugira indimi nyinshi; by’umwihariko, izo mu bihugu bikiri mu nzira y’amajyambere, bituma abana bagira amahirwe menshi kurushaho yo kubona akazi k’ingirakamaro.
Muri Ekose, buri shuri riba ritandukanye bitewe n’indimi bigisha.
Amashuri menshi azibanda ku indimi z’ubu, mu gihe abandi bigisha indimi zifatwa ko ari ingenzi mu Bwongereza iyo harebwa umwaka wa 2020, nk’ikimandare cyangwa ikiyapani.
Icyaba gishishikaje umwana wawe cyose, buri gihe haba hari indimi uhitamo mu mashuri yigenga, aho abarimu bazigisha aba ari inzobere muri ayo masomo.
Amashuri yigenga yo muri Ekose yiyemeje kwigisha ku buryo bitegura abana no kubaha ubumenyi busabwa kugira ngo bagere ku ntego, uko ahazaza haba hameze kose.
Ntabwo bishobora kwanga muri iki gihe, mu bucuruzi mpuzamahanga, indimi zikomeza kuba ikintu cy’ingenzi ku hazaza h’igihugu, rero bigomba no kugaragara mu burezi.
Ni byo koko, indimi zigezweho zigomba gufatwa nk’"ubumenyi butuma hatangwa amakuru ku rwego mpuzamahanga.”
Amashuri yigenga akomeza gutanga aya mahitamo, uburyo butandukanye n’ubudashyikirwa ku rubyiruko rwo muri Ekose.
Ibyiza ni uko tugomba kubikora.
John Edward ni Umuyobozi mukuru w’Akanama k’amashuri yigenga muri Ekose
Ku Cyumweru, LeBron agiye gukinira umukino wa mbere ikipe ya Lakers i San Diego
Gutegereza biri hafi kurangira ubwo abafana bategereje kureba LeBron James atangira gukina umukino we wa mbere akinira ikipe ya Los Angeles Lakers.
Umutoza w’ikipe ya Lakers, Luke Walton, yatangaje ko James azakina mu mukino ubanziriza shampiyona uzaba ku Cyumweru aho bazacakirana n’ikipe ya Denver Nuggets i San Diego.
Ariko umubare w’iminota azakina ntabwo yari yemezwa.
"Izaba irenze iminota 48," byavuzwe na Walton ku rubuga rwemewe rw’ikipe ya Lakers".
Umunyamakuru w’ikipe ya Lakers, Mike Trudell, yanditse kuri Twitter ko James azakina iminota ibaze.
Nyuma y’imyitozo yabaye mu ntangiriro z’iki cyumweru, James yabajijwe ku byerekeye gahunda ze afitiye ikipe ya Lakers" ingengabihe y’imikino ibanziriza shampiyona igera kuri itandatu.
Ati: "Sinkeneye gukina imikino ibanziriza shampiyona kuri uru rwego ngezeho mu mwuga wanjye kugira ngo nitegure."
Igihe ibikorwa byo kwiyamamaza kwa Trump muri West Virginia, kuri shene ya YouTube
Perezida Donald Trump yatanyiye kwiyamamaza hari umuyaga mwinshi iri joro muri Wheeling, West Virginia.
Ni cyo gikorwa cyo kwiyamamaza cya mbere cya Trump mu bikorwa bitanu biteganyijwe mu cyumweru gitaha, harimo kugenda ahagarara ahantu hazwi harimo Tennessee na Mississippi.
Mu gihe amatora yo kwemeza atari yakorwa ku wo yahisemo ngo ajye mu mwanya w’Umukuru w’Urukiko rw’Ikirenga, Trump agamije gushakisha ubufasha ku matora yo mu gihembwe hagati yegereje kuva aho Abarepubulikani bafite ibyago byo kudakomeza kugenzura Kongere igihe amatora azaba mu Ugushyingo.
Ni ryari kwiyamamaza kwa Trump muri West Virginia biri bube iri joro ndetse ni gute byareberwa kuri interineti?
Kwiyamamaza kwa Trump muri Wheeling, muri West Virginia biteganyijwe kuba saa 7 z’ijoro ku isaha ya ET, ku wa Gatandatu, tariki ya 29 Nzeli 2018.
Ushobora kureba kwiyamamaza kwa Trump muri West Virginia kuri interineti ku ihuza ry’ibiri kuba hakoreshejwe interineti kuri YouTube.
Birashoboka ko Trump ari buvuge ku iburanisha ryo muri iki cyumweru ku byerekeye uwatanzwe ngo azabe Umukuru w’Urukiko rw’Ikirenga witwa Brett Kavanaugh, bikaba byaragiye bikomera kubera ibirego by’imyitwarire idahwitse ku byerekeye ibitsina aho amatora ya Sena yari yitezwe yo kumwemeza yabaye asubitswe bitewe ni uko FBI iri gukora iperereza.
Ariko icy’ibanze kigamijwe muri uku kwiyamamaza ni ugufasha Abarebupulikani guhangana n’amatora akomeye yo mu Ugushyingo kugira ngo rikomeze kugira imbaraga.
Bityo, abashinzwe kwiyamamaza kwa Perezida Trump bavuze ko ibyo bikorwa byo kwiyamamaza bitanu bizaba mu cyumweru gitaha bigamije "guha imbaraga abakorerabushake n’abarwanashyaka mu gihe Abarepubulikana bagerageza kurinda no kwakura umubare nyamwinshi bafite w’abasenateri n’abadepite," hakurikijwe ibitangazwa n’ikinyamakuru cya Reuters.
Umuvugizi w’ibikorwa byo kwiyamamaza bya Trump wifuje ko ikinyamakuru cya Reuters kimuvuga ati: "Kugenzura Kongere ni ibintu by’ingenzi cyane muri gahunda afite ku buryo perezida azakorera urugendo muri leta nyinshi zishoboka mu gihe tugana mu gihe kirimo ibikorwa byinshi byo kwiyamamaza."
Biteganyijwe ko ibikorwa byo kwiyamamaza bizabera ku kibuga cya Wesbanco Arena muri Wheeling, icyo gikorwa cyo kwiyamamaza gishobora kuzana abarwanashyaka baturutse muri "Ohio na Pennsylvania kandi bikanatangazwa n’ibinyamakuru byo muri Pittsburgh," hakurikijwe ibivugwa n’ikinyamakuru cya West Virginia Metro News.
Ku wa Gatandatu, azaba ari bwo bwa kabiri mu kwezi gushize Trump asuriye West Virginia, leta yatsinzemo amatora ku ijanisha rirenga 40 ry’amanota mu 2016.
Trump ari kugerageza gufasha umukandida w’umusenateri w’umurepubulikani wo muri West Virginia witwa Patrick Morrisey, uri inyuma mu majwi.
Simon Haeder, umuhanga mu bya politiki wo muri Kaminuza ya West Virginia University, aganira n’ikinyamakuru cya Reuters: "Ntabwo ari ikimenyetso cyiza kuri Morrisey kuba perezida agomba kuza kugira ngo amufashe kongera amajwi."
Irushanwa rya Ryder Cup ryo mu 2018: Ikipe y’Amerika yerekana imbaraga zo guhangana kugira ngo ikomeze igire icyizere cyo kujya mu mikino yo ku Cyumweru
Nyuma y’umwaka w’imikino, ku wa Gatandatu nyuma ya saa sita imikino y’amarushanwa ya gorufe ashobora kuba ari yo irushanwa rya Ryder ryari rikeneye.
Amahirwe ahari ni uko hari igitekerezo cy’imikinire cyazanywe ariko ni kimwe mu byo abakiriya bizera kandi bitar icyane kurusha iby’amarushanwa ameze nkaya.
Rero ni he twavuga ko imbaraga ziri?
Jordan Spieth yatemberaga ku gicamunsi yagize ati: "Bari bayoboye n’amanota atandatu none ubu ni ane, rero ndakeka ko turi kugenda tugaragaza imbaraga."
Birumvikana ko Uburayi bufite amahirwe, buri imbere n’amanota ane mu gihe hari indi mikino cumi n’ibiri igomba gukinwa.
Abanyamerika nk’uko Spieth abivuga, bumva ko bafite umuyaga mwinshi ubangamira amato yabo kandi bafite ibyinshi byo guterwamo ishyaka, byibuze bitari imimerere ya Spieth na Justin Thomas bakinanye umunsi wose kandi buri wese abona amanota atatu muri ane.
Spieth yagiye atsinda cyane avuye aho umupira uteretse awutera mu kobo kabugenewe kandi ari kuba intangarugero.
Abo bari kwishimira itsinda n’urusaku rwinshi barushijeho ubwo yateye agapira kakagwa mu mwobo, atsindira amanota y’ingenzi kugira ngo umukino ungane ubwo we na Thomas bari inyuma n’amanota abiri nyuma y’imikino ibiri.
Umupira yatsinze watumye batsinda umukino kuri 15 na wo wavugirijwe induru z’ibyishimo, uburyo wakwizera ko yizera ko ikipe y’Amerika itarimo.
Spieth ati: "Ugomba kwinjira mu mizi no guhangayikishwa n’umukino wawe ubwawe."
Ni byo buri umwe muri abo bakinnyi asigaranye.
Imyobo 18 yo gushyiramo agapira.
Abakinnyi bonyine barusha amanota Spieth na Thomas mu minsi ibiri ishizwe ni Francesco Molinari na Tommy Fleetwood, bakaba ari abakinnyi bazwie cyane mu Irushanwa rya Ryder Cup.
Amahire y’Uburayi arahari ariko birashoboka ko yatsinda imikino ine kuri ine ntihagire ikigenda nabi.
"Moliwood" ni bo bonyine muri babiri batarabashije gutera umupira ku wa Gatandatu nyuma ya saa sita, ariko bananze ko batera agapira mu mwobo ku wa Gatandatu mu gitondo, ku wa Gatanu nimugoroba ndetse no mu gice cya kabiri cy’umukino wo gutera umupira mu twobo cumi n’umunani ku wa Gatanu mu gitondo.
Iyo mikinire n’uburyo ingufu zabo zagendagamo yaba ari ukujya no kuva mu itsinda ryari ribashagaye bishimangira ko ari bo bakinnyi umuntu akwiye guhangana na bo ku Cyumweru kandi hashobora kuba hari abakinnyi bazwi cyane kurushaho kugira ngo batume Uburayi bubona itsinzi mu gihe izuba riraba rirengera kuri Le Golf National kurusha Fleetwood cyangwa Molinari.
Ibyiza ni uko byombi byakorerwa ku myobo itandukanye.
Kuvuga ku nsinzi y’Uburayi byaba bikozwe imburagihe.
Bubba Watson na Webb Simpson bakoreye akazi Sergio Garcia, intwari y’umupira w’amaguru wa mugtiondo, ubwo yahuzwaga na Alex Noren.
Gutera agapira n’imipira ibiri ijya mu icyenda yatumye umwesipanyoro n’umunyasuwede batera umupira ariko ntiwigera aho wuririra umanukira mu kobo.
Ku Cyumweru, nta muntu uba uhari wo kugufasha gukura umupira mu kobo wateyemo.
Imikino ya gorufe yo gutera imipira ine inakinwa n’abakinnyi bane irashimishije kureba uyegereye kubera ikiganiro kiba kiri hagati y’abakinnyi bahujwe ari babari, inama batanga, inama badatanga n’uburyo ndetse ni uko ingamba zishobora guhinduka mu kanya nk’ako guhumbya.
Uburayi bwakinnye neza nk’ikipe kugeza ubu kandi buyoboye n’amanota ahagije ku munsi wa nyuma ariko iyi mikino ikinwa n’abakinnyi bane na yo garagaje ko ikipe y’Amerika ifite imbaraga zo kurwanira amanota; by’umwihariko, kuri za leta zagendaga zishidikanywaho.
Uburayi buyoboye n’amanota 10-6 ku munsi wa nyuma w’irushanwa rya Ryder Cup
Uburayi bufite amahirwe meza ku munsi wa nyuma y’irushanwa rya Ryder Cup nyuma y’aho bugaragariye ku wa Gatandatu mu mikino irimo gutera udupira tune aho iyoboye n’ibitego 10-6 yatsinze Amerika.
Abakinnyi beza cyane ari bo Tommy Fleetwood na Francesco Molinari ni bo bayoboye umukino batsinda inshuro ebyiri umukinnyi uri kugorwa n’umukino witwa Tiger Woods kugira ngo abe ari bo biharira amanota yo mu irushanwa rya Le Golf National agera kuri ane.
Uruhande rw’Uburayi rwa Thomas Bjorn, ruharanira kugumana igikombe rwatsinzwe na Hazeltine hashize imyaka ibiri, rwarushije uruhande rw’Amerika rutari kwitwara neza mu mikino ya mugitondo yo gutera udupira tune, barutsinda ku manota 3-1.
Ikipe y’Amerika yagaragaje kwirwanaho mu mikino ya bane, itsindamo imikino ibiri, ariko ntabwo byababujije gutsindwa.
Uruhande rwa Jim Furyk rukeneye amanota umunani mu mukino wo gutera imipira 12 wo ku Cyumweru kugira ngo igumane igikombe.
Fleetwood ni we mukinnyi w’umunyaburayi wa mbere ugitangira gukina watsindiye amanota ane yikurikiranya mu gihe we na Molinari, bahawe akazina ka "Molliwood" nyuma y’icyumweru gishimishize aho ari bo bakinnyi babiri bonyine batsindiye amanota ane mu mikino ine ibanza mu mateka y’irushanwa rya Ryder Cup.
Kuba yaratsinze Woods na Patrick Reed mu mukino wa bane ibyo batumye atsinda neza Woods utari umeze neza n’umunyamwerika ugitangira gukina witwa Bryson Dechambeau aho babonye amanota arenga 5&4.
Woods, wakinnye imikino ibiri ku wa Gatandatu, yagaragaje imikinire yo ku rwego rwo hejuru ariko ubu yatsinzwe imikino 19 mu mikino 29 yakinnye mu mikino yo gutera udupira tune n’imikino y’abakinnyi bane na barindwi yikurikiranyije.
Justin Rose, ntiyakinnye mu mikino yo gutera udupira tune ya mugitondo, yasubiranye n’uwo bakinanaga witwa Henrik Stenson mu mukino wa bane ubwo batsindwaga 2&1 na Dustin Johnson na Brooks Koepka, bakaba umwe ari ku mwanya wa mbere n’uwa gatatu ku rwego rw’isi.
Uburayi ntabwo bwakinnyi uko bwari busanzwe bukina ku buryo bushimishije, wari umunsi w’umuyaga waturukaga mu majyepfo y’uburengerazuba bwa Paris.
Uwekuganye ibikombe bitatu bikomeye witwa Jordan Spieth na Justin Thomas bashyizweho umwitangirizwa ku banyamerika w’amanota abiri ku wa Gatandatu.
Batsinze kuri 2&1 barusha abesipanyoro ari bo Jon Rahm na Ian Poulter mu mukino wo gutera udupira tune maze baza kugaruka nyuma batsinda Poulter na Rory McIlroy 4&3 mu mukino wa bane nyuma yo gutsindwa ku myobo ibiri ya mbere ibanza.
Kabiri mu mateka y’irushanwa rya Ryder Cup ni byo ikipe yari yatsinzwe amanota ane yigaranzuye iyayitsinze igera mu mikino ihuza umukinnyi umwe umwe, nubwo abafite igikombe bo ku ruhande rwa Furyk bakeneye kunganya gusa kugira ngo bagume igikombe.
Nyuma yo kuba abakabiri beza mu minsi ibiri, ariko noneho ku Cyumweru umukino bazakina bazihorera nubwo uzaba ubarenze.
Koreya ya ruguru ivuga ko 'nta buryo' bwo kwambura ibisasu bya kirimbuzi igihugu kimwe nta cyizere
Ku wa Gatandatu, Minisitiri w’ububanyi n’amahanga wa Koreya ya ruguru yabwiye Umuryango w’abibumbye ko gukomeza gushyiraho ibihano bituma kutizerana birushaho gukomera kuri Amerika kandi ko nta buryo igihugu gishobora kureka umugambi wacyo wo gukora ibisasu kirimbuzi ari cyo cyonyine igihe bimeze bityo.
Ri Yong Ho yabwiye abayobozi bo ku rwego rw’igihugu mu Nteko Rusange ngarukamwaka ko "hafashwe ingamba zikwiye" mu mwaka ushize, nko guhagarika igerageza ry’ibisasu kirimbuzi, gusenya ahageragerezwa ibisasu kirimbuzi no kwizeza ko nta gukomeza gukora ibisasu kirimbuzi n’ikoranabuhanga ry’ibisasu kirimbuzi.
Ati: "Icyakora, ntabwo tubona igisubizo gikwiye kiri gutangwa n’Amerika."
"Nta cyizere kuri Amerika ko hazabaho ubwizerane mu by’umutekano w’ibihugu byacu kandi niba bimeze gutyo nta buryo dushobora nk’igihugu kimwe kubanza kureka gukora ibisasu kirimbuzi."
Mu gihe Ri yasubiyemo ibirego bisanzwe bya Koreya ya ruguru ku byerekekeye kwinganira kwa leta ya Washington ku buryo buri mu "byiciro" bwo kureka gukora ibisasu kirimbuzi aho Koreya ya ruguru ishobora kugenga ihembwe mu gihe igenda itera intambwe, amagambo yavuze asa nk’aho afite agaciro nubwo atigeze ahakana ko leta ya Pyongyang ishobora kureka gukora intwaro kirimbuzi nk’uko yabikoze mbere.
Ri yagendeye magambo yavuzwe n’abaperezida bombi ari bo Kim Jong Un na Donald Trump mu nama ya mbere yahuje perezida uri ku butegetsi muri Amerika na perezida wa Koreya ya ruguru i Singapuru tariki ya 12 Kamena, ubwo Kim yizezaga ko ari gukora kugira ngo "areke gukorera ibisasu kirimbuzi mu mwigimbakirwa wa Koreya" mu gihe Trump yijeje ko azarinda umutekano wa Koreya ya ruguru.
Koreya ya ruguru yashakaga uko irangiza intambara mu buryo buzwi ya Koreya yo mu 1950-53, ariko Amerika yavuze ko Pyongyang igomba kubanza kureka gukora ibisasu kirimbuzi.
Leta Washington yanze kwemera ko igabanya ibihano bikomeye byo ku rwego mpuzamahanga yafatiye Koreya ya ruguru.
Ri ati: "Amerika ikomeza gutsimbarara ko "tubanza kureka gukora ibisasu kirimbuzi" maze bikongera urwego rw’igitutu hashyirwaho ibihano kugira ngo bagere ku ntego yabo bakoresheje ingufu, nubwo banga ko "hatangazwa irangira ry’intambara.""
"Igitekerezo cy’uko ibihano bishobora gutuma dushyirwa ku mavi ni inzozi zidashoboka ku baturage batwirengagiza.
Ariko ikibazo ni uko ibihano bikomeje gushyirwaho bituma turushaho kubatera icyizere."
Ri ntacyo yigeze itangaza kuri gahunda z’inama ya kabiri izahuza Kim na Trump aho perezida w’Amerika yabigarutseho mu nama y’Umuryango w’abibumbye mu ntangiriro z’icyumweru.
Ahubwo minisitiri yagaragaje inama eshatu hagati ya Kim na perezida wa Korea y’epfo, Moon Jae-in, mu mezi atanu ashize maze agira ati: "Iya igihugu birebwa n’iki kibazo cyo kureka gukora ibisasu kirimbuzi cyari Koreya y’epfo atari Amerika, kureka gukora ibisasu kirimbuzi by’umwigimbakirwa wa Koreya ntabwo byari kuba byarahagaze."
Kandi, ijwi ry’ijambo rya Ri ryari ritandukanye ku buryo butangaje n’iry’umwaka utaha, ubwo yarari mu Nteko rusange y’Umuryango w’abibumbye avuga ko gushaka kurasa Amerika hakoreshejwe rokete za Koreya byashooboka nyuma y’aho "Bwana Perezida wifuza ikibi" Trump yise Kim "umugabo ukora ibisasu" ufite gahunda yo kwiyahura.
Uyu mwaka mu nama y’Umuryango w’abibumbye, Trump, aho mu mwaka ushize yateye ubwoba bwo "gusenya burundu" Koreya ya ruguru, yashimagije Kim ku bw’umurava we wo gutera intambwe yo kureka gukora ibisasu, ariko yavuze ko hari byinshi bigikeneye gukorwa ndetse n’ibihano bigumishijweho kugeza Koreya ya ruguru iretse gukora ibisasu.
Ku wa Gatatu, Trump yavuze ko adafitei gihe ibyo yabikoramo, avuga ko "N’iyo byafata imyaka ibiri, itatu cyangwa amezi atatu; ntacyo bitwaye."
Ubushinwa n’Uburusiya bajya impaka n’Akanama k’Umuryango w’abibumbye gashinzwe umutekano ko kagomba kugororera leta ya Pyongyang ku bw’intambwe yatewe.
Icyakora, Umunyamabanga wa leta y’Amerika, Mike Pompeo, ku wa Kane yabwiye Akanama gashinzwe umutekano ko: "Kongerera ingufu ibihano bitangwa n’Akanama gashinzwe umutekano bigomba gukomeza ku buryo bukomeye kandi nta kunanirwa kugeza hagaragajwe ko ibisasu kirimbuzi byakuweho ku buryo busesuye, ndakuka kandi bwasuzumwe."
Akanama gashinzwe umutekano katoye nta n’umwe uvuyemo kongerera ibihano Koreya ya ruguru guhera mu 2006 kugira ngo habuze uburyo bwo gutera inkunga leta ya Pyongyang mu mugambi wayo wo gukora ibisasu kirimbuzi n’ibisasu bya rokete.
Pompeo yahuye na Ri ku nama yo ku ruhande yabaye mu gihe habaga inama y’Inteko rusange y’Umuryango w’abibumbye kandi nyuma y’aho yavuze ko azongera gusura Pyongyang ukwezi gutaha kugira ngo hategurwe inama ya kabiri.
Pompeo amaze gusura Koreya ya ruguru inshuro eshatu uyu mwaka, ariko uruzinduko aheruka kuhagirira ntirwagenze neza.
Yavuye i Pyongyang muri Nyakanga avuga ko hari intambwe yatewe, aho nyuma y’amasaha make Koreya ya ruguru yanyomoje ibyo yavuze aho yatangaje ko "ibyo asaba bimeze nk’iby’agatsiko k’amabandi."
Koreya ya ruguru yatanze icyizere mu nama na Moon ko uku kwezi izasenya ahakorerwa za misire ndetse n’inzu zikorerwamo ibisasu bya kirimbuzi igihe Amerika na yo "yafata ingamba zimeze kimwe."
Yavuze ko Kim yamubwiye ko "ingamba zimeze kimwe" yifuzaga ko zifatwa ari izo kwizezwa umutekano hakurikijwe isezerano ryatanzwe na Trump i Singapuru kandi akaba akomeje atuma umubano na leta ya Washington usubira kumera neza.
Abanyeshuri biga muri kaminuza ya Harvard biga amasomo yo kuruhuka bihagije
Isomo rishya ryazanywe na kaminuza ya Harvard University uyu mwaka ryatumye abanyeshuri bose batari barangiza icyiciro cya kabiri cya kaminuza babona ibitotsi byinshi kugira ngo barwanye umuco wa kigabo uri kugenda ukura wo kwiga banywye kafeyine bakiga 'ijoro ryose.'
Ukora muri kaminuza yabonye ko abanyeshuri bari ku mwanya wa mbere muri kaminuza imwe akenshi baba badafite amakuru y’iby’ibanze ku byerekeye uko bakwiyitaho ubwabo.
Charles Czeisler, umwarimu w’ubuganga bukoresha ibitotsi mu ishami ry’ubuvuzi rya kaminuza ya Harvard Medical School n’inzobere mu bitaro bya Brigham and Women's Hospital, yateguye isomo, aho yizera ko ari ryo rya mbere rifite iyo mitegurire muri Amerika.
Yagize igitekerezo cyo gutangiza isomo nyuma yo gutanga ikiganiro ku ngaruka zo kudasinzira neza bigira ku myigire.
'Icyo kiganiro kirangiye, umukobwa umwe yaranyegereye maze arambwira ati: 'Kubera iki ari njye uri bubibwirwa nonaha, ngeze mu mwaka wa nyuma wa kaminuza y’icyiciro cya kabiri?'
Avuga ko nta muntu n’umwe wigeze umubwira akamaro ko gusinzira, bikaba byarantangaje,' uko ni ko yabwiye ikinyamakuru cya The Telegraph.
Isomo, ryatangiye gutangwa bwa mbere, risobanurirwa abanyeshuri iby’ibanze by’uko kuryama neza bifasha abanyeshuri n’abakinnyi kwitwara neza, ndetse bikananoza imibereho myiza muri rusange.
Paul Barreira, porofeseri mu by’ubuzima bwo mu mutwe mu Ishami ry’ubuvuzi rya kaminuza ya Harvard n’umuyobozi mukuru wa kaminuza ushinzwe serivisi z’ubuzima, yavuze ko kaminuza yahisemo kuzana iryo somo nyuma y’aho abanyeshuri batasinziraga mu cyumweru.
Isomo rimara isaha ririmo imikoro yo gushyikirana itandukanye.
Mu gice kimwe hari ishusho y’icyumba cyo kuraramo, aho abanyeshuri bakanda ku bikombe by’ikawa, amarido, inkweto za siporo n’ibitabo maze bakabwirwa igaruka za kafeyine n’urumuri ni uko imikinire igirwaho ingaruka no kudasinzira neza ndetse n’akamaro ko kugira umuco mwiza wo gusinzirira igihe.
Mu kindi gice, abitabiriye isomo batwirwa uko kudasinzira by’igihe kirekire bishobora kongera ibyago byo kurwara indwara y’umutima, gucika k’udutsi tw’ubwonko, kugira agahinda gakabije no kurwara kanseri.
Ikarita ya kaminuza, ifite udushushondanga tugaragaza amakuru, ishishikariza abitabiriye isomo gutekereza ku byerekeye ibyo bakora ku buryo buhoraho.
'Turabizi ko bitahita bihindura imyitwarire y’abanyeshuri.
Porofeseri Czeisler ati: “Ariko twizera ko bafite uburenganzira bwo kumenya; nk’uko ufite uburenganzira bwo kumenya ingaruka ku buzima zo guhitamo kunywa itabi.'
Ati: “Haracyari umuco wo kwiyemeza ku biga 'nijoro',” yongeraho ko ikoranabuhanga rigezweho n’igitutu kigenda cyiyongera ku banyeshuri bivuze ko kubura ibitotsi ari ikibazo kigenda cyiyongera.
Ati: “Gukora ku buryo ubona ibitotsi bihagije, byiza, bigomba kuba 'intwaro y’ibanga' ku banyeshuri yo kurwanya siteresi, umuaniro n’umuhangayiko”; ndetse no kwirinda kwiyongera ibiro, kuko kubura ibitotsi bishyira ubwonko mu buryo bwo kwicwa n’inzara, bigatuma buhora bushonje.
Raymond So, umunyeshuri w’imyaka 19 wo muri California wiga ubutabir n’imiterere y’imibiri y’ibinyabuzima, yafashije porofeseri Czeisler gutegura isomo, kuko yari yarize amasomo ye umwaka ushize mu mwaka wa mbere yari agiye kwiga muri Harvard.
Yavuze ko isomo ryafunguye amaso ye maze rituma ashaka uko ryakwigishwa muri kaminuza yose.
Yizera ko intambwe ikurikira, ari ugusaba ko abanyeshuri barangije icyiciro cya kabiri cya kaminuza barangiza gahunda zimwe mbere yo kujya mu bigo bihatanirwamo akazi.
Porofeseri Czeisler atanga inama y’uko abanyeshuri bagomba gutekereza gushyiraho integuza y’igihe bagira mu buriri ndetse n’igihe babyukira n’igihe bamenya ibintu byabangiza nk’'urumuri rw’ubururu rutangwa na ekara z’ibikoresho by’ikoranabuhanga n’urumuri rwa LED, byatuma uko uryamana ni uko ubyuka biva ku murongo, bigatuma ugira ibibazo byo gusinzira.
Livingston 1 - 0 Rangers: Igitego cya Menga cyashegeshe abakinnyi batozwa na Gerrard
Rangers yongeye gukorwa mu jisho aho igitego cya Dolly Menga cyatsinzwe ikipe ya Steven Gerrard igitego 1-0 kuri Livingston.
Uruhande rwa Ibrox rwasaga nk’aho rugiye gutsinda bwa mbere kuva rwatsindwa muri Gashyantare na St Johnstone ibitego 4-1, ariko ikipe ya Gary Holt yatsinze ikipe ya Gerrard bwa kabiri mu mikino 18 nk’umuyobozi kugira ngo ikipe ye isigare inyuma ho amanota muri Shampiyona ya Ladbrokes inyuma y’ikipe ya Hearts.
Menga yatsinze igitego mu minota irindwi mbere y’uko igice cya mbere kirangira aho abakinnyi ba Rangers basga ntabo batari bubashe kucyishyura.
Mu gihe ubu Rangers yamanutse ikajya ku mwana wa gatandatu, Livingston yazamutse ijya ku mwanya wa gatatu kandi ikaba iri inyuma ya Hibernian ku kinyuranyo cy’ibitego.
Kandi hashobora kuba hari ibindi bibazo bitegereje Rangers nyuma y’aho umusifuzi wo ku ruhande, Calum Spence, yavuwe igikomere cyo mu mutwe nyuma y’aho ikintu gisa n’aho cyamukubise kivuye kure.
Gerrard yakoze impinduka umunani mu ikipe ye ayo yatsinze ikipe ya Ayr kugira ngo ijye mu mikino ya kimwe cya kabiri cy’irushanwa rya red Cup.
Ku rundi ruhande, Holt, yajyanye abakinnyi 11 ba Livi bakuye inota ku ikipe ya Hearts mu cyumweru gishize kandi yakabaye yarashimishijwe n’uko ikipe ye yanize abo bahanganye mu mukino wose.
Rangers ishoboroa kuba yihariye cyane umupira ariko Livingston yabyaje umusaruro umupira muke bagiye babona.
Bakabaye batsinze mu minota mike ubwo umupira wa mbere waterwaga na Menga watewe Scott Pittman ugana mu izamu rya Allan McGregor ariko umukinnyi wo hagati amahirwe yari abonye umupira awutera hanze.
Umupira wa kufura watewe ugana mu izamu na Keaghan Jacobs wasanze umunyezamu, Craig Halkett, ariko umukinnyi ukina inyuma witwa Alan Lithgow yatumye umupira ugana hanze y’izamu.
Rangers yayoboye umukino ariko yasaga nk’aho yakwiye kugira byinshi ikora kurusha kugira icyizere hakurikijwe uko bakinaga mu gice cya gatatu cya nyuma.
Nta gushidikanya ko Alfredo Morelos yumvaga ko yaragakwiye kuba yahawe penaliti ku munota wa mirongo irindwi na gatanu ubwo we na Steven Lawless bagonganaga ariko umusifuzi, Steven Thomson, akaba yanze guha agaciro ibyo umunyakorombiya yaregeraga.
Rangers yabashije gutera amashoti abiri gusa agana mu izamu mu gice cya mbere ariko uwahoze ari umunyezamu w’ikipe ya Ibrox, Liam Kelly, ntabwo yakanzwe n’umupira w’umutwe watewe na Lassana Coulibaly ndetse n’ishoti ridakanganye rya Ovie Ejaria.
Mu gihe igitego cya mbere cya Livi cyatsinzwe ku munota wa 34 gishobora kuba cyaturutse kuri atake, nta n’umwe wahakana ko batari bakwiye kugitsinda ukanakurikije uko cyateguwe.
Na none Rangers yananiwe kugarura umupira w’umuterekano watewe na Jacobs.
Scott Arfield ntacyo yigeze akora ku mupira watewe na Declan Gallagher awuhereza Scott Robinson, utarigeze icyo akora kugira ngo ahagarike umupira winjijwe mu buryo bworoshye mu izamu na Menga.
Gerrard yagize icyo akora mu kiruhuko ubwo yahinduranyaga agakuramo Coulibaly agashyiramo Ryan Kent, ibyo bikaba byari bigiye gutanga umusaruro w’ako kanya ubwo umukinnyi w’imbere ku ruhande yahawe umupira Morelos ariko Kelly yiruka neza maze ahagarika umupira watewe.
Ariko Livingston yakomeje kunanira ikipe yayisuye gukina umupira isanzwe ikina, aho Lithgow na Halkett bagiye batera imipira miremire ubutitsa.
Uruhande rwa Holt rwakabaye rwatsinze ikindi gitego mu minota ya nyuma ariko McGregor yihagaze neza abuza Jacobs gutera umupira ubwo Lithgow yateraga umupira w’umutwe ukajya hanze.
Rangers yasimbuje Glenn Middleton waje kuvuga ko hagakwiye gutangwa penaliti aho yanganye na Jacobs ariko na none umusifuzi Thomson yabyirengagije.
Almanac: Uwahimbye icyuma cya Geiger Counter
Ndetse na paji yacu yo mu kinyamakuru cyitwa "Sunday Morning" Almanac: Tariki ya 30 Nzeli 1882, hashize iminsi 136 uyu munsi ndetse TURACYAYIBARA... umunsi umunyabugenge w’ahazaza witwa Johannes Wilhelm "Hans" Geiger yavukiye mu Budage.
Geiger yakoze uburyo bwo gutahura no gupima ukurekurwa k’uduce tw’ubumara twakozwe, ubwo buryo yahimbye bwatumye hakorwa igikoresho cyizwi nka Geiger Counter.
Icyo cyuma kikaba cyarashingiweho na siyansi guhera ubwo, icyuma kizwi nka Geiger Counter cyanabaye icyuma gishingirwaho mu by’imyidagaduro, nko muri filime yo mu 1950 yitwa "Bells of Coronado," irimo abakinnyi b’abanyasiyansi b’abacanshuro ari bo Roy Rogers na Dale Evans:
Umugabo: "Icyo gikoresho ni ikihe?"
Rogers: "Ni icyuma cyitwa Geiger Counter, gikoreshwa mu kumenya amabuye y’agaciro arimo uduce tw’ubumara nka iraniyumu.
Iyo wampaye izi ekuteri, ushobora kumva neza ihindagurika rya atome zirekurwa n’uduce tw’ubumara turi muri ayo mabuye y’agaciro."
Evans: "Twavuga ko, zitangiye gusimbagurika!"
"Hans" Geiger yapfuye mu 1945, habura iminsi mike ngo yizihize isabukuru y’amavuko ya 63.
Ariko icyuma yavumbuye cyamwitiriwe cyo kiracyariho.
Urukingo rwa kanseri rushya rushobora kwigisha ubudahangarwa bw’umubiri 'kubona' uturemangingo fatizo tubi
Urukingo rwa kanseri rushya rushobora kwigisha ubudahangarwa bw’umubiri 'kubona' uturemangingo fatizo tubi maze rukatwica
Urukingo rwigisha ubudahangarwa bw’umubiri kugira ngo bumenye uturemangingo fatizo tubi nka kimwe mu bigize uburyo bwo kuvura
Ubwo buryo burimo gukura uturemaningo fatizo dufasha mu gutuma umubiri ugira ubudahangarwa ku murwayi, maze tugahindurirwa muri laburatwari
Ubwo zishobora 'kubona' poroteyine isanzwe igaragara muri kanseri nyinshi maze zikongera guterwa mu mubiri
Urukingo ruri gukorerwaho igerageza ruri kugaragaza ibisubizo bitanga icyizere ku barwayi barwaye kanseri zitandukanye.
Umugore umwe yavuwe hakoreshejwe urukingo, rukaba rwigisha ubudahangarwa bw’umubiri kumenya uturamangingo fatizo tubi, rwatumye kanseri y’umurerantanga we ikira nyuma y’amezi 18.
Uburyo bukoreshwa burimo gukura uturemangingo fatizo mu murwayi, tugahindurirwa muri laburatwari kugira ngo tubashe "kubona" poroteyine igaragara muri kanseri nyinshi yitwa HER2 maze utwo turemangingo fatizo tukongera tugaterwa mu mubiri.
Porofeseri Jay Berzofsky, wo mu Kigo cy’Amerika gishinzwe kurwanya kanseri cyitwa US National Cancer Institute muri Bethesda, Maryland, ati: "Ibisubizo twabonye bigaragaza ko dufite urukingo rutanga icyizere cyane."
Porofeseri Berzofsky asobanura ko HER2 "ituma amoko menshi ya kanseri akura," harimo kanseri y’ibere, y’umurerantanga, y’ibihaha n’urura runini.
Uburyo bumwe bwo gukura uturemangingo tw’ubudahangarwa bw’umubiri mu murwayi no "kwigisha" utwo turemangingo tw’umubiri kwibasira uturemaningo fatizo twa kanseri bwakoreshejwe mu kuvura kanseri y’amaraso.
Kanye West yavuze amagambo ashimagiza abashyigikiye Trump, yambaye ingofero yanditseho MAGA, nyuma yo kugaragara mu kiganiro cya SNL.
Ntibyagenze neza
Kanye West yavugirijwe induru muri sitidiyo mu kiganiro cya Saturday Night Live nyuma y’imiririmbire idashamaje ayo yashimagijemo Perezida w’Amerika, Donald Trump, maze avuga ko aziyamamaza mu mataro ya perezida yo mu 2020.
Nyuma yo kuririmba indirimbo ye ya gatatu y’iryo joro, yahamagaye Ghost Town aho yari yambaye ingefero Make America Great, maze yibasira abademokarate kandi yongera kuvuga ko ashyigikiye Trump.
"Inshuro nyinshi cyane mvuga ku muzungu, bagira bati: "Ni gute ushobora gukunda Trump, sakora irondaruhu?"
Ati: “Ni ukuvuga ngo niba mpangayikishijwe n’irondaruhu, nakabaye naravuye muri Amerika kera cyane."
Ikiganiro cya SNL cyatangiye harimo umukino wo gusetsa harimo kunenga ukinwamo n’umukinnyi w’ikirangirire muri Hollywood witwa Matt Damon aho yasetse ubuhamya bwa Brett Kavanaugh mbere y’uko Komite ya Sena ishinzwe ubutabera igira icyo ikora ku kirego cyo cyatanzwe na Christine Blasey Ford ku byerekeye gusagarirwa ku gitsina.
Nubwo bitatangajwe mu binyamakuru, amashusho y’amagambo yavuzwen a West yashyizwe ku mbuga mpuzambaga n’umunyarwenya witwa Chris Rock.
Ntabwo bigaragara neza niba Rock yari agamije kunenga West hakurikijwe ibyo yashyize ku rubuga.
Kandi, West yijujutiye kuba abareba ikiganiro baravuze amagambo menshi inyuma ya podiyumu ku ngofero yari yambaye.
"Baransagariye inyuma ya podiyumu.
Baravuze ngo: 'Ntujye kuri podiyumu wambaye iyo ngofero'
Baransagariye!
Ati: “Maze bavuga ko ntaho mpagaze," hakurikijwe ibyavuzwe n’ikinyamakuru cya Washington Examiner.
West akomeza agira ati: "Murashaka kubona ko ntaho mpagaze?" avuga ko ari "bwambare ingofero ya supamani, kubera ko bisobanuye ko utambwira icyo ngomba gukora. Murifuza ko isi itera imbere?
Muzagerageze gukundana."
Amagambo yavuze yatumye avugirizwa induru byibuze inshuro zigera kuri ebyiri mu bari bakurikiye ikiganiro n’abo mu kiganiro cya SNL basa nk’aho bakojejwe isoni nk’uko bitangazwa n’ikinyamakuru cya Variety, aho umuntu umwe yabwiye icyo kinyamakuru ko: "Sitidiyo yose yaguye mu kantu."
West yazanywe bwa nyuma nk’uwasimbuye umuhanzikazi Ariana Grande, aho uwahoze ari umukunzi we, umuraperi Mac Miller yari amaze iminsi mike apfuye.
West yatangaje benshi mu miririmbire y’indirimbo ye yitwa I Love it, aho yari yambaye nk’icupa rya Perrier.
West yashyigikiwe n’umukuru w’itsinda rigendera ku matwara ya kera ryitwa TPUSA, Candace Turner wanditse kuri Twittera agira ati: "Umwe mu bantu bagaragaza ishyaka ryinshi: WAKOZE CYANE GUHAGARARIRA ABIFUZA IMPINDUKA."
Ariko umunyamakuru wakira ikiganiro witwa Karen Hunter yanditse kuri Twitter ko West ari "kugaragaza uwo ari we mu by’ukuri kandi ni byiza cyane."
"Ariko nahisemo KUTAGIRA uwo mpemba (ngura umuziki we cyangwa imyenda ye ngira ngo nteze imbere "ubuhanzi" bwe) nizera ko ari kwakira no gukwirakwiza ingengabitekerezo yangiza abaturage b’agace ntuyemo.
Yaribohoye.
Akomeza agira ati: “Natwe twaribohoye.”
Mbere y’igitaramo, umuraperi yatangaje kuri Twitter ko yahinduye izina rye, avuga ko kuri ubu "ari uwahoze azwi ku izina rya Kanye West."
Si we muhanzi wa mbere wahinduye izina, kandi akurikiye abandi babikoze bairmo Diddy, unazwi ku izina rya Puff Daddy, Puffy na P Diddy.
Umuraperi mugenzi we, Snoop Dogg yigeze gukoresha izina rya Snoop Lion ndetse n’umuhanzi w’icyamamare uherutse gupfa witwa Prince, yahinduye izina akajya akoresha ikimenyetso kandi uwo muhanzi yigeze kwitwa Prince.
Gushinja kugerageza kwica umuntu mu guterana ibyuma muri resitora ya Belfast
Umugabo w’imyaka 45 yashinjwe kuba yaragerageje kwica nyuma y’aho umugabo aterewe icyuma muri resitora mu burasirazuba bwa Belfast ku wa Gatanu.
Ibyo bibazo byavutse muri Ballyhackamore, nk’uko Polisi ibivuga.
Uregwa yitezweho kugezwa imbere y’Urukiko rw’ibanze rwa Belfast ku wa Mbere.
Ibyo ashinjwa bizasuzumwa n’Ibiro by’ubushinjacyaha.
Umukinnyi wa filime y’uruhererekane ya Game of Thrones witwa Kit Harington yamaganye imico mibi ya kibago
Kit Harington azwi kuba akina acanga inkota aho aba yitwa Jon Snow muri filime y’uruhererekane yo ku ngoma ya cyami ishingiye ku bitekerezo irimo imirwano myinshi ya televiziyo ya HBO yitwa Game of Thrones.
Ariko uwo mukinnyi, w’imyaka 31, yamaganye iby’ivangura rishingiye kuri iyo ntwari igaragaza imiterere ya kigabo, avuga ko ibyo akina bisobanuye ko ingimbi akenshi zumva zogomba kwikomeza kugira ngo zubahwe.
Avugana n’ikinyamakuru cya The Sunday Times Culture, Kit yavuze ko yizera ko 'hari ikitaragenze neza' maze yibaza uko ashobora gukemura ikibazo cy’imico mibi ya kigabo mu gihe hatangijwe inkundura yo guharanira uburenganzira bw’abagore izwi nka #Me.
Kit, uherutse gushyingiranwa n’umukinnyi bakinana muri filime y’uruhererekane ya Game of Thrones witwa Rose Leslie, nawe ufite imyaka 31, yemeye ko yumva 'afite imbaraga nyinshi' ku byerekeye gukemura ikibazo.
Ati: 'Numva ubwanjye numva mfite imbaraga nyinshi kuri ubu, nkibaza nti: “Ese ni ha haturutse imico mibi ya kigabo?,’
'Ni twigisha abagabo iyo bari gukura, ku bijyanye n’ibibazo turi kubona ubu ngubu?'
Kit yizera ko televiziyo ishobora kuba ibifitamo uruhare rumwe mu kwiyongera kw’imico mibi ya kigabo bitewe n’abakinnyi ba filime bagaragaza cyane imico mibi ya kigabo.
Akomeza agira ati: 'Ni iki umuntu avukana ndetse ni ikihe yigishwa?
Ni iki cyigishwa kuri televiziyo, kandi ni ikihe kigishirizwa ku muhanda, bigatuma ingimbi zumva ko zifite igice runaka gituma zihinduka abagabo?
Ndatekereza ko icyo ari ikibazo gikomeye cyane mu bihe turimo: Ni gute twabihindura?
Kubera ko bigaragara ko hari ikintu kitagenze neza ku rubyiruko rwacu.'
Mu kiganiro, yanemeye ko adashobora gukina filime z’uruhererekane zibanziriza cyangwa zikurikira iya Game of Thrones igihe iyo filime y’uruhererekane izaba irangiye muri iyi mpeshyi, avuga ko 'atagishaka ibyo kurwanira ku rugamba no kugendera ku mafarasi'.
Uhereye kuri November Kit azakina mu nkuru yongewe gukina ya Sam Shepard yitwa True West ikaba ari inkuru y’utunganya filime n’umuvandimwe we w’umujura.
Umukinnyi aherutse gutangaza ko abona ko guhura n’umugore we, Rose, ari cyo kintu cyiza cyavuye muri filime y’uruhererekane ya Game of Thrones.
Ati: 'Nahuye n’umugore wanjye turi gukina filime y’uruhererekane, bityo bimpa umuryango wanjye w’ahazaza n’ubuzima bwanjye bushya buhera ubwo.'
Rose yakinnye yitwa Ygritte, akaba yari uwakundwaga na Kit ukinwa na Jon Snow, muri filime y’uruhererekane ishingiye ku makabyankuru yahawe igihembo cya Emmy.
Bashyingiranywe muri Kamena 2018 ku butaka bw’inyubako y’umuryango wa Leslie muri Ekose.
Agakoko gatera sida/Sida: Ubushinwa buvuga ko habayeho izamuka ringana na 14% ry’ubwandu bushya
Ubushinwa bwatangaje ko habayeho ubwiyongere bwa 14% ku mibare y’abaturage babwo bafite agakoko gatera sida n’abarwaye sida.
Abantu barenga 820 000 baranduye mu gihugu nk’uko bitangazwa n’abayobozi b’inzego z’ubuzima.
Hafi abantu bashya 40 000 bavuzweho ko banduye mu gihembwe cya kabiri cya 2018 gusa.
Umubare munini w’abandura bashya bayanduye bitewe n’imibonano mpuzabitsinda, bikaba bitandukanye ni uko byari bimeze mu minsi yashize.
Ubusanzwe, agakoko gatera sida kandura ku buryo bwihuse mu bice bimwe na bimwe by’Ubushinwa bitewe no gutanga amaraso yanduye.
Ariko umubare w’abantu bandura agakoko gatera sida muri ubu buryo waragabanutse ukaba ugeze hafi kuri zeru, abayobozi b’inzego z’ubuzima mu Bushinwa babitangarije mu nama yabereye mu ntara ya Yunnan.
Icyakora umwaka ku wundi, umubare w’ababana n’agakoko ka sida n’abarwaye sida mu Bushinwa wiyongeraho abantu 100 000.
Ubwandu bw’agakoko ka sida binyuze mu mibonano mpuzabitsina oni ikibazo gikomeye ku bakora imibano mpuzabitsina bahuje ibitsina mu Bushinwa.
Gukora imibonano mpuzabitsina ku babihuje byaretswe kugirwa icyaha mu Bushinwa mu 1997, ariko ivangura rikorerwa abakora imibonano mpuzabitsinda babihuje rigenda ryiyongera.
Kubera ko igihugu kigendera ku mahame ya kera, ubushakashatsi bwagereranyije ko 70-90% by’abagabo bakorana imibonano mpuzabitsina n’abandi bagabo bagera aho bagashyingiranwa n’abagore.
Ubwandu bwinshi bw’iyo ndwara buturuka mu gukora imibonano mpuzabitsinda nta kwirinda ku buryo buhagije muri uwo mubano.
Kuva mu 2003, leta y’Ubushinwa yijeje ko hazaboneka ku buryo rusange imiti y’agakoko gatera sida nka kimwe mu bigize igikorwa cyo guhashya icyo kibazo.
Maxine Waters yahakanye iby’uko amakuru y’abasenateri bo mu ishyaka ry’abarepubulikani yatangajwe n’umwe mu bakozi, yamagana 'ibinyoma byateza ibibazo' no kuba 'hari gutegurwa umugambi mubisha'
Ku wa Gatandatu uhagarariye Amerika witwa Maxine Waters yamaganye ibirego by’uko umwe mu bakozi be yatangaje amakuru bwite y’abasenateri b’abarepubulikani kuri paji z’abanyamategeko ku rubuga rwa Wikipedia.
Umudemokarate wo muri Los Angeles yavuze ko ibyo bigero biri gutizwa umurindi n’abayobora ibiganiro n’imbuga "bishyigikiye cyane abarepubulikani."
Waters yavuze mu magambo yatangarije kuri Twitter avuga ko ari: "Ibimenyoma, ibinyoma, ibinyoma bibi cyane."
Amakuru yatangajwe bivugwa ko arimo aderesi zo mu rugo na nomero za telefone z’abasenateri b’Amerika Lindsey Graham wo muri South Carolina na Mike Lee na Orrin Hatch, bombi bo muri Utah.
Amakuru yagaragaye kuri interineti ku wa Kane, atangajwe n’umuntu utazwi muri Capitol Hill mu iburanisha ryakorwaga n’inteko y’abasenateri ku birego by’imyitwarire yerekeye igitsina idahwitse yaregwaga uwatanzweho kuzahagararira IUrukiko rw’ikirenga witwa Brett Kavanaugh.
Ayo makuru yagiye hanze bibaye nyuma y’aho abasenateri batatu bahase ibibazo Kavanaugh.
Hill atangaza ko: “Imbuga z’abakonserivateri nka Gateway Pundit na RedState zatangajwe ko aderesi ya IP igaragaza aho ibyo byatangajwe byaturutse bifite aho bihuriye n’ibiro bya Waters kandi bikaba byaratangaje amakuru k’umwe mu bakozi ba Waters.”
Watera akomeza avuga ko: "Ibi birego nta shingiro bifite kandi si ukuri na busa, ahubwo ni ibinyoma byambaye ubusa."
"Umwe mu bakozi banjye, aho umwirondoro we, amakuru bwite n’umutekano we byashyizwe mu kaga bitewe ni uko habayeho ibirego birimo uburiganya n’ibinyoma; ntabwo yari afite uruhare rwo gushyira aya makuru hanze.
Ibi birego nta shingiro bifite kandi si ukuri na busa, ahubwo ni ibinyoma byambaye ubusa."
Amagambo yavuzwe na Waters yahise atuma anengerwa bikomeye kuri interineti, harimo no kunengwa n’uwahoze ari Umunyamabanga ushinzwe itangazamakuru mu Ngoro ya Perezida w’Amerika, Ari Fleischer.
Fleischer ati: "Uku guhakana guteye umujinya."
"Bikaba bigaragaza ko adafite ubushake bwo kuba umwe mu bagize Kongere.
Iyo umuntu ashinjwe ikintu atigeze akora, agomba kutarakara.
Ntagomba kwanga ko ubuyobozi bukora akazi kabwo.
Ntagomba kwibaza icyateye umurega kumurega.
Agomba gucisha make kandi agatuza."
Fleischer yahatirijwe kugereranya uko Waters yakiriye ibirego ni uko abademokarate banenze Umucamanza Kavanaugh, nawe washinjwe n’abamunenga kuba asa nk’aho yarakaye mu iburanisha ryo ku wa Kane.
Omar Navarro, umukandida w’umurepubulikani uri guhatana kugira ngo akure Waters mu mwanya mu matora yo mu gihembwe hagati, nawe yagaragaje ibitekerezo bye kuri Twitter.
Yandika kuri Twitter agira ati: "Byaba bikomeye biramutse ari ukuri."
Mu magambo yavuze, Waters yavuze ko ibiro bye byamenyesheje "inzego zibishinzwe ndetse n’inzego nyubahirizamategeko bikaba biri kureba kuri ibyo avuga ko ari uburiganya.
Akomeza agira ati: "Tuzakora ku buryo ababikoze byose bagaragazwa," kandi bazaryozwa mu rwego rw’amategeko ibikorwa byose bakoze bisenya cyangwa bibi ku bakozi bose bankorera."
Gusuzuma filime yitwa Johnny English Strikes Again - Rowan Atkinson udafite imbaraga zihagije yakinnye komedi ari umunetsi
Ubu, byamaze kuba umuco kureba umumaro w’uko Ubwongereza buzikura mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi, bikaba bimeze kimwe nka filime nshya ivuga ku mwongereza kandi bikaba bisa nk’aho bishoboka ko iyi filime nshya yo mu ruhererekane rwa filime zamenyekanye nka Johnny English irimo imirwano na komedi; ikaba yaratangiye mu mwaka wa 2003 yitwa Johnny English nyuma ikaza kongera gusohoka mu mwaka wa 2011 yitwa Johnny English Reborn.
Filime imeze nk’ikinamico ya komedi ivuga ku ngingo idafatika izagaragaza amahirwe dufite nk’igihugu mu mahirwe yo kujyana ibicuruzwa hanze?
Ku rugero urwo ari rwo rwose, umukinnyi ufite imitunu, washaje udafite ubushobozi witwa Johnny English yari afite uruhushya rwo kongera agahabwa amahirwe yo gukina filime ya kabiri, iryo zina rye rumvikana kurusha ibindi bintu byose bikaba ari igihangano cyagutse cya komedi cyakorewe abatavuga Icyongereza bo mu bice bikunda kureba filime.
Akina ari umwanjenti w’ibanga ukina yigira ukuntu gusekeje kugira ngo agaragaze isura ya bwana Clouseau, ujya kumera neza nk’uko bwana Bean akina ameze aho aba yagejeje ibintu kure nk’uko byari bimeze mu birori byo gufungura byiswe Chariots of Fire byo muri Olempike yabereye i Londere mu 2012.
By’umwimerere, ishingiye ku mugenzu ndetse n’umugabo w’umunyamagahanga witwa Atkinson wigeze gukina mu matangazo yamamaza ryanyuraga kuri televiziyo ya Barclaycard TV ubu ashobora kuba yaribagiranye, usiga ateje akavuyo.
Hari ibihe bibiri byiza mu isohorwa rya JE.
Nakunze uko Johnny English yegera kajugujugu mu gihe yari yambaye imyenda yo kwikingira y’indwanyi z’abo mu gihugmbi magana atanu ndetse n’umupanga wa kajugujugu ukaze gukora gato kuri kasike yari yambaye.
Impano ya Atkinson yo gukina komedi akoresheje umubiri we irigaragaza cyane, ariko uko asetse bisa nk’aho bidafite imbaraga kandi ntibisanzwe aho biri mu kavuyo kwneshi by’umwihariko nka filime zubatse amazina zizwi cyane nka 007 na Mission Impossible aho abakinamo "bazi icyo bakeneye" ubwabo bakina ibyo gusetsa ari nk’inyongezo.
Gusetsa biba bisa nk’aho bigenewe abana bato aho kuba abantu bakuru kandi ibikorwa bidasanzwe by’ubusazi bya Johnny English ntabwo birimo guhanga udushya kandi byibanda ku mafilime akinwa na Atkinson aho aba adasohora ijambo na rimwe ari Bean.
Inkuru yagiye igarukwaho cyane ni uko Ubwongereza bwari mu kaga gakomeye.
Umujura mu by’ikoranabuhanga rya mudasobwa yinjirira itsinda ry’abatasi rikomeye mu Bwongereza, akagaragaza imyirondoro y’abajenti bose b’abatasi b’abongereza bari gukorera ibikorwa ahantu hatandukanye, aho hari umukinnyi ugaragazwa ari mu kazi ariko bikaba bibabaje kuba yarahawe gukina agace gato witwa Kevin Eldon.
Ni cyo cyari ikibazo cy’ingutu kuri Minisitiri w’intebe wirata kandi uhanganye na benshi, akaba ari mu mazi abira aho ashobora kuba ari umunyapolitiki udakunzwe na gato: Emma Thompson afite imikinire myiza aho aba agiye kumera nka Teresa-May ariko mu byo agomba gukina nta kinini kirimo gifatika.
Abajyanama mu by’ubutasi be bamubwira ko umutasi uri ahantu hose yashyizwe ku karubanda, bikaba ari ngombwa ko hari umuntu agomba gukura mu kiruhuko cy’izabukuru.
Kandi bisobanuye ko nta wundi atari Johnny English, aho muri icyo gihe aba afite akazi k’ubwarimu mu ishuri rihenze, ariko akaba atanga amasomo atari mu nteganyanyigisho aho aba yigisha uko waba umutasi: Izo ni inama nziza aho English aho atanga isomo ku Ishuri rimeze nk’irya Rock ku byerekeye gukora ubutasi.
English asubizwa mu kigo cya Whitehall aho agomba guhabwa amabwiriza yihutirwa no kongera kubonana n’uwo bakoranaga kera witwa Bough, wongera gukinwa na Ben Miller.
Ubu, Bough yarashatsi, akaba yarashakanye n’umukomanda utwara ubwato bugendera munsi y’amazi, uwo mwanya ukinnywa na Vicki Pepperdine ariko ntubyazwa umusaruro.
Rero ni Batman na Robin bakina ibintu bakabizambya cyane muri Serivisi y’ibanga y’umwamikazi, bahura n’umugore ukaze ukorera Olga Kurylenko witwa Ophelia Bulletova.
Hagati aho, Minisitiri w’inebe yarari kugwa mu mutego w’umuhanga mu by’ikoranabuhanga ufite miriyari uvuga ko ashobora gukemura ikibazo cya mudasobwa kiri mu Bwongereza: Umunyamahirwe make witwa Jason Volta, umwanya kunwa na Jake Lacy.
English batangira Bough urugendo rugoye rwabo rwo kwiyoberanya bikabije: Bigira abaseriveri, bashumika resitora y’abafaransa; bateza akavuyo bagerageza kwinjira mu buryo bwa magendu mu bwato buhenze bwo gutembereramo bwa Volta; maze English ashaka kwikorera ibintu mu buryo bwe ubwo yageragezaga gukoresha ikuteri z’ukuri kudafatika kugira ngo yimenyereze imbere mu nzu ya Volta.
Ibyo byose bikinwa mu gice cya nyuma cya filime, ariko nk’uko bishimsihije kandi bikaba bikomeye, hari televiziyo y’abana yerekana ibyo byose.
Ni ibintu bisanzwe cyane.
Kandi ni ko izindi filime zose za Johnny English zimeze aho ntareka kubitekerezaho: Ese uruganda rwa filime mu Bwongereza ntirushobora guha Rowan Atkinson unwanya wo gukina neza akagaragaza impano ye?
Ishyaka ry’abakozi rirahakana ko riri gutekereza ku mugambi ugenewe abongereza yo gukora iminsi ine mu cyumweru ariko bakishyurwa iminsi itanu
Jeremy Corbyn wo mu ishyaka ry’abakozi ari tugekereza ku mugambi ukomeye aho uzasiga abongereza bose bakoze iminsi ine mu cyumweru, ariko bakishyurwa iminsi itanu.
Ishyaka rivuga ko ryifuza ko abayobozi b’amasosiyete atandukanye bashaka uko bazigama amafaranga binyuze mu iterambere ry’ubwenge buhangano (AI) rigenewe abakozi kugira ngo bahabwe umunsi w’inyongera w’ikiruhuko.
Bishobora gusiga abakozi baryoherwa na wikendi y’iminsi itatu, ariko bakishyurwa amafaranga bari basanzwe bishyurwa.
Abatanze amakuru bavuga ko icyo gitekerezo 'kibereye' umugambi w’ishyaka mu by’ubukungu kandi rikaba riteganya guhindura ibintu bikanogera abakozi bo mu gihugu.
Guhindura hakajya hakorwa iminsi ine mu cyumweru bishyigikiwe na Kongere ya sendika y’abakozi nk’uburyo bwo gutuma abakozi babyaza umusaruro impinduka ziri mu bukungu.
Umukomeye mu ishyaka ry’abakozi yabwiye ikinyamakuru cya The Sunday Times ati: 'Isuzuma ry’ingamba ryitezweho gutangazwa mbere y’impera z’umwaka.
'Ntabwo ari ibintu bizaba umunsi umwe ariko gukora iminsi ine mu cyumweru ni icyifuza kibereye uburyo bw’imikorere y’ishyaka ryo gushyira ibintu ku murongo mu by’ubukungu mu nyungu z’abakozi ndetse n’ingamba z’ishyaka mu by’inganda muri rusange.'
Ishyaka ry’abakozi rishobora kuba atari ryo rya mbere rishyigikiye icyo gitekerezo, ishyaka riharanira ibidukikije ryasezeranyije ko rizashyiraho uburyo bwo gukora iminsi ine mu cyumweru mu gikorwa cyagutse cyo kwiyamamaza mu matora rusange cyo mu mwaka wa 2017.
Icyakora, magingo aya icyo cyifuzo ntabwo gishyigikiwe n’abayoboke bose b’ishyaka ry’abakozi.
Umuvugizi w’ishyaka ry’abakozi yagize ati: 'Gukora iminsi ine mu cyumweru ntabwo ari ingamba z’ishyaka kandi ntabwo biri gutekerezwaho n’ishyaka.'
Uwungirije Shansoriye, John McDonnell, yakoresheje inama y’ishyaka ry’abakozi yabaye mu cyumweru gishize kugira ngo agaragaze icyerekezo cye ku mpinduka y’abasosiyarisite mu bukungu.
Bwana McDonnell yavuze ko yari yiyemeje kwisubiza imbaraga zanyazwe n’'abayobozi batagira isura' ndetse na 'ba rusahurira mu nduru b’amasosiyete y’amazi, gaze n’amashanyarazi.
Imigambi ya shansoriye wungirije inagaragaza ko abafatanyabikorwa bari mu masosiyete atanga amazi bashobora kudashyigikira umugambi we wose uko wakabaye mu gihe leta y’abakozi ya 'gabanya amafaranga' ishingiye ku bikorwa bibi yabonye biri gukorwa.
Yanemeje ko ateganya gushyira abakozi mu nama y’ubuyobozi bw’amasosiyete maze agashyiraho ikigo giharanira inyungu z’abakozi cyiswe Inclusive Ownership Funds aho kizajya giha 10 ku ijana ry’imigabane y’amasosiyete yigenga abakozi, aho biteganyijwe ko buri umwe ashobora kubona umugabane ku nyungu ugera ku mapawundi 500.
Lindsey Graham, John Kennedy babwiye ikiganiro cya "60 Minutes" niba iperereza rya FBI kuri Kavanaugh rishobora guhindura ibitekerezo byabo
Iperereza rya FBI ku byaha biregwa Umucamanza witwa Brett Kavanaugh byatindije byihuze icyumweru amatora ya nyuma ku kwemezwa nka Perezida w’Urukiko rw’Ikirenga, kandi hibazwa niba ibyo iryo shami ryabonye bishobora gutuma abasenateri b’abarepubulikani bisubiraho ntibakomeze kumushyigikira.
Mu kiganiro cyatamutse ku Cyumweru, umukozi ukorera ikiganiro cya "60 Minutes" witwa Scott Pelley yabajije abasenateri b’abarepubulikani John Kennedy na Lindsey Graham niba FBI ishobora kugira ibyo ivumbura bishobora gutuma bahindura ibyo batekereza.
Kennedy yasaga nk’aho yisanzuye kurusha mugenzi we wo muri South Carolina.
Kennedy ati: "Ni ko bimeze rwose."
"Navuze ibyerekeye kujya mu iburanisha, ni ko navuze, navuganye n’Umucamanza Kavanaugh.
Naramuhamagaye nyuma y’aho ibi bibaye, mvuga ko ibyo ashinja byasohitse, nti: 'Warabikoze?'
Yahagaze ku ijambo rye, yiyemeje kandi avuga neza uko byagenze."
Icyakora, amatora ya Graham yasaga nk’aho yarangije kwemezwa.
Ati: "Nafashe icyemezo ku byerekeye Brett Kavanaugh kandi ndifuza gufata gusenya ibyo ashinjwa."
"Dr. Ford, sinzi icyabaye, ariko nzi ibi: Brett yabihakanye yivuye inyuma," ibyo byongeweho na Graham ashaka kuvuga kuri Christine Blasey Ford.
"Kandi buri wese avuga ntabwo ashobora kubigenzura.
Ni ibirego byo mu myaka 36 ishize.
Nta kintu gishya mbona gishobora guhinduka."
Iserukiramuco ryiswe Global Citizen Festival ndetse hari icyo ryakoze kugira ngo rigabanye ubukene?
Kuri uyu wa Gatandatu, New York izakira iserukiramuco ryiswe Global Citizen Festival, rikaba ari igikorwa cy’umuziki ngarukamwaka kiba kirimo abaririmbyi b’ibirangirire baririmba ndetse banafite umugambi ushimishije, kurandura ubukene mu isi.
Ubu, ni umwaka wa karindwi ribaye, iserukiramuco ryiswe Global Citizen Festival rihuruza abantu ibihumbi bakaza muri Central Park's Great Lawn batazanywe gusa no kwishimira ibikorwa n’abahanzi bakomeye nka Janet Jackson, Cardi B na Shawn Mendes, ahubwo banakora ubukangurambaga ku ntego nyakuri y’iryo serukiramuciro aho ari ukurandura ubukene bukabije mu mwaka wa 2030.
Iserukiramuco ryiswe Global Citizen Festival, ryatangijwe mu 2012, rikaba ari igikorwa cyiyongera ku mushinga witwa Global Poverty Project, cy’itsinda mpuzamahanga rikora ubuvugizi ryizera ko hazabaho kurandura ubukene hongerwa umubare w’abantu bari kuburwanya ku buryo bugaragara.
Kugira ngo uhabwe itike y’ubuntu yo kukujyana muri iryo serukiramuco (keretse wifuza kwishyura itike y’abanyacyubahiro), abajya muri iryo serukiramuco bagomba gukora imirimo itandukanye cyangwa "ibikorwa" nk’ubukorerabushake, koherereza imeyiri abayobozi b’isi, guhamagara cyangwa ubundi buryo bw’ingirakamaro bwo gufasha mu gukora ubukangurambaga bw’intego bafite yo kurandura ubukene.
Ariko ni gute iserukiramuco ryiswe Global Citizen rigana ku ntego mu gihe habura imyaka 12 ngo intego yaryo igerweho?
Ese igitekerezo cyo guhemba abantu kujya muri konseri y’ubuntu ni bwo buryo buboneye bwo gutuma abantu basaba ko hagira igikorwa cyangwa ni ubundi buryo bwitwa "guharanira gukanda kuri interineti"; abantu bumva ko bari gukora impinduka nyayo bashyira umukono ku busabe bwo kuri interineti cyangwa kohereza ubutumwa kuri Twitter?
Kuva mu 2011, iserukiramuco rya Global Citizen rivuga ko ryanditse "ibikorwa" bigera kuri miriyoni 19 byakozwe n’abarishyigikiye, biganisha ku ntego zitandukanye.
Ribuga ko ibyo bikorwa byafashije mu gutuma abayobozi b’isi batangaza amabwiriza n’ingamba bingana n’agaciro ka miriyari 37 z’amadorali y’Amerika bigamije kugira icyo bihindura ku buzima bw’abarenga miriyari 2,25 z’abantu bitarenze mu mwaka wa 2030.
Mu ntangiriro za 2018, itsinda ryagaragaje ibyo ryiyemeje ibikorwa bigera kuri 390 aho byibuze amadorali y’Amerika agera kuri miriyari 10 yatanzwe cyangwa yakusanyijwe.
Itsinda rigereranya ko inkunga yabonetse kugeza ubu yazanye impinduka zitaziguye ku bantu hafi miriyoni 649 ku isi yose.
Bimwe mu byakozwe harimo imikoranire n’ishyirahamwe ryitwa The Power of Nutrition, ishyirahamwe ry’abashoramari bo mu Bwongereza ndetse n’abashyira ingamba mu bikorwa biyemeje "gufasha abana gukoresha ubushobozi bwabo bwose," biyemeza guha u miriyoni 35 z’amadorali y’Amerika mu gufasha kurangiza imirire mibi mu gihugu nyuma yo kubona ubutumwa bwo kuri Twitter burenga 4 700 bwanditse na Global Citizens.
"Ku bufasha bwa leta y’Ubwongereza, abaterankunga, leta z’ibihugu n’umuryango wa Global Citizens kimwe nkawe, dushobora gushyira iherezo ku busumbane mu by’imibereho bigasigara ari amateka," Ambasaderi w’ishyirahamwe ryitwa The Power of Nutrition, Tracey Ullman, yabibwiye imbaga muri konseri yabaga ako kanya i Londere muri Mata 2018.
Itsinda ryanavuze ko nyuma y’aho hakozwe ibikorwa birenga 5 000 bsiaba ko Ubwongereza bunoza imirire y’ababyeyi n’abana, leta yatangaje ko igiye gutera inkunga umushinga w’ishyirahamwe ryitwa the Power of Nutrition, bikaba bizagera ku bagore n’abana miriyoni 5 bazahabwa ubufasha mu by’imirire.
Mu gusubiza kimwe mu bibazo bikunda kwibazwa ku rubuga rwayo kigira kiti: "Ni iki gituma utekereza ko dushobora kurandura ubukene bukabije?"
Umuryango wa Global citizen wasubije ko: "Bizaba ari inzira ndende kandi ikomeye; rimwe na rimwe harimo kugwa no kutegera ku ntego.
Ariko, nk’uko impinduramatwara zikomeye mu guharanira uburenganzira bwa muntu n’izo kurwanya irondaruhu muri Afurika y’epfo zabayeho mbere y’uko dutangira ibikorwa, tuzagera ku ntegeo, kubera ko iyo dufatanyije tugira imbaraga kurushaho.
Abahanzi barimo Janet Jackson, the Weeknd, Shawn Mendes, Cardi B, Janelle Monáe ni bamwe mu bazaririmba uyu mwaka mu gitaramo kizabera i New York, kikazayoborwa na Deborra-Lee Furness na Hugh Jackman.
Amerika ishobora gukoresha amato y’intambara kugira ngo "ifunge" maze ibuze ko abarusiya bohereza mu mahanga ingufu; bikaba bitangazwa n’Umunyamabanga ushinzwe ibikorwa by’imbere mu gihugu
Leta ya Washington ishobora "niba ari ngombwa" gufata icyemezo cyo gukoresha amato y’intambara yayo mu rwego rwo kubuza ko gaze icuruzwa n’abarusiya zigera ku masoko atandukanye, harimo Uburasirazuba bwo hagati, bikaba byaratangajwe n’Umunyamabanga ushinzwe ibikorwa by’imbere mu gihugu witwa Ryan Zinke, nk’uko byagarutsweho n’ikinyamakuru cya Washington Examiner.
Zinke yashinje Uburusiye kwivanga mu ntambara yo muri Siriya; ahanini bukaba bwaragiyeyo ku butumire bwa leta yemewe, ariko akaba ari urwitwazo kuko yifuza gushakisha isoko rishya rya gaze.
Bivugwa ko yavuze ko: "Nizera ko impamvu bari mu Burasirazuba bwo hagati ari ko bifuza kubona isoko rya gaze nk’uko babikora mu burasirazuba bw’Uburayi, igice cy’amajyepfo cy’Uburayi."
Kandi, hakurikijwe ibitangazwa n’abayobozi, hari uburyo n’ubushobozi bwo guhangana na byo.
Ati: "Amerika ifite ubushobozi, dukoresheje amato y’intambara yacu, bwo gukora ku buryo imihanda yo mu nyanja ifungurwa kandi niba ari ngombwa tukayifunga, kugira ngo twizere neza ko gaze yabo itagera ku isoko."
Zinke yarari kugeza ijambo abitabiriye igikorwa cyakiriwe n’itsinda rya Consumer Energy Alliance, rikaba ari itsinda ridaharanira inyungu aho rivuga ko ari "ijwi ry’abakoresha gaze" muri Amerika.
Yakomeje agereranya uburyo bukoreshwa na leta ya Washington mu guhangana n’Uburusiya na Irani, avuga ko ntaho ibyo bihugu byombi bitaniye.
Ati: "Amahitamo y’ubukungu kuri Irani n’Uburusiya ari, hafi, yo kugira ingufu no gusimbura ibikomoka kuri peterori," yabivuze ashaka kuvuga ko Uburusiya ari "ifarasi y’inyamayeri" aho ubukungu bushingira cyane bikomoka kuri peteroli.
Ayo magambo yavuzwe nyuma y’aho ubutegetsi bwa Trump bufite gahunda yo kongera ingano ya gaze yahinduwemo ibisukika mu Burayi, bugasimbura Uburusiya, aho ari bwo bugurisha gaze ku giciro gito ku banyaburayi.
Bityo, abayobozi bo mu butegetsi bwa Trump, harimo na Perezida w’Amerika Donald Trump ubwe, bagerageza kureshya Ubudage kugira ngo buve mu mushinga "utaboneye" w’imiyoboro ya gaze wahawe izina rya Nord Stream 2, aho Trump avuga ko byatumye leta ya Berlin iba "ingwate" ya leta y’ i Moscow.
Moscow yakomeje gutangaza ishingamira ko miriyari 11 z’amadorali y’Amerika ziri mu mushinga w’imiyoboro ya gaze wahawe izina rya Nord Stream 2, witezweho gukuba kabiri ubushobozi bwari busanzweho bw’imiyoboro bukagera kuri metero kibe miriyari 110, nta kindi ugamije uretse kuba umushinga w’ubukungu.
Leta ya Kremlin ivuga ko kuba leta ya Washington itemera na gato uwo mushinga bishingiye ahanini ku mpamvu z’ubukungu kandi bikaba ari urugero rwiza rugaragaza kubogama mu guhangana ku isoko.
"Ndizera ko dusangiye ibitekerezo ko gaze idashobora kuba igikoresho cyo gushyira uruhande runaka ku gitutu kandi ko abayikoresha bagomba kubasha guhitamo abayigemura," ayo ni amagambo ya Minisitiri w’Uburusiya ushinzwe ingufu, Aleksandr Novak, nyuma y’inama yamuhuje n’Umunyamabanga wa leta ushinzwe ingufu muri Amerika, Rick Perry, i Moscow muri Nzeli.
Aho Amerika ihagaze ntabwo higeze hakirwa neza n’Ubudage, bukaba bwarongeye gushimangira ko bushyigikiye uwo mushinga.
Ishyirahamwe rikomeye mu Budage rishinzwe iby’inganda ryitwa Federation of German Industries (BDI), ryasabye ko Amerika yirinda kwegera ibyerekeye ingamba z’ingufu mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi ndetse n’amasezerano yakozwe hagati ya leta ya Berlin na Moscow.
"Mfite ikibazo gikomeye iyo igihugu cya gatatu kivanze mu buryo tugemuramo gaze," amagambo ya Dieter Kempf, umuyobozi w’ishyirahamwe rya Federation of German Industries (BDI) akaba aherutse kubivugira mu nama yahuje Shansoriye w’Ubudage, Angela Merkel, na Perezida w’Uburusiya, Vladimir Putin.
Elizabeth Warren "azatekereza cyane" ku byo kwiyamamariza kuba perezida mu 2020, bikaba bitangazwa na Senateri wa leta Massachusetts
Ku wa Gatandatu Senateri wa leta ya Massachusetts, Elizabeth Warren, yavuze ko agomba "gutekereza cyane" kwiyamamariza kuba perezida nyuma y’amatora yo mu gihembwe hagati.
Mu mbwirwaruhame yo mu nzu mberabyombyi ya Holyoke, Massachusetts, Warren yemeje ko ari gutekereza kwiyamamaza.
Hakurikijwe ibivugwa n’ikinyamakuru cya The Hill, yagize ati: "Igihe kirageze ko abagore bajya i Washington maze bakunga leta yacu yacitsemo ibice aho izaba iyobowe n’umugore."
"Nyuma ya tariki ya 6 Ukuboza, nzatekereza cyane ku kwiyamamariza kuba perezida."
Warren yagize icyo avuga kuri Perezida Donald Trump mu mbirwaruhame yo mu nzu mberabyombi, avuga ko ari "kuganisha igihugu mu cyerekezo kitari cyo.
Ati: "Mpangayikishijwe cyane n’ibyo Donald Trump ari gukorera demokarasi yacu."
Warren yagarutse cyane anenga Trump ndetse n’uwo yagennye ko aba Perezida w’Urukiko rw’Ikirenga, Brett Kavanaugh.
Mu butumwa bwo kuri Twitter bwo ku wa Gatanu, Warren yagize ati: "Ni byo koko dukeneye ko FBI ikora iperereza mbere y’amatora."
Icyakora, ubushakashatsi bwasohowe ku wa Kane bwagaragaje ko abenshi mu batora mu gace Warren aturukamo badatekereza ko agomba kwiyamamaza mu 2020.
Abantu mirongo itanu n’umunani ku ijana by’"abashobora" gutora muri leta ya Massachusetts bavuze ko senateri atagomba kwiyamamaza, hakurikijwe ubushakashatsi bwakozwe na kaminuza ya Suffolk University Political Research Center/Boston Globe.
Mirongo itatu na kabiri ku ijana bashyigikiye ko yiyamamaza.
Ubushakashatsi bwagaragaje ko ashyigikiwe cyane n’uwahoze ari Guverineri witwa Deval Patrick, aho 38 ku ijana bashyigikiye ko yiyamamaza naho 48 ku ijana bakaba batabishyigikiye.
Abandi bafite amazina akomeye b’abademokarate baganiriweho ko bashobora kwiyamamaza mu matora yo mu 2020 harimo uwahoze ari Visi Perezida, Joe Biden, na Senateri wa Vermont, Bernie Sanders.
Biden yavuze ko ashobora gufata icyemezo ku buryo buzwi muri Mutarama, ibyo byatangajwe n’ikinyamakuru cya Associated Press.
Sarah Palin avuga ku ihungabana rya Track Palin mu kwiyamamaza kwa Donald Trump
Track Palin, w’imyaka 26, yamaze umwaka muri Irake nyuam yo gushyira ku rutonde rw’abazajyayo muri Nzeli.
Yarafashwe maze ashinjwa gukora ihohoterwa rikorerwa mu ngo ku wa Mbere nijoro
Yabibwiye abari bari mu kwiyamamaza kwa Donald Trump muri Tulsa, Oklahoma ati: "Ibyo umwana wanjye ari kunyuramo, ibyo yahuye na byo, nshobora kubihuza ni uko indi miryango iri kumba uburemere bw’ihungabana ndetse n’ibikomere abasirikare bacu bagarukana."
Palin yavuze ku ifatwa rye aryita "gushakira ikibazo aho kitari" kandi avuga ko umuhungu we ndetse n’abandi bahoze ku rugamba, "bagaruka batandukanye, bagaruka barakomerewe, bagaruka bibaz niba hari icyubahiro gihabwa abasirikare bagenzi babo n’abarwanira mu kirere ndetse na buri musirikare kubera ko uko bitangiye igihugu."
Yafatiwe ku wa Mbere muri Wasilla, Alaska maze ashinjwa ihohoterwa rikorerwa mu ngo no gusagarira umugore, abangamira kuvuga iby’ihohoterwa rikorerwa mu ngo ndetse no gutunga imbunda igihe yafashe ibiyobyabwenge, hakurikijwe ibivugwa na Dan Bennett, umuvuguzi w’Ishami rya Polisi rya Wasilla.
Leta 18 na D.C. bishyigikiye uburyo bwo kwamagana ingamba nshya zo gusaba ubuhungiro
Leta cumi n’umunani na District of Columbia bishyigikiye ibyashyizwe mu butabera bibuza ingamba nshya z’Amerika zo kwima ubuhungiro abahohotewe bahunga agatsiko k’abagizi ba nabi cyangwa ihohoterwa rikorerwa mu ngo.
Abahagarariye leta 18 n’akarere batanze inyandiko y’incamake y’inshuti z’urukiko ku wa Gatanu muri Washington kugira ngo bakumire ingamba zerekeye abasaba ubuhunguro nk’uko bitangazwa n’ikinyamakuru cya NBC News.
Amazina yose y’abatanze ikirego bashyigikiye Grace v. Sessions avuga ko ikirego cy’ishyirahamwe rya American Civil Liberties Unionfiled cyatanzwe muri Kanama haregwa ingamba za leta ntabwo kigeze gitangazwa.
Yavuze ko uwo bakundana "ndetse n’abahungu be bari mu gatsiko k’abagizi ba nabi," bamuhohoteye ariko abayobozi b’Amerika bakanga ubusabe bwe bwo kubona ubuhungiro tariki 20 Nyakanga.
Yafungiwe muri Texas.
Abunganira leta bashyigikira Grace yasobanuye El Salvador, Honduras na Guatemala, bikaba ari byo bivamo umubare mwinshi w’abasaba ubuhungiro muri Amerika, nk’igihugu gihura n’ibibazo biri ahantu henshi by’udutsiko tw’abagizi ba nabi n’ihohoterwa rikorerwa mu ngo.
Ingamba nshya z’Amerika ku basaba ubuhungiro zahinduye icyemezo cyo mu 2014 cy’Urwego rushinzwe ubujurire bw’abimukira cyatumye abimukira badafite ibyangombwa bahunze ihohoterwa rikorerwa mu ngo basaba ubuhungiro.
