Umucamanza mukuru wa District of Columbia, Karl Racine, mu ijambo yavuze ku wa Gatanu, yavuze ko ingamba nshya "zirengagiza amategeko amaze imyaka mirongo ya leta, y’igihugu ndetse n’ayo ku rwego mpuzamahanga."
"Itegeko ry’igihugu risaba ko ibirego byo gusaba ubuhungiro byose biburanishwa hashingiwe ku makuru yihariye ndetse ni uko icyo kirego cyabayeho kandi izo ngamba nshya zashyizweho zikaba zirenga kuri iryo hamwe," ibyo byanditse mu nyandiko y’incamake yatanzwe n’inshuti z’urukiko.
Abacamanza bakomeje gusaba muri iyo nyandiko y’incamake ko ingamba zibuza abimukira kwinjira bibangamira ubukungu bw’Amerika, bavuga ko bishoboka cyane ko baba ba rwiyemezamirimo ndetse "bakanatanga akazi ka ngombwa."
Muri Kamena, Umucamanza mukuru, Jeff Sessions, yasabye ko abacamanza baburanisha imanza z’abimukira batazongera guha ubuhungiro abakorewe ihohoterwa bahunga ihohoterwa ryo mu ngo ndetse n’ihohoterwa rikorwa n’abo mu gatsiko k’abagizi ba nabi.
Mu byatangajwe na Sessions tariki ya 11 Kamena kuri izo ngamba yagize ati: "Ubuhungiro buhabwa abava mu bihugu bakomokamo kubera ko bari kugirirwa nabi cyangwa bafite ubwoba bw’uko bashobora gukorerwa ivangura rishingiye ku ibara ry’uruhu, idini, ubwenegihugu, cyangwa kuba bari mu itsinda ry’abantu runaka cyangwa kubera ibitekerezo bya politiki bafite."
Ubuhungiro ntabwo bigamije kugabanya ubukana bw’ibibazo; nubwo byaba ari ibibazo bikomeye bite abantu bahura na byo buri munsi ku isi yose.
Ibikorwa bikomeye by’ubutabazi muri Palu mu gihe umubare w’abapfuye wikubye kabiri mu gushaka byihuse ko hari abakorotse
Ku barokotse, ibibazo byakomezaga gukomera uko amasaha yicuma.
Umubyeyi witwa Risa Kusuma w’imyaka 35, waruri guhoza umwana we w’umuhungu ufite umuriro ku kigo kijyanwaho abarokowe yarakariye umujyi wa Palu agira ati: "Ndumva bikomeye cyane."
"Buri munota haza imbangukiragutabara izanye imirambo.
Amazi meza ni imbonekarimwe."
Abahatuye bagaragaye bari kugaruka mu ngo zabo zasenyutse, bafate ibyari ibyabo byarengewe n’amazi, bagerageza gushakisha icyaba kikiri kizima bakoresha.
Abantu amajana barakomeretse naho ibitaro byangijwe n’umutingito ufite ubukana bwa 7.5 byari byarengewe.
Bamwe muri bo barakomeretse, harimo Dwi Haris, wavunitse umugongo n’urutugu, aryamye hanze y’ibitaro bya gisirikare by’i Palu, aho abarwayi bari kuvurirwa hanze bitewe ni uko hari imitingito mito ikomeza kumvikana.
Amarira yari yuzuye mu maso ye ubwo yasubiragamo uko ibintu byagenze aho yumvishe umutingito ukaze utigisa icyumba cya hoteri kiri muri etaje ya gatanu yari arimo hamwe n’umugore we n’umwana we.
"Nta gihe twari dufite cyo guhunga.
Nakanzwe n’ibisigazwa by’inkuta, ni ko mbitekereza," Haris yabwiye ibiro ntaramakuru by’Amerika bizwi nka Associated Press, yongeraho ko umuryango we waruri mu mujyi watashye ubukwe.
"Numvise umugore wanjye ari gutaka asaba ubufasha, ariko nyuma aza guceceka.
Sinzi uko byamugendekeye we n’umwana wanjye.
Ndizera ko batekanye."
Ambasaderi w’Amerika ashinja Ubushinwa 'kubangama' aho bukoresha amatangazo yamamaza icengezamatwara'
Icyumweru kimwe nyuma y’aho ikinyamakuru cyo mu Bushinwa cyanyujije itangazo rya paji enye mu kinyamakuru kandikirwa buri munsi muri Amerika cyiyemera ku bucuruzi bufitiye inyungu Amerika n’Ubushinwa, ambasaderi w’Amerika mu Bushinwa yashinje leta ya Beijing gukoresha ikinyamakuru cyo muri Amerika kugira ngo isakaze icengezamatwara ryayo.
Ku wa Gatatu ushize, Perezida w’Amerika, Donald Trump, yavuye ukuntu kinyamakuru cya China Daily cyishyuye amafaranga y’umurengera ikinyamakuru cya Des Moines Register; kikaba ari ikinyamakuru cya leta ya Iowa kigurisha ibinyamakuru cyane; nyuma y’aho ashinjirije Ubushinwa gushaka kwivanga mu matora ya kongere y’Amerika tariki ya 6 Ugushyingo, Ubushinwa bukaba buhakana ibyo birego.
Ibyo Trump ashinja leta ya Beijing by’uko yashatse kwivanga mu matora y’Amerika bigaragaza icyo abayobozi b’Amerika babwiye ikinyamakuru cya Reuters ko ari icyiciro gishya mu gushyira umugambi ku rundi rwego wateguwe na leta ya Washington ugamije gushyira igitutu ku Bushinwa.
Mu gihe ari ibisanzwe ko leta z’amahanga zishyiraho amatangazo yamamaza kugira ngo zamamaze ubucuruzi, leta ya Beijing n’iya Washington kuri ubu zihugiye mu ntambara y’ubucuruzi yafashe indi ntera aho yageze n’aho hongerwa imisoro ku bicuruzwa byinjizwa muri buri gihugu.
Ubushinwa na bwo bwihoreye mu rwego rw’imisoro intambara y’ubucuruzi igitangira aho byateganyijwe ko isibasira abohereza ibicuruzwa hanze bo muri leta ya Iowa yafashije Ishyaka ry’abarepubulikana rya Trump, ibyo bitangazwa n’impuguke ku mubano w’Ubushinwa n’Amerika.
Terry Branstad, ambasaderi w’Amerika mu Bushinwa akaba yaramaze igihe kirekire ari guverineri wa leta ya Iowa, akaba ari umucuruzi ukomeye wohereza ibicuruzwa byinshi bikomoka ku buhinzi mu Bushinwa, yavuze ko leta ya Beijing ibangamiye abahinzi, aborozi n’abakora ubucuruzi b’abanyamerika,.
Ubushinwa, Branstad yanditse mu hagenewe ibitekerezo mu kinyamakuru cya Des Moines Register cyasohotse ku Cyumweru agira ati: "Ubu bwakajije umurego mu kutabangamira no gushyira amatangazo y’icengezamatwara mu binyamakuru byacu byigenga."
Branstad ati: “Mu rwego rwo gukwirakwiza icengezamatwara ryabwo, leta y’Ubushinwa iri kungukira mu muco w’Amerika wo guha umuntu ubwisanzure bwo kuvuga icyo ashaka ndetse n’ubwigenge bw’ibinyamakuru ushyira amatangazo yishyurwa mu kinyamakuru cya Des Moines Register."
"Mu bitandukanye, ku ma kiyosike agurisha ibinyamakuru mu mihanda ya hano muri Beijing, ubonamo ibyavuzwe n’abatishimiye imikorere ya leta ariko ntabwo ubonamo ishusho nyayo y’ibitekerezo bitandukanye by’uko abashinwa bashobora kuba bari mu nzira y’ubukungu irimo ibibazo, bitewe ni uko itangazamakuru rihozwaho ijisho n’ishyaka riri ku butegetsi rya Chinese Communist Party," ni ko yanditse.
Yongeyeho ko "kimwe mu binyamakuru bikomeye mu Bushinwa cyahunze icyo kiraka cyo gutangaza" inkuru ye, nubwo atigeze avuga izina ry’icyo kinyamakuru.
Abasesenguzi bari kuburira ko abarepubulikani bari kwitandukanya n’abagore batora mbere gato y’amatora yo hagati mu gihembwe hamwe na Kavanaugh Debacle
Mu gihe abenshi mu bakomeye bo mu ishyaka ry’abarepubulikani bategereje kandi bari gushyigikira uwatanzwe kuzaba Umukuru w’Urukiko rw’ikirenga, Brett Kavanaugh, uri kuregwa ibyaha byinshi byo gusagarira umugore bishingiye ku gitsina, umusesenguzi yaburiye ko ibyo bakora bitazakirwa neza; by’umwihariko, ku ruhande rw’abagore, mu gihe cy’amatora yeregeje yo hagati mu gihembwe.
Amarangamutima agaragiye iki kibazo ni menshi cyane kandi abenshi mu barepubulikani bamaze kwigaragaza barekana ko bifuza ko amatora akomeza.
Ibyo bintu ntabwo bishobora gusubizwa inyuma," ibyo Grant Reeher, umwairmu w’isomo rya politiki wa kaminuza yo muri Syracuse yitwa Maxwell School yabibwiye ikinyamakuru cya The Hill mu nkuru yatangajwe ku wa Gatandatu.
Reeher yavuze ko ashidikanya ko ibyo Senateri Jeff Flake (Umurepubulikana uhagarariye leta ya Arizona) yatangaje ku munot wa nyuma kugira ngo FBI ikore iperereza bizaba bihagije kugira ngo hahoshwe uburakare bw’abatora barakaye.
"Abagore ntabwo bazigera bibabirwa ibyabaye ejo hashize; ntabwo bazabyibagirwa ejo hazaza kandi nta nubwo bazabyibagirwa mu Ugushyingo," ibyo Karine Jean-Pierre, umujyanama mukuru n’umuvugizi ku rwego rw’igihugu w’itsinda riharanira iterambere ryitwa MoveOn yabivuze ku wa Gatanu, hakurikijwe ibyatangajwe n’ikinyamakuru cyo muri Washington, D.C.
Ku wa Gatanu mu gitondo, abigaragambya baririmbaga bagira bati: "Ugushyingo kwageze!" ubwo bigaragambirizaga mu kirongozi cya Sena mu gihe abarepubulikani bagenzura Komite ishinzwe ubutabera bahisemo gukomeza bakemeza igenwa rya Kavanaugh nubwo hari ubuhambya bwatanzwe na Dr. Christine Blasey Ford, nk’uko bitangazwa na Mic.
Stu Rothenberg, umusesenguzi wa politiki udafite ishyaka abarizwamo, yabwiye urubuga rw’amakuru ko: "Ishyaka ry’abademokarate n’icyo bagamije biri ku rwego rwo hejuru."
"Abantu bari kuvuga ko n’ubundi biri ku rwego rwo hejuru, kandi ni ukuri.
Ariko bishobora kugera hejuru kurushaho; by’umwihariko, mu bagore batari bamenye neza uwo bazatora mu nkengero z’umujyi ndetse n’abatora bakiri bato, bafite imyaka kuva 18 kugera ku 29, iyo badakunda perezida, akenshi ntibatora."
Nubwo mbere y’uko Ford atanga ubuhamya mu ruhame asobanura neza uko yasagariwe bishingiye ku gitsina bikozwe n’uwashyizweho ngo azabe Umukuru w’urukiko, abasesenguzi bavuga ko ibintu bidashobora kwakirwa neza mu gihe abarepubulikani bakomeza kugira ngo yemezwe.
Michael Steele, wahoze ari umuyobozi mukuru wa Komite y’abarepubulikani ku rwego rw’igihugu, mu ntangiriro z’icyumweru gishize, mu makuru yatangajwe na NBC News yagize ati: "Ibi byabaye akavuyo gateye urujijo mu ishyaka ry’abarepubulikani."
"Ntabwo ari ibyerekeye amatora ya komite cyangwa amatora ndakuka cyangwa niba Kavanaugh yakwicazwa, binerekeye ku buryo abalepubulikani bitwara muri iki kibazo ndetse ni uko bamufashemo," amagambo ya Guy Cecil, umuyobozi mukuru wa Priorities USA, itsinda rifasha gutora abademokarate, yabitangaje kuri shene y’amakuru.
Icyakora, abanyamerika barasa nk’aho bacitsemo ibice ku byerekeye uwo bakwiye kwizera nyuma y’ubuhamya bwa Ford na Kavanaugh, aho abenshi bahengamiye ku buhamya bwatanzwe n’uwa nyuma.
Ubushakashatsi bushya bwakozwe n’ikigo cya YouGov bwerekana ko 41 ku ijana by’abasubije bizera nta gushidikanya cyangwa bashobora kuba bizera ubuhamya bwa Ford, mu gihe 35 ku ijana bavuze ko bizera nta gushidikanya cyangwa bashobora kuba bizera ubuhamya bwa Kavanaugh.
Naho, 38 ku ijana bavuze ko batekereza ko Kavanaugh ashobora kuba cyangwa nta gushidikanya ko yabeshye mu buhamya yatanze, mu gihe 30 ku ijana bavuze bimwe kuri Ford.
Nyuma y’aho Flake asabye ko hagira igikorwa, kuri ubu FBI iri gukora iperereza ku birego byatanzwe na Ford ndetse byibuze n’umwe umushinja, Deborah Ramirez, nk’uko bitangazwa na The Guardian.
Ford yatanze buhamya mbere ya Komite ya sena ishinzwe ubutabera hakurikijwe indahiro yatanzwe mu cyumweru gishize ivuga ko Kavanaugh yari yanyweye maze akamusagarira ku myaka 17.
Ramirez ashinja uwatangajwe ko azaba Umukuru w’Urukiko rw’ikirenga ko yamweretse ubugabo bwe mu gihe yari yitabiriye ibirori mu gihe yigaga muri kaminuza ya Yale mu myaka ya za 80.
Uwavumbuye urubuga mpuzamahanga arateganya gutangira interineti nshya kugira ngo ahangane na Google na Facebook
Tim Berners-Lee, wahimbye urubuga mpuzamahanga, agiye gutangiza sosiyete agamije guhangana na Facebook, Amazon na Google.
Umushinga uheruka w’igihangange mu ikoranabuhanga, Inrupt, ni sosiyete yashingiye ku rubuga ruboneka hose rwa Berners-Lee rwitwa Solid.
Solid ituma abarukoresha bahitamo aho amakuru yabo abikwa ndetse n’abantu bemerewe kugera kuri ayo makuru.
Mu kiganiro cyihariye yahaye sosiyete ya Fast Company, Berners-Lee yateye urwenya avuga ko icyo Inrupt igamije ari "kwigarurira isi."
Avuga kuri iyo sosiyete agiye gutangiza, yagize ati: "Tugomba kubikora nonaha."
"Ni igihe ndangamateka."
Porogaramu ikoresha ikoranabuhanga rya Solid kugira ngo yemerere abantu kwishyiriraho "ububiko bw’amakuru bwite bwo kuri interineti" cyangwa POD.
Bushobora kujyaho urutonde rw’abo mwandikirana, urutonde rw’ibyo gukora, indangaminsi, isomero ry’umuziki n’ibindi bikoresho bwite n’ibyo mu mwuga.
Rumeze nka Google Drive, Microsoft Outlook, Slack na Spotify byose bikaba biboneka muri mushakisha imwe kandi icyarimwe.
Icyihariye kuri ubwo bubiko bw’amakuru bwite bwo kuri interineti ni uko bireba ku buryo busesuye ukoresha akaba ari we ugena ugera ku makuru runaka.
Sosiyete ibyita "kongerera ubushobozi abantu ku giti cyabo binyuze mu makuru."
Igitekerezo cya Inrupt, hakurikijwe ibitangazwa n’Umuyobozi mukuru wa sosiyete witwa John Bruce, ni uko sosiyete igomba kuzana ubushobozi, ibikorwa n’ubumenyi biboneye kugira ngo bifashe mu gutuma Solid igera kuri bose.
Kuri ubu, sosiyete igizwe na Berners-Lee, Bruce, urubuga rw’umutekano rwazanywe na IBM, bamwe mu bakozi bakora porogaramu bahawe amasezerano yo gukora ku mishinga itandukanye ndetse n’ihuriro ry’abakorerabushake bandika kode.
Guhera iki cyumweru, abakora ikoranabuhanga ku isi bashobora kwikorera porogaramu zikoresha urusobemiyoboro rw’uruhererekane hakoreshejwe ibikoresho biboneka ku rubuga rwa Inrupt.
Berners-Lee yavuze ko we n’itsinda rye batari kuvugana na "Facebook na Google ku byerekeye niba batangiza cyangwa batatangiza impinduka aho uburyo ubucuruzi bwabo bukoramo bushobora kuba bwarangiye mu gihe gito gishoboka.
"Ntabwo turi kubasaba urushya."
Mu byatangajwe kuri Medium byashyizwe ahagaragara ku wa Gatandatu, Berners-Lee yanditse avuga ko icyo Inrupt "igamije ari ugutanga ingufu zo mu rwego rw’ubucuruzi ndetse n’imikoranire ifasha kurinda ubusugire n’ubuziranenge bw’urubuga rushya rwubatswe hakoreshejwe Solid."
Mu 1994, Berners-Lee yahinduye interineti ubwo yashingaga Ihuriro ry’urubuga mpuzamahanga muri Kaminuza ya Massachusetts Institute of Technology.
Mu mezi make ashize, Berners-Lee yabaye ijwi rizana impinduka mu biganiro bigamije gutuma interineti itagira uyiharira.
No mu gihe yatangije Inrupt, Berners-Lee azakomeza kuba Uwashinze n’Umuyobozi mukuru w’Ihuriro ry’urubuga mpuzamahanga, Ishyirahamwe ryiswe Web Foundation n’Ikigo cya Open Data Institute.
Berners-Lee ati: "Mfitiye icyizere cyinshi ku bihe biri imbere mu rwego rw’imbuga mpuzamahanga."
Bernard Vann: Umwe mu bahawe umudari wa WW1 Victoria Cross yakorewe ibirori
Umwe mu bakorera idini ry’Urusengero rw’Ubwongereza yahawe umudari wa Victoria Cross mu ntambara y’isi ya mbere nk’indwanyi akaba yarakorewe ibirori mu mujyi avukamyo nyuma y’imyaka 100.
Liyetona Koroneri Revera Bernard Vann yahawe uwo mudari tariki ya 29 Nzeli 1918 mu gitero cyagabwe i Bellenglise no muri Lehaucourt.
Icyakora, yishwe na mudahushwa nyuma y’iminsi ine kandi ntabwo yigeze amenya ko yatsindiye umudari usumba iyindi mu ngabo z’Ubwongereza.
Ku wa Gatandatu, ibuye ryo kumwibuka ryamuritswe n’abuzukuru be babiri mu karasisi kabereye i Rushden, Northamptonshire.
Umwe mu buzukuru be, Michael Vann, yavuze ko ari "ikimenyetso cyiza cyane" kuba ibuye rimuritswe neza hashize imyaka 100 nyuma y’imirwano yatumye sekuru ahabwa umudari wa mbere ukomeye.
Ku bw’ikinyamakuru cya London Gazette, tariki ya 29 Nzeli 1918; Liyetona Koroneri Vann yayoboye batayo ye ayinzuza mu muyobora wa Saint-Quentin "unyura mu gihu gikaze kandi iri kumishwaho amasasu menshi y’ingabo zirwanira ku butaka ndetse n’ayo mu mbunda za mashinigani."
Nyuma yaje kwihuta agana aho urugamba rwari rukomeye maze n’"ubutwari bikomeye" ayobora ingabo ze zikomeza gusonga imbere zihashya umwanzi kugeza aho ubwe yabashije guhashya amatsinda atatu y’abasirikare bari bahanganye.
Liyetona Koroneri yishwe na mudahushwa w’umudage tariki ya 4 zUkwakira 1918, habura ukwezi kumwe ngo intambara irangiye.
Michael Vann, w’imyaka 72, yavuze ko ibikorwa bya sekuru byari "ikintu nzi ko ntashobora kuzigera nkorera kubera ko ariko bikaba bituma yicisha bugufi."
We n’umuvandimwe we, Dr James Vann, na bo bashyize indabo ku mva nyuma y’akarasisis, kakaba karayobowe na bande y’urubyiruko yitwa Brentwood Imperial Youth Band.
Michael Vann yagize ati: "Numva ntewe ishema cyane no kuba naragize uruhare muri aka karasisi" maze yongeraho ko "imbaraga z’intwari nyayo zigaragazwa n’ubufasha butangwa n’abantu benshi."
Abafana b’imikino ndyarugamba izwi ku izina rya MMA bamaze ijoro ryose badasinziriye bategereje kureba umukino wa Bellator 206, ahubwo berekwa filime y’ibitente y’uruhererekane yitwa Peppa Pig
Bitekerezeho nawe, wamaze ijoro ryose udasinziriye kugira ngo ureba aho baterana imigeri n’amakofi mu murwano wa Bellator 206 bikarangira wangiwe kureba umurwano wari utegerejwe na benshi.
Urutonde rw’imikino rwo muri San Jose rwari ruriho ko hari bube imirwano 13, harimo itandatu itegerejwe na benshi ndetse ikerekanwa ako kanya mu ijoro mu Bwongereza kuri shene ya 5.
Saa 6 z’igitondo, ubwo Gegard Mousasi na Rory MacDonald bari biteguye guhura, abareba televiziyo mu Bwongereza baguye mu kantu ubwo shene barebaga yahindutse iyi’ibitente bizwi nka Peppa Pig.
Bamwe ntibashimishijwe n’ibyabaye nyuma y’aho bamaze ijoro ryose bataryamye kugeza mu masaha ya mugitondo ahanini bategereje umurwano.
Umwe mu bafana kuri Twitter yasobanuye ko guhindura bakerekana ibitente by’abana ari "urwenya rudafite shinge na rugero."
"Ni amategeko ya leta ko 6:00 z’igitondo ibyerekanwa bitari bibereye ubwo barahinduye bashyiramo porogaramu z’abana, " byavuzwe na Dave Schwartz, Visi Perezida wa Bellator ushinzwe imenyekansihabikorwa n’itumanaho, ubwo yabazwaga iby’amashusho yerekanywe.
""Peppa the pig," yego."
Perezida wa sosiyete ya Bellator, Scott Coker, yavuze ko bagiye kugira icyo bahindura ku ngengabihe yabo harimo n’abareba televiziyo bo muri Bwongereza mu minsi iri imbere.
Coker yavuze ko: "Ntekereza ko igihe ntekereza ku byerekeye kureba umurwano warangiye, ntekereza ko ahari bashobora kugira icy babikoraho."
"Ariko ni saa kumi n’ebyiri z’igitondo ku Cyumweru iyo ngiye kandi ntabwo tubasha kugira icyo tubihinduraho kugeza bibaye ku Cyumweru ku isaha yacu, bikaba ari ku wa Mbere ku isaha yabo.
Ariko turi kugira icyo tubikoraho.
Munyizere, ubwo nahinduraga shene hari imyandiko myinshi yagendaga igaruka kandi yose ntabwo yatangaga ubutumwa bwiza.
Twari turi kugerageza kubikemura, dutekereza ko byari ikibazo cya tekiniki.
Ariko ntibyari byo, byari ikibazo cya leta.
Ndabasezeranya ko ubutaha bitazongera kubaho.
Tuzabigabanya bibe imirwano itanu aho kuba itandatu; nk’uko dusanzwe tubikora kandi twagerageje guha byinshi abafana bacu maze turarengera.
Ni ibyabaye bibabaje."
Ikiganiro cya radiyo cyitwa Desert Island Discs: Tom Daley yumvise 'acishijwe bugufi' ku byerekeye imibonano mpuzabitsina
Umukinnyi mu kwibira mu mikino ya Olempike witwa Tom Daley yavuze ko yakuze yumva ko acishijwe bugufi kuri buri wese kubera iby’imbonano mpuzabitsina bye, ariko byamuteye ishyaka ryo kuba yarageze ku ntego.
Uwo mukinnyi w’imyaka 24 yavuze ko atigeze abimenya kugeza agiye mu mashuri yisumbuye abona ko "buri wese atari ko ameze nkanjye."
Avugana bwa mbere kuri mu kiganiro cya Radiyo ya 4 cyitwa Desert Island Discs gikorwa na Lauren Laverne, yavuze ko yavuze ku byerekeye uburenganzira bw’abatinganyi kugira ngo ahe abandi "icyizere."
Yanavuze ko kuba umubyeyi byatumye yita gake ku byo gutsindira imidari yo mu marushanwa ya Olempike.
Usanzwe atangaza ikiganiro kimaze igihe kirekire, Kirsty Young, yari yafashe amezi menshi y’ikiruhuko kubera uburwayi.
Agaragara nk’uwatawe mu kiganiro cya mbere cya Laverne, Daley yavuze ko yumva ko "ari munsi" y’undi wese abyiruka kubera ko "bitari byemewe mu muryango gukunda abahungu n’abakobwa."
Yagize ati: "Kugeza uyu munsi, ibyo byiyumvo byo kumva ko ndi hasi no kumva ko ntandukanye, byagiye biba ikintu gikomeye cyampaye ububasha n’imbaraga zo kubasha kugera ku ntego."
Yifuzaga kugaragaza ko yari "ikintu runaka," yabivuze atyo kugira ngo atagira uwo atenguha ubwo yageze aho akamenya ibyerekeye iby’imibonano mpuzabitsina bye.
Umukinnyi watsindiye imidari ibiri y’umuringa mu mikino ya Olempike yabaye ukora ubukangurambaga bw’abahuje ibitsina uzwi cyane kandi yakoresheje ubwitabire mu mikino y’ibihugu bivuga icyongereza n’ibyakoronijwe n’Ubwongereza izwi nka Commonwealth Games muri Ositaraliya kugira ngo asabe ibihugu byinshi kureka kugira icyaha igikorwa cyo guhuza ibitsina ku babihuje.
Yavuze ko yabishyize hanze kubera ko yumvaga afite amahirwe yo kubasha kubaho yisanzuye nta ngingimira kandi yifuzaga guha abandi "icyizere."
Umukinnyi watsindiye shampiyona y’isi inshuro eshatu yavuze ko gukundana n’umugabo w’umunyamerika utunganya filime, Dustin Lance Black, bahuye mu 2013; "byamutunguye."
Daley yashyingiranwe n’uwatsindiye igihembo cya Oscar, umurusha imyaka 20, umwaka ushize ariko avuga ko ikinyuranyo cy’imyaka kitigeze kiba ikibazo.
"Iyo unyuze mu bintu byinshi ufite imyaka mito"; aha yavugaga ko yagiye mu mikino ya Olempike bwa mbere afite imyaka 14 kandi se umubyara akaba yarishwe na kanseri nyuma y’iminsi itatu, avuga ko byari bimugoye kubona umuntu banganya imyaka wahuye nk’ibyo yahuye na byo.
Abo bakundana babaye ababyeyi muri Kamena, babyarana umwana w’umuhungu witwa Robert Ray Black-Daley, maze Daley avuga ko "ibitekerezo bye byose" byahindutse.
Ati: "Iyo uza kumbaza umwaka ushize icyo nari nkeneye kurusha ibindi byose, nari kuvuga ko 'nifuza gutsindira umudari wa zahabu'."
"Urabizi ko, hari ibintu bikomeye cyane kurusha imidari ya zahabu itangwa mu marushanwa ya Olempike.
Umudari natsindiye mu marushanwa ya Olempike ni Robbie."
Umuhungu we yitwa amazina ya se Robert, wapfuye mu 2011 afite imyaka 40 nyuma yo kumusangamo kanseri y’ubwonko.
Daley yavuze ko ise atigeze yemera ko agiye gupfa kandi ko nta kintu cya nyuma yamusabye yari amatike yabo yo kujya mu mikino yagomba kubera i Londere mu 2012; kuko yifuzaga ko bicara mu myanya y’imbere.
Ati: "Ntabwo nashoboraga kumubwira nti: 'wowe papa ntabwo uzabasha kwicara mu myanya y’imbere."
Ati: "Nari mfashe intoki ze ubwo yaheraga umwuka kandi amaze guhumeka umwuka wa nyuma ni bwo nemeye ko yapfuye maze nemera neza ko atari intarumikwa."
Umwaka ukurikiyeho Daley yahatanye mu mikino ya Olempike yo mu 2012 maze yegukana umudari w’umuringa.
Ati: "Narimbizi ko ibi ari byo nari nararose mu buzima bwanjye bwose, kwibirira imbere y’abafana bo mu gihugu cyanjye mu mikino ya Olempike, nta marangamutima yaruta ayo."
Byanatumye agira igitekerezo cy’indirimbo ye ya mbere akunda yitwa Proud by Heather Small, ayo yagiye icurangwa aho ari hose ari kwitegura gukina imikino ya Olempike kandi ikaba igituma ashesha urumeza.
Ikiganiro cya Desert Island Discs kizatambuka kuri radiyo ya BBC Radio 4 ku Cyumweru saa 11:15 z’igitondo ku isaha yo mu Bwongereza.
Umukinnyi wasubiye inyuma witwa Mickelson yashyizwe ku gatebe k’abasimbura mu marushanwa ya Ryder Cup yabaye ku wa Gatandatu
Umukinnyi w’umunyamerika witwa Phil Mickelson azaca agahigo ku Cyumweru ubwo azakina umukino we wa 47 mu marushanwa ya Ryder Cup, ariko bizasaba ko imikinire ye iba myiza kurushaho kugira ngo yirinde kuba yananirwa kugira ibyo ageraho.
Mickelson, ari gukina mu mikino iba buri myaka ibiri ku nshuro ya 12, akaba yarashyizwe ku gatebe k’abasimbura na kapiteni Jim Furyk mu mukino wo gutera udupira tune n’ukinwa n’abakinnyi banwe yabaye ku wa Gatandatu.
Aho kuba ari we ukora ibikorwa by’ibanze nk’uko akenshi akunda kubikora muri Amerika, uwatsinze amarushanwa atanu akomeye umunsi we awugabanyamo kuba ku gatebe k’abasimbura no gukora ku buryo imikinire ye igenda neza kugira ngo akosore ibitagenda neza.
Ntabwo ari gukina neza cyane n’ubwo ageze ku bushorishori bw’umwuga we, umukinnyi w’imyaka 48 ntabwo aba ameze neza mu rwego rw’umubiri kugira ngo akine amarushanwa ya Le Golf National, aho abakina badatera umupira neza babihomberamo.
Kandi niba imikinire ubwayo adahagije, Mickelson, mu mukino wa cyenda wo ku Cyumweru, arahura n’uwatsindiye shampiyona y’ubwongereza yitwa British Open ari we Francesco Molinari, wakinanye n’umukinnyi ukibitangira witwa Tommy Fleetwood kugira ngo batsinde imikino yabo yose uko ari ine muri iki cyumweru.
Niba abanyamerika, batarabona amanota ane nyuma yo gutangira imikino 12 umwe umwe, batangira irushanwa ku buryo bukomeye, umukino wa Mickelson ushobora kuba ari umukino w’ingenzi cyane.
Furyk yagaragaje icyizere uwo mugabo yifitiye, nubwo nta kindi kinini ashobora kubivugaho.
Furyk ati: "Arumva neza uruhare rwe yari afite uyu munsi, yankubitse agashyi ku mugongo maze anshyira ukuboko ku rutugu maze ambwiraza ko yiteguye ejo hazaza."
"Yifitiye icyizere cyinshi cyane.
Ari umwe mu bakinnyi b’ibirangirire kandi yatanze umusanzu munini muri aya makipe mu minsi yashize ndetse no muri iki cyumweru.
Ntabwo nari nigeze mbona ko ashobora gukina imikino ibiri.
Nari nabonye byinshi biruseho, ariko uburyo byagenze ndetse n’uburyo twari twatekereje ko biri bugende.
Yifuza gukina nk’undi uwo ari we wese."
Mickelson azaca ku gahigo kari gafitwe na Nick Faldo kuba yarakinnye imikino myinshi mu irushanwa rya Ryder Cup ari ku Cyumweru.
Bishobora kuba ari iherezo ryo gukina mu irushanwa rya Ryder Cup rikaba ritarahuye na gato n’uduhigo yagezeho nk’umukinnyi ku giti cye.
Mickelson yatsinze inshuro 18, atsindwa inshuro 20 maze anganya inshuro zirindwi, nubwo Furyk yavuze ko kuba ahari bituma ikipe ari iby’agaciro.
Asobanura ko: "Arasetsa, aratebya, ni umunyabwenge, akunda gusebya abantu kandi ni umugabo mwiza umuntu yakwifuza kugira mu cyuma ikipe irimo."
"Ntekereza ko abakinnyi bakiri bato bishimiye kuba bari kumwe na we, iki cyumweru bikaba byari byiza kubirebesha amaso.
Atanga byinshi birenze gukina."
Kapiteni w’Uburayi, Thomas Bjorn, azi ko kuba ayoboye n’amanota menshi bishobora kuyoyoka bidatinze
Thomas Bjorn, kapiteni w’Uburayi, azi ko kuyobora n’amanota menshi kugeza ku munsi wa nyuma w’imikino ikinwa n’umukinnyi umwe mu marushanwa ya Ryder Cup bishobora guhinduka nabi mu buryo bworoshye.
Ikipe ya Dane yatangiye gukina umukino wa 1997 muri Valderrama, aho ikipe yari iyobowe na kapiteni witwa Seve Ballesteros yari imbere n’amanota atanu barusha abanyamerika ariko ni bo baje kurangiza bari imbere ku manota make, batsindira kuri 14½-13½.
"Ukomeza kwiyibutsa ko twari tuyoboye n’amanota menshi muri Valderrama; twari tuyoboye muri Brookline, aho yatsinzwe no muri Valderrama, aho yatsinze, ariko ni ibyo gusa," byavuzwe na Bjorn, uri ku ifoto, nyuma yo kureba abakinnye imikino yo mu 2018 batsinda 5-3 mu mikino yo ku wa Gatanu n’ejo hashize bayoboye n’amanota 10-6 mu marushanwa ya Le Golf National.
Rero, amateka azanyereka ndetse n’abandi muri iyo kipe ko bitarangiye.
Ariko uzakoresha imbaraga zose ejo.
Usohoke maze ukore ibintu byiza gusa.
Ntabwo byari byarangira kugeza ubonye amanota yandikwa ku rubaho.
Dufite intego kandi ni ukugerageza gutsindira iki gikombe, aho akaba ari ho twibanze.
Nabivuze kuva kera, nshobora kwibanda ku bakinnyi 12 bari ku ruhande rwacu, ariko tunazi ikiduhagaze imbere ku rundi ruhande; abakinnyi bakomeye ku rwego rw’isi."
Bjorn akomeza avuga ko ashimishijwe ni uko abakinnyi banjye bakinnye ku kibuga cya gorufe kitari cyoroshye, agira ati: "Ntabwo nshobora kuza imbere ubwanjye muri aya marushanwa.
Ejo hari ibikomeye kurushaho.
Ejo ni imikinire y’umuntu ku giti cye igomba kugaragazwa kandi ni ryo tandukaniro ry’ibyo dukwiye gukora.
Ni byiza kuba uri kumwe n’uwo mukinana iyo ibintu biri kugenda neza, ariko ni ryari uri gukina ku giti cyawe bwite, noneho ukagerageza ubushobozi bwawe bwose nk’umukinnyi wa gorufe.
Ubu ni bwo butumwa ugomba guheraza abakinnyi, bukaba bugamije gutuma bitanga uko bashoboye ejo.
Ubu ngubu, usiga iby’uwo mukinana inyuma maze ugende maze wibyaze umusaruro ubwawe, nawe ubwawe."
Ku bitandukanye na Bjorn, nomero itandukanye n’iyambarwa na Jim Furyk azareba uko abakinnyi be bitwara kugira ngo bakine neza ku giti cyabo kurusha uko babikoze n’abo bakinna, umwihariko ni ukuba Jordan Spieth na Justin Thomas, babonye amanota atatu muri ane.
Furyk ubwe yari ku mpera zombi z’umunsi wa nyuma w’amarushanwa, aho yabaye umwe mu ikipe yatahukanye itsinzi muri Brookline mbere yo gutsindwa ubwo Uburayi bwikuraga mu marushanwa yiswe "Miracle at Medinah."
"Ndibuka uko buri jambo ribigize," yabivuze ubwo yasubizga igihe yari abajijwe uko Ben Crenshaw, wari kapiteni y’ikipe yo mu 1999, yafashemo abakinnyi kugeza ku munsi wa nyuma.
"Dufite imikino 12 y’ingenzi ejo, ariko mugomba gutangira mwihuse nk’uko mwabibonye muri Brookline, nk’uko mwabibonye muri Medinah.
Iyo imbaraga ziri kugana mu ruhande rumwe, bishyira igitutu ku bari gukina imikino yo hagati.
Dushyiraho abakinnyi bari bukine hakurikijwe umukino ndetse no gusohora abakinnyi mu buryo bubereye twumva ko turi bukunde, murabizi, turi kugerageza gukora ibitangaza ejo."
Thomas yahawe umukoro wo kugerageza kuyobora ikipe kugira ngo yigaranzure maze ihure na Rory McIlroy mu mukino w’ishiraniro, hamwe na Paul Casey, Justin Rose, Jon Rahm, Tommy Fleetwood na Ian Poulter ndetse n’abandi banyaburayi bari mu gice cy’imbere cy’amarushanwa.
Bjorn avuga ku guhitamo abakinnyi bakina imikino ikinwa n’umukinnyi umwe: "Najyanye n’iri tsinda ku buryo bukurikira kubera ko ntekereza ko ririmo abakinnyi bose bazifashishwa."
Ubwato bushya bw’intambara bw’Ubudage bwongera guhindurira igihe
Ubwato bw’intambara bushya bw’Ubudage bwakabaye bwarahawe uburenganzira bwo kujya mu nyanja mu mwaka wa 2014 kugira ngo busimbure amato yashaje yakoreshwaga mu ntambara y’ubutita, ariko ntabwo bwari bwaboneka kugeza byibuze umwaka utaha bitewe na sisitemu idakora neza ndetse n’ibiguzi byo hejuru, nk’uko bitangazwa n’ibinyamakuru byo muri ako gace.
Guha uburenganzira bwo kujya mu nyanja ubwato bwa "Rheinland-Pfalz," akaba ari bwo bwato buyobora ubundi mu bwato bufite ikirango gishya cyo mu bwoko bwa Baden-Wuerttemberg, byarasubitswe kugeza mu gihe cya mbere cya 2019, hakurikijwe ibivugwa n’ikinyamakuru cya Die Zeit aho cyanditse amagambo yavuzwe n’umuvugizi w’igisirikare.
Ubwo bwato bwakabaye byarasanze andi mato y’intambara mu 2014, ariko habayeho ibibazo bwo kubwohereza mu nyanja bituma uwo mushinga ukomeye ujya mu bibazo.
Amato ane yo mu bwoko bwa Baden-Wuerttemberg, ni amato yatumijwe n’ingabo zirwanira mu mazi mu mwaka wa 2007 aho yagomba kuza gusimbura amato yashaje yo mu bwoko bwa Bremen.
Birumvikana ko agomba kuba afite imizinga ikomeye, amoko ya misire zitandukanye aburinda ibisasu by’indege n’iby’amato ndetse n’ikoranabuhanga ryo kwinjira mu mazi y’umwanzi ntawe uyarabutse, nko kugabanya uburyo abonwamo na radari, ibimenyetso by’imirasire y’umutuku ndetse no kumva n’ibyuma bifata amajwi.
Ikindi k’ingenzi kigize ayo mato harimo kuba yasanwa hashize igihe kirekire, bigomba kuba bishoboka ko hakwiye gushyirwa mu nyanja amato mashya kugeza byibuze mu myaka ibiri avuye ku cyumbu kitari icyo mu gihugu yaturutsemo.
Icyakora, gukomeza gutinda bivuze ko amato arimo ikoranabuhanga rigezweho, nk’uko byavuzweho ko ashobora gutuma Ubudage buteganya kugira imbaraga mu mahanda, iryo koranabuhanga rizaba ritakijyanye n’igihie mu gihe azaba atangiye gukoreshwa, bikaba bivugwa n’ikinyamakuru cya Die Zeit.
Ubwo bwoto butaziye igihe bwo mu bwoko bwa F125 bwagarutsweho mu binyamakuru umwaka ushize, ubwo ishami ry’abasirikare b’abadege barwanira mu mazi ryanze ku mugaragaro guha uburenganzira ubwo bwato ngo bujye mu nyanja maze bukabusubiza ahakorerwa amato hitwa Blohm & Voss muri Hamburg.
Ni bwo bwari ubwa mbere igisirikare kirwanira mu mazi cyasubije ubwato muri sosiyete yabukoze nyuma yo kubugemura.
Nta mpamvu nini izwi yateye kuba bwarasubijweyo, ariko ibinyamakuru byo mu Budage byuvze ko hari inenge nyinshi kandi zikomeye muri "porogaramu n’imashini" zatumye ubwato ntacyo bwamara igihe bujyanywe ku rugamba.
By’umwihariko, inenge za porogaramu zari zikomeye cyane mu gihe amato yo mu bwoko bwa Baden-Wuerttemberg aba azakoreshwa n’itsinda ry’abasare 120, bikaba ari igice cy’abasare bakoreshaga ubwato bushaje bwo mu bwoko bwa Bremen.
Kandi, byagaragaye ko ubwato bufite ibiro byinshi ku buryo butangaje bikaba bigabanya imikorere yabwo bikanatuma ubushobozi bw’ingabo zirwanira mu mazi bugabanuka mu kugira ibyongerwa ku bwato byavuguruwe mu minsi iri imbere.
Ubwato bwa "Rheinland-Pfalz" bupima toni 7 000 bugaragara ko buremereye inshuro zikubye kabiri ubwato bwo mu bwoko bumwe bwakoreshejwe n’abadage mu ntambara y’isi ya kabiri.
Usibye imashini zifite inenge, igiciro cy’umushinga wose, harimo no gutoza abasare, na byo biri kuba ikibazo.
Bivugwa ko cyageze kuri miriyari 3,1 z’amayero (miriyari 3,6 z’amadorali y’Amerika), bivuye kuri miriyari 2,2 z’amayero zari zateganyijwe.
Ibibazo byibasiye ayo moko mashya y’ubwato biri kugarukwaho cyane mu gihe haherutse gutangwa gasopo y’uko imbaraga z’igisirikare kirwanira mu mazi cy’abadage ziri kugabanuka.
Mu ntangiriro z’uyu mwaka, Hans-Peter Bartels, umuyobozi mukuru wa komite ishinzwe ubwirinzi mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko y’Ubudage, yemeye ko igisirikare kirwanira mu mazi kuri ubu "kiri kubura amato yakoreshwa mu gihe hagiye kugabwa igitero."
Uwo muyobozi yavuze ko ikibazo cyagiye gikura uko ibihe bisimburana, kubera ko amato ashaje yaretse kugendera mu nyanja ariko nta yandi mato ayasimbura yigeze atangwa.
Yiganyiye avuga ko nta bwato na bumwe bwo mu bwoko bwa Baden-Wuerttemberg bwabashije kujyanwa mu ngabo zirwanira mu mazi.
Umuryango wa National Trust wumviriza ubuzima bw’ibanga bw’uducurama
Ubushakashatsi bushya buri gukorwa mu nyubako iri mu misozo miremire yo muri Ekose bugamije kugaragaza uko uducurama dukoresha iyo misozi kugira ngo duhige ibiribwa.
Hizerwa ko ibizava muri ubwo bushakashatsi bizagaragaza neza imyitwarire yihariye y’inyamabere bigurukuka ndetse no gufasha kumenya uko hakorwa ibikorwa byo kuzisigasira.
Ubushakashatsi buri gukorwa n’abanyasiyanse bo mu muryango wa National Trust for Scotland buzakurikirana uducurama dusanzwe n’uducurama tutadasnzwe ndetse n’uducurama twuzwiho kugira amatwi maremare tw’ikigina n’uducurama two mu bwoko bwa Daubenton mu busitani bwa Inverewe Gardens muri Wester Ross.
Utwuma dufata amajwi twihariye tuzashyirwa ahantu h’ingenzi kuri iyo nyubako kugira ngo hakurikiranwe ibikorwa by’uducurama mu mwaka wose.
Umukozi ukorera umuryango wa NHS n’abakorerabushake na bo bazakora ubushakashatsi bagenda bakoresheje utwuma dutahura aho uducurama duherereye dufatwa mu ntoki.
Isesengura ry’amajwi rikozwe n’inzobere ry’ayo majwi yose yafashwe rizemeza umurongo uducurama tuvuganiraho ndetse n’ubwoko bw’uducurama dukora ibikorwa runaka.
Ikarita y’aho uducurama tuba na raporo bizatangwa kugira ngo hashyirweho ishusho isobanuye ku buryo burambuye yerekana imyitwarire yatwo.
Rob Dewar, umujyanama mu byo kubungabunga ibidukikije ukorera umuryango wa NTS, yizera ko ibizava muri ubwo bushakashatsi bizagaragaza ibice biturwamo by’ingenzi cyane ku ducurama ndetse ni uko bikoreshwa na buri bwoko bw’uducurama.
Aya mnakuru azafasha mu kumenya ibyiza byo gucunga aho uducurama tuba nko gushyiraho ubwatsi buribwa n’udusimba ni uko hasigasirwa ibiti byarikwamo n’uducurama ndetse n’andi moko bifitanye isano ya hafi.
Uducurama muri Ekose no mu Bwongereza twagiye tugabanuka cyane mu kinyejana gishize.
Turibasiwe bitewe n’inyubako n’imirimo y’iterambere ibangamira ibyari byatwo ndetse no kubura aho tuba.
Tiribine zikoreshwa n’umuyaga ndetse n’urumuri na byo byatera ibibazo ndetse n’ibipapuro bijyanwa n’umuyaga n’imiti imwe n’imwe iterwa ku bikoresho by’inyubako ndetse no kuba twasagarirwa n’injangwe zororerwa mu ngo.
Ubusanzwe, uducurama turareba.
Icyakora, bitewe no kuba dusanzwe duhiga mu ijoro amatwi yatwo ni ingenzi cyane kurusha amaso yatwo iyo turi gufata icyo turi guhiga.
Dukoresha tekiniki yo kumenya aho ikintu giherereye hegendewe ku ijwi kugira ngo tumenye neza aho udukoko duto duherereye neza ndetse n’imbogamizi ziri aho tuguruka tugana.
Umuryango wa NTS, ushinzwe kwita ku nyubako z’amateka zirenga 270, ubusitani bw’ingenzi 38 ndetse na hegitari 76 000 by’ubutaka mu bice by’igihugu, wita ku ducurama ku buryo bukomeye.
Ufite inzobere icumi zabihuguriwe, zikora ubushakashatsi ku buryo buhoraho, zigenzura ibyari by’uducurama ndetse rimwe na rimwe zikarokora uducurama.
Umuryango wanashyizeho icyanye cyihariye muri Ekose akaba ari na cyo cya mbere kigenewe uducurama mu nyubako ya Threave muri Dumfries na Galloway, hakaba hari amoko umunani mu moko icumi y’uducurama aboneka muri Ekose.
Umuyobozi ushinzwe kugenzura inyubako, David Thompson, avuga ko iyo nyubako ari ko gace keza ku ducurama.
Ati: "Hano muri Threave, ni ho hari agace keza kabereye uducurama."
"Dufite inyubako zishje, ibiti bikuze cyane ndetse n’ahantu heza uducurama twakwarika.
Ariko hari byinshi ku ducurama bitari byamenyekana, rero akazi dukora hano no mu zindi nyubako ni ukudufasha gusobanukirwa biruseho ibyo dukeneye kugira ngo dukomeze twororoke."
Ashimangira umumaro wo kugenzura ahari uducurama mbere yo gukora imirimo yo gusana inyubako kubera ko gusenya umuntu atabanje kureba icyari kirimo agacurama k’ingore bishobora kwica uducurama tw’ingore tukiri duto tugera kuri 400, bika byatuma ubwo bwoko bwose buzima.
Uducurama turarinzwe kandi kutwica, kudusagarira cyangwa kutubangamira cyangwa kwangiza ibyari byatwo bihanwa n’amategeko.
Elisabeth Ferrell, umuyobozi w’umunya Ekose ukorera umuryango ubungabunga uducurama uzwi nka Bat Conservation Trust, yashishikarije rubanda kuza bagatanga ubufasha.
Ati: "Turacyafite byinshi byo kwiga ku byerekeye uducurama twacu kandi hari menshi mu moko yacu tutazi uko uducurama tubamo tumerewe."
Ronaldo yamaganye ibirego byo gufata ku ngufu mu gihe abunganizi mu by’amategeko biteguye kujyana mu nkiko ikinyamakuru cyo mu Budage
Cristiano Ronaldo avuga ko ibirego byo gufata ku ngufu ashijwa ari "amakuru y’ibihuha," avuga ko abantu "bifuza kwimenyekanisha ubwabo" bakoresheje izina rye.
Abunganizi mu by’amategeko be barateganya kurega ikinyamakuru cyo mu Budage cyitwa Der Spiegel, cyatangaje ibyo birego.
Umukinnyi ukinira ikipe y’igihugu ya Porutigari n’ikipe ya Juventus ukina asatira yashijwe kuba yarafashe ku ngufu umunyamerikakazi witwa Kathryn Mayorga, mu cyumba cya hoteri cyo muri Las Vegas mu mwaka wa 2009.
Bivugwa ko yamwishyuye amadorali 375 000 kugira ngo aceceke ntazavuga ku byabaye, nk’uko ikinyamakuru cya Der Spiegel cyabitangaje ku wa Gatanu.
Avugira muri videwo y’imbonankubone kuri Instagram avugana n’abamukurikira bagera kuri miriyoni 142 amasaha make ibyo birego bimaze gutangazwa, Ronaldo, w’imyaka 33, yamaganye ibyavuzwe avuga ko ari "amakuru y’ibihuha."
"Oya, oya, oya, oya, oya.
Ibyo bavuze uyu munsi, ni amakuru y’ibihuha," umukinnyi watsindiye igihembo cya Ballon d'Or inshuro eshanu yabivugiye imbere ya kamera.
"Bifuza kwimenyekanisha ubwabo bakoresheje izina ryanjye.
Birasanzwe.
Bifuza kumenyekana bavuze izina ryanjye, ariko ni kimwe mu bigize akazi dukora.
Ndi umugabo wishimye kandi byose bimeze neza," uwo mukinnyi yabyongeyeho aseka.
Abunganizi mu by’amategeko ba Ronaldo bari gutegura kurega ikinyamakuru cya Der Spiegel cyatangaje ibyo birego, bakaba barabyise "gutangaza amakuru ku buryo butemewe ibirego bikekwa ku buzima bwite bw’umuntu," hakurikijwe ibivugwa n’ibiro ntaramakuru by’abongereza byitwa Reuters.
Umwunganizi mu by’amategeko witwa Christian Schertz yavuze ko uwo mukinnyi yashaka uko ahabwa impozamarira ku "kwangiza imico ye myiza bitewe n’uburemere bw’akarengane, bikaba bishobora kuba ari ukurenga cyane ku burenganzira bwa muntu mu myaka ishize."
Ibyo birego bivugwa ko byabaye muri Kamena June 2009 bikabre a muri hoteri ya Palms Hotel and Casino muri Las Vegas.
Nyuma yo guhurira mu kabyiniro, Ronaldo na Mayorga bavugwaho kuba barasubiranye mu cyumba cy’uwo mukinnyi, aho bivugwa ko yamufashe ku ngufu mu kibuno, hakurikijwe impapuro zatanzwe n’Urukiko rw’ibanze rw’Intara ya Clark muri Nevada.
Mayorga avuga ko Ronaldo yapfukamye nyuma ibyo bimaze kuba maze akamubwira ko "99 ku ijana" ari "umuntu mwiza" akaba atengushywe n’iryo "rimwe ku ijana."
Inyandiko zivuga ko Ronaldo yemeje ko abo bombi bakoranye imibonano mpuzabitsina, ariko bakaba bari babyumvikanyeho.
Mayorga anavuga ko yagiye kuri Polisi kandi afite amafoto yafotowe ibikomere yagize ari kwa muganga, ariko nyuma aza kumvikana gukemura ikibazo hatabayeho kujya ku nkiko kuko yumvaga "afite ubwoba bw’uko habaho kwihotera" kandi yari anahangayikishijwe ni uko "yakozwa isoni mu ruhame."
Umunyamideri w’imyaka 34 avuga ko ubu ari gushaka guhindura ibyo bumvikanye kuko akomeje guhungabanywa n’ibyabaye.
Ronaldo yarari hafi kujya mu ikipe ya Real Madrid avuye muri Manchester United mu havugwaga ko yaba hari uwo yasagariye kandi muri iyi mpeshyi yagiye mu ikipe ikomeye ya Juve aguzwe miriyoni 100 z’amayero.
Kuva mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi k’Ubwongereza bizwi nka Brexit: Ubwongereza 'bushobora kwicuza ubuziraherezo' nyuma yo kubura inganda zikora imodoka
Ubwongereza "bushobora kwicuza ubuziraherezo" bubuze izina bufite nk’ubwa mbere ku isi mu gukora imodoka nyuma yo kuva mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi, bikaba bitangazwa n’Umunyamabanga ushinzwe ubucuruzi witwa Greg Clark.
Yongeraho ko "bihangayikishije” ko uruganda rwa Toyota rwo mu Bwongereza bwabwiye BBC ko Ubwongereza nibuva mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi nta kumvikana kubayeho ruzahagarika by’igihe gito gukorera imodoka mu ruganda rwayo ruri i Burnaston, hafi ya Derby.
Clark ati: "Tukeneye kumvikana."
Uruganda rukora imodoka rukomoka mu Buyapani bwavuze ko ingaruka zo gutinda ku mupaka zabaho mu gihe nta bwumvikane bubayeho igihe Ubwongereza bwaba buvuzuye mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi byatuma habura akazi kenshi.
Uruganda rwa Burnaston; rukora imodoka za Auris na Avensis za Toyota, rwakoze hafi imodoka 150 000 mu mwaka ushize aho 90% by’izo modoka zajyanwe gucururizwa hanze mu bihugu biri mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi.
Marvin Cooke, umuyobozi ushinzwe uruganda rwa Toyota ruri i Burnaston ati: "Igitekerezo cyanjye ni uko niba Ubwongereza buvuye mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi mu mpera za Werurwe, hazabaho gukora imodoka mu ruganda rwacu."
Izindi nganda zikorera imodoka mu Bwongereza zagaragaje ubwoba bw’uko kuva mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi nta masezerano abayeho ku buryo ubucuruzi ndengamupaka buzakorwamo, harimo Honda, BMW na Jaguar Land Rover.
Urugero, BMW ivuga ko izafunga uruganda ruto ruri muri Oxford nyuma y’ukwezi kumwe Ubwongereza buvuye mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi.
Impungenge zikomeye ni uko inganda zikora imodoka bavuga ko uko babona ibikoresho ni uko bacuruzwa ibicuruzwa biri mu bibazo mu gihe nta bwumvikane bubayeho nyuma y’aho Ubwongereza buviriye mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi.
Uruganda rwa Toyota ruri gukora ku buryo bwo "kugabanya igihe gukora imodoka bimara”, aho ibikoresho bihagera buri minota 37 bivuye ku babigemura yaba mu Bwongereza no mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi kugira ngo hakorwe imodoka zatumijwe.
Igihe Ubwongereza buviriye mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi nta masezerano abayeho tariki ya 29 Werurwe, hashobora kubaho igahagarikwa ry’ibikorwa ku mpaka aho urwo ruganda ruvuga ko ibshobora gutuma habaho gutinda ndetse n’ubuke bw’ibikoresho.
Ntibyapfa gushoboka ko Toyota ishobora kuba yabika imodoka zakozwe mu munsi umwe mu bubiko ifite mu ruganda ruri i Derbyshire, sosiyete ni ko yabivuze kandi bishobora guhagarika ikorwa ry’imodoka.
Bwana Clark avuga ko umugambi wa Theresa May wo kuva mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi hari ibyo uteganya ku mibanire n’Umuryango w’ubumwe bw’Ubuaryi "wagize ibyo uhindurwamo neza kugira ngo hirinde ko habaho igenzura rikomeye ku mupaka."
"Tugomba kugirana amasezerano. Aganira n’ikiganiro cya Today cyo kuri radiyo ya BBC Radio 4 yagize ati: “Turifuza ko tugirana amasezerano meza azatuma tutagera ku ntego gusa muri iki gih ahubwo ko byatuma tunabasha kubona ayo mahirwe."
"Ikigaragara ni uko atari kuri Toyota gusa ahubwo ari no ku zindi nganda zikora imodoka aho dukeneye kubasha gukomeza ibyakabaye uburyo bwo kubona ibikoresho no kugemura ibicuruzwa bigera ku ntego."
Toyota ntiyabashije kuvuga igihe gukora imodoka bizahagararira, ariko mu gihe kirekire, yaburiye ko ibiguzi byiyongera bizagabanya uko uruganda ruhangana ku isoko maze bitagtuma habura akazi kenshi.
Peter Tsouvallaris, wakoreye i Burnaston mu gihe cy’imyaka 24 kandi akaba ari mu bagize sendika y’abakozi muri urwo ruganda, avuga ko abanyamuryango be bakomeje kugira impungenge: "Nkurikije uko ibintu mbibona, iyo imirimo imwe n’imwe ikuweho ntiyigera igaruka.
Umuvugizi wa leta yagize ati: "Tugomba gushyiraho gahunda ihamye kandi yizewe y’ahazaza hacu ku mibanire n’Umuryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi."
Guhura kwa Trump na Rosenstein gushobora kongera gutinzwa nk’uko bitangazwa n’Ibiro bya Perezida w’Amerika
Guhura gukomeye kwa Donald Trump n’intumwa nkuru ya leta yungirije, Rod Rosenstein, bishobora "kwigizwa inyuma ho ikindi cyumweru" mu gihe guhangana ku watoranyijwe ngo ahagararire urukingo rw’ikirenga, Brett Kavanaugh, bikomeje; ibyo byatangajwe n’Ibiro bya Perezida w’Amerika kuri iki Cyumweru.
Rosenstein agenzura imirimo y’umujyanama whariye Robert Mueller, uri gukora iperereza ku kwivanga k’Uburusiya mu matora, imikoranire hagati y’abafasha Trump n’Uburusiya ndetse no kuba perezida yabuza ko ubutabera bukora akazi kabwo.
Byaba bishoboka cyangwa bidashoboka ko Trump yirukana intumwa nkuru ya leta, ndetse no kuba byashyira mu kaga ubwigenge bwa Mueller, byatije umurindi ibihuha by’i Washington mu mezi menshi.
Mu ntangiriro z’uku kwezi, ikinyamakuru cya New York Times cyatnagaje ko Rosenstein yaganiye yambaye utwumva dufata amajwi kugira ngo afata amajwi y’ikiganiro yagiranye na Trump ndetse no kuba bishoboka ko perezida yakweguzwa hakurikijwe ivugurura ry’ingingo ya 25 yo mu Itegeko Nshinga ry’Amerika.
Rosenstein yahakanye ibyatangajwe.
Ariko ku wa Mbere ushize, yagiye mu Biro bya Perezida w’Amerika, hari ibivugwa ko ashobora kwegura.
Ahubwo, inama yagiranye na Trump, waruri ku cyicaro cy’Umuryango w’Abibumbye i New York, yatangajwe ku wa Kane.
Trump yavuze ko "yahitamo" kutirukana Rosenstein ariko noneho inama yagomba kubahuza irasubikwa bitewe ni uko yirindaga guhura na Komite ya Sena ishinzwe ubutabera ku iburanisha aho Kavanaugh n’umwe mu bagore bamushinja kuba yaragize imyitwarire idahwitse mu byerekeye imibonano mpuzabitsina, Dr Christine Blasey Ford, bombi batanze ubuhamya.
Ku wa Gatanu, Trump yasabye ko FBI ikora iperereza ku birego biregwa Kavanaugh, birushaho gutinza amatora asesuye ya Sena.
Umunyamabanga ushinzwe itangazamakuru wa Trump, Sarah Sanders, yagaragaye kuri televiziyo ya Fox News ku Cyumweru.
Abajijwe ibyerekeye inama na Rosenstein, yagize ati: "Ni itariki itari yemeranywaho, bishobora kuba uku kwezi, ishobora no kwigizwayo ikindi cyumweru bitewe n’ibindi bintu biri kuba mu rukiko rw’ikirenga.
Ariko twese tuzareba uko bizagenda kandi nzahora mpa amakuru mashya ibitangazamakuru."
Bamwe mu banyamakuru ntibemera ibyo byatangajwe: Sanders ntabwo yigeze atumiza inama mu Biro bya Perezida w’Amerika kuva tariki ya 10 Nzeli.
Host Chris Wallace yibajije impamvu.
Sanders yavuze ko ubuke bw’amakuru mashya butatewe no kwanga abanyamakuru ba televiziyo "bitewe n’imyitwarire yabo idahwitse," nubwo yavuze ko: "Ntemeranya ni uko avuga ko bitwara mu buryo budahwitse."
Noneho yavuze ko kuvugana ku buryo butaziguye hagati ya Trump n’itangazamakuru biziyongera.
"Perezida ajya agira igihe akabazwa ibibazo akanatanga ibisubizo kurusha undi mu perezida wase wamubanjirije," akaba yarabitangaje, abyongera ku byo yari amaze kuvuga ari ko nta gihamya: "Twarebye kuri iyo mibare."
Ibiganiro bitangirwamo amakuru mashya biracyaba, nk’uko bivugwa na Sanders, ariko "iyo itangazamakuru ribonye amahirwe yo kubaza perezida w’Amerika ibibazo ku buryo butaziguye, biba ari byiza cyane kurusha kuvugana nanjye.
Tugerageza kubikora kenshi kandi mwabonye tubikora mu byumweru bike bishize kandi bizatwara umwanya nari gutangamo amakuru mashya igihe mushobora kuvugana na perezid aw’Amerika."
Ku buryo busanzwe, Trump yakira ibibazo iyo ari gusohoka mu Biro bya Perezida w’Amerika cyangwa yitabiriye ikiganiro cyaguyye cyangwa ari mu nama n’itangazamakuru hari abanyacyubahiro bamusuye.
Kugira na ikiganiro n’itangazamakuru ari wenyine ntibikunze kubaho.
Iki cyumweru i New York, ahari perezida yerekanye impamvu, aho yagiye arenga ku mategeko maze rimwe na rimwe akagaragara ku buryo budasanzwe mbere y’abanyamakuru bateranye.
Umunyamabanga ushinzwe ubuzima yandikiye abakozi bo mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi bakorera ikigo cya NHS Scotland ku bwoba bwatewe ni uko Ubwongereza bugiye kuva mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi
Umunyamabanga ushinzwe ubuzima yandikiye abakozi b’Umuryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi bakorera mu kigo cya NHS kiri muri Ekose agaragaza uko igihugu kibashimira kandi cyifuza ko baguma mu kazi nyuma y’uko Ubwongereza buviriye mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi.
Jeane Freeman, umwe mu bagize Intego ishinga amategeko ya Ekose yoherereje ibaruwa habura amezi atagera kuri atandatu ngo Ubwongereza bwikure mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi.
Leta ya Ekose yamaze kwiyemeza kwishyura ikiguzi cy’abaturage bo mu Muryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi bakora muri serivisi zayo zasheshwe.
Mu ibaruwa yanditse, Madamu Freeman yagize ati: "Mu mpeshyi, ibiganiro hagati y’Ubwongereza n’Umuryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi ku buryo bwavamo byarakomeje, biganira ku cyemezo cyitezwe muri uyu muhindo.
Ariko leta y’Ubwongereza yongere ingufu mu bikorwa byayo byo kwitegura igihe hatabayeho amasezerano.
Ndabizi ko ari ibihe bidukomereye cyane kuri twese.
Ni yo mpamvu nifuzaga kongera kugira icyo mbivugaho kuri ubu ngaragaza uburyo mpa agaciro umusanzu wa buri mukozi, hatitawe ku bwenegihugu bwe.
Abakozi bagenzi banjye baturuka mu bihugu bigize Umuryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi, bazana ubunararibonye n’ubumenyi by’ingirakamaro byongerera imbaraga kandi bikananoza akazi gakorwa muri serivisi z’ubuzima ndetse bikaba ari n’inyungu ku barwayi n’imiryango duha serivisi.
Nta kabuza ko Ekose ari iwanyu kandi turifuza cyane ko muhaguma."
Christion Abercrombie yabazwe ku buryo bwihutirwa nyuma yo gukomereka mu mutwe
Umukinnyi ukina mu b’inyuma w’ikipe ya Tennessee State Tigers witwa Christion Abercrombie yabazwe ku buryo bwihutirwa nyuma yo gukomera ku mutwe mu mukino wabaye ku wa Gatandatu aho batsinzwe 31-27 n’ikipe ya Vanderbilt Commodores, nk’uko bitangazwa n’umuvugizi w’ikipe ya Tennessean witwa Mike Organ.
Umutoza mukuru w’ikipe ya Tennessee State, Rod Reed, yabwiye abanyamakuru ko uko gukomereka kwabaye mbere gato yo kujya mu kiruhuko cy’igice cya mbere.
Reed ati: "Yaje anyuze ku ruhandee maze aba ari ho agwa."
Abatoza n’abaganga bongereye umwuka wa ogisijeni Abercrombie iruhande rw’ikibuga mbere yo kumushyira ku ngombyi no kumujyana kugira ngo asuzumwe byisumbuyeho.
Umukozi wo muri ikipe ya Tennessee State yabwiye umunyamakuru witwa Chris Harris w’ikinyamakuru cya WSMV muri Nashville, Tennessee, ko Abercrombie yavuye aho yabagirwaga mu bitaro bya Vanderbilt Medical Center.
Harris yongeyeho ko "nta bisobanuro byari byaboneka ku buryo yakomeretsemo/igihe azamara" kandi ikipe ya Tennessee State iri kugerageza kumenya igihe uko gukomereka kwabereye.
Abercrombie, umunyeshuri waruri gukina umwaka wa kabiri, ni wo wari umwaka wa mbere we akinira ikipe ya Tennessee State nyuma yo guhabwa taransiferi imuvana Illinois.
Ku Cyumweru, yateye takere mbere yo gusohoka mu mukino, aho b yatumye takere zose yateye zigera kuri 18.
Abaguzi b’abanyamahanga bazajya bacibwa imisoro myinshi ku byangombwa bitangwa na leta igihe baguze umutungo utimukanwa mu Bwongereza
Abaguzi b’abanyamahanga bishyuzwa imisoro myinshi ku byangombwa iyo baguze umutungo utimukanwa mu Bwongereza aho ayo mafaranga arenga bishyuzwa akoresha mu gufasha abatagira aho baba hakurikijwe imigambi mishya y’abanyapolitike bo mu Bwongereza
Ibyo bigamije kuburizamo gutuma umugambi wa Corbyn wo kureshya urubyiruko rutora
Imisoro ku byangombwa bitangwa na leta uzishyuzwa abasanzwe batishyura umusoro mu Bwongereza
Ushinzwe isanduku ya leta irateganya gushaka miriyoni 120 z’amapawundi buri mwaka kugira ngo zifashe abatagira aho baba
Abaguzi b’abanyamahanga bishyuzwa imisoro myinshi ku byangombwa iyo baguze umutungo utimukanwa mu Bwongereza aho ayo mafaranga arenga bishyuzwa akoresha mu gufasha abatagira aho baba , biikaba biri butangazwe na Theresa May uyu munsi
Uwo mugambi ugaragara nk’aho ugamije kugerageza kuburizamo umugambi wa Jeremy Corbyn ntugere ku ntego wari ugamije kureshya urubyiruko rutora aho rusezeranywa ko ruzahabwa amazu ahendutse maze imisoro myinshi ikishyuzwa abakorera menshi.
Kongera imisoro ku byangombwa bitangwa na leta bireba abantu ku giti cyabo n’ibigo bitishyura imisoro mu Bwongereza, aho amafaranga arenga agamije kongerera imbaraga umugambi wa leta wo kurwanya abadafite aho barambika umusaya haboneye.
Uko kwishyuza imisoro ihanitse, bikaba bije byiyongera ku misoro ku byangombwa bya leta isanzweho, harimo ibipimo byo hejuru byazanywe mu myaka ibiri ishizwe ku bashaka kugira inzu ya kabiri n’abagura amazu bagamije kuyakodesha ndetse iyo misoro ikaba igera kuri gatatu ku ijana.
Ushinzwe isanduku ya leta yiteze ko uwo mugambi uzakusanya miriyoni 120 z’amapawundi buri mwaka.
Igereranya ry’ijanisha rya 13 ku nyubako nshya zubatswe i Londere zigurwa n’abadatuye mu Bwongereza, bituma ibiciro byiyongera kandi bigatuma bigora abagura iyo mazu bwa mbere ku buryo bayaturamo.
Mu duce twinshi dutuyemo abakire mu gihugu; by’umwihariko, mu murwa mukuru, hahindutse "imijyi idatuwe" kubera ko umubare munini w’abanyamahanga bagura imitungo itimukanwa bamara igihe kinini batari mu gihugu.
Ingamba nshya zije nyuma y’ibyumweru Boris Johnson asabye ko imisoro y’ibyangombwa bya leta igabanya kugira ngo harusheho gufasha urubyiruko gutunga inzu zabo bwite.
Yashinje amasosiye y’ubwubatsi akomeye ku gutuma ibiciro by’amazu bikomeze kuba bihanitse aho yikubira ubutaka ariko ntibukoreshejwe, maze asaba Madamu May kureka ntihakwe imisoro myinshi ku mazu agura make mu rwego rwo gukemura ikibazo cy’"imiturire giteye inkeke" mu Bwongereza.
Bwana Corbyn yatangaje imigambi myinshi ishishikaje yagiye atanga ku buryo hakorwa amavugururwa, harimo kugenzura amafaranga y’ubukode no gushyira ihereza ku burengaizira bwa ba nyir’amazu bigenga bwo "kwirukana abakodesha nta mpamvu ifatika."
Anifuza guha akanama ububasha bukomeye bwo kubaka amazu mashya.
Madamu May ati: "Umwaka ushize navuze ko nzashyira imbaraga cyane mu kugaruraho inzozi z’abongereza; bikaba ari uko ubuzima bugomba kuba neza kurushaho kuri buri gisekuru gishya.
Kandi ibyo bikaba bivuze ko tugomba gukemura ibibazo bigaragara ku isoko ry’amazu.
Ubwongereza buzakomeza kwakirana yombi abantu bifuza gutura, gukorera no gushakira ubuzima hano.
Icyakora, ntabwo twavuga ko bizorohera abantu bataba mu Bwongereza ndetse n’amasosiyete aba mu mahanga yifuza kugura amazu ku buryo bworoshye nk’abatuye mu Bwongereza bakora cyane.
Ku bantu benshi inzozi zabo zo gutunga inzu zagiye ziyoyoka ku buryo bukomeye, kandi kurara ahantu hatameze neza birarushaho kuba impamo."
Jack Ross: 'Intego yanjye ikomeye ni ugutoza ikipe y’igihugu ya Ekose'
Umutoza w’ikipe ya Sunderland, Jack Ross, avuga ko "intego ye ikomeye" ari ukuba umutoza w’ikipe y’igihugu ya Ekose mu gihe runaka.
Umunya Ekose, w’imyaka 42, ari gushaka uko yakora ibishoboka byose ngo agarura ikipe yo mu majyaruguru y’uburasirazuba mu bihe byiza, iri ku mwanya wa gatatu muri Shampiyona y’icyiciro cya kabiri, ibua amanota atatu ngo ijye ku mwanya wa mbere.
Yagiye gutoreza kuri sitade yitwa Stadium of Light muri iyi mpeshyi nyuma y’aho St Mirren asubiye muri Shampiyona ya Ekose y’ubushize.
"Nifuzaga gukinira igihugu cyanjye nk’umukinnyi.
Nahamagawe mu ikipe ya B bikaba ari ibyo," Ross yabibwiye ikiganiro cya BBC Scotland cyitwa Sportsound.
"Ariko nakuze ndeba ikipe ya Ekose kuri Hampden kenshi ndi kumwe na papa nkiri umwana kandi ni ikintu buri gihe cyatumye nsubirayo.
Ayo mahirwe aza rimwe, igihe nzaba nshobora gutoza neza ikipe."
Ababanjirije Ross nk’abatoza ba Sunderland harimo Dick Advocaat, David Moyes, Sam Allardyce, Martin O'Neill, Roy Keane, Gus Poyet na Paulo Di Canio.
Uwahoze ari umutoza w’ikipe ya Alloa Athletic avuga ko yumva nta bwoba afite nyuma yo gutera ikirenge mu batoza bakomeye batoje iyo kipe ikomeye, aho yigeze kwanga gutoza amakipe arimo Barnsley na Ipswich Town.
"Kugera ku ntego kwanjye kuri ubu bizapimwa no kuba nakwibaza nti: 'Ese nshobora gusubiza iyi kipe muri Shampiyona y’icyiciro cya mbere?'
Ati: “Kubera ko imiterere n’ibikorwaremezo by’iyi kipe, nta gushikanya ko bikwiye kujya muri Shampiyona y’icyiciro cya mbere."
"Ntabwo ari akazi koroshye kuhagera, ariko birashoboka ko nibona ubwanjye gusa nk’ushobora kugera ku ntego hano igihe nshoboye kuba ntasubiza iyi kipe muri iyo shampiyona."
Ross amaze gusa imyaka itatu mu mwuga w’ubutozi, nyuma y’igihe kirekire amaze ari umutoza wungirije mu ikipe ya Dumbarton akaba yaranamaze amezi 15 ari mu batoza b’ikipe ya Hearts.
Yafashije Alloa kutamanuka ngo ijye mu cyiciro cya gatatu maze ahindura ikipe ya St Mirren yari igiye kumanuka mu ngo ijye mu cyiciro cya kabiri, maze yegukana igikombe cya shampiyona umwaka w’imikino wakurikiyeho.
Kandi Ross avuga ko yumva ubu ameze neza nyuma y’ibyo yakoze mu mwuga wo gukina we mu makipe ya Clyde, Hartlepool, Falkirk, St Mirren na Hamilton Academical.
"Byarashobokaga ko inzira zizahura mu buryo bwan yabwo," aribuka ubwo yabivugaga yimeye gutoza ikipe ya Alloa.
"Nta gushidikanya ko natekerezaga ko ubutozi ari cyo kintu cyari cyimbereye kurusha cyane ibyo gukina.
Birasa nk’aho bitangaje ariko ntacyo bitwaye, nabayeho ubuzima bwiza kandi nishimira ibyo nagezeho.
Ariko gukina bishobora kuba bikomeye.
Hari ibintu byinshi ushobora kunyuramo buri cyumweru.
Ndacyabinyuramo ariko biri mu ishusho ya siteresi n’igitutu cy’akazi ariko numva ubutoza ari ikintu cyiza.
Buri gihe nashakashaga gutoza none ubu ni byo ndi gukora, numva ari wo mwuga nakoze ntuje mu buzima bwanjye bwose ndi umuntu mukuru."
Ushobora kumva ikiganiro cyose mu kiganiro cya Sportsound kizatambuka ku Cyumweru, tariki ya 30 Nzeli, kuri radiyo ya Radio Scotland hagati ya 12:00 z’umugoroba na 13:00 z’umugoroba ku isaha yo mu Bwongereza
Igihe gikwiye cyo gufata kamwe ni saa 5:30 z’umugoroba ku wa Gatandatu, bikaba byaragaragajwe n’ubushakashatsi
Izuba ry’igikatu ryo mu mpeshyi ryongeye umubare w’abongereza bagana mu tubari tudahagaze neza ariko bishyira igitutu cyinshi ku maresitora atandukanye.
Amatsinda y’utubari yagize ubwiyongera bwa 2,7 ku ijana by’abatugana muri Nyakanga; ariko abarira muri resitora bagabanutseho 4,8 ku ijana nk’uko imibare ibigaragaza.
Peter Martin, umugishwanama mu by’ubukungu wa sosiyete ya CGA, yakusanyije iyo mibare, yagize ati: "Izuba rikomeje no kuba Ubwongereza bukomeje kugera kure mu marushanwa y’igikombe cy’isi bivuze ko Nyakanga izakurikiza uko Kamena yagenze, ubwo abagana utubari biyongeyeho 2,8 ku ijana, usibye ko amaresitora yo yakomeje kwibasirwa bikomeye.
Igabanuka rya 1,8 ku ijana mu bucuruzi bwa resitora muri Kamena byabaye bibi kurushaho muri Nyakanga.
Utubari dutangirwamo inzoga byagaragaye ko byitwaye neza ku buryo bukomeye kurusha uko amaresitora yarari kugenda asubira inyuma.
Utubari dutangirwamo ibyo kurya na two twakozweho n’izuba, nubwo bitari bikomeye nk’uko byagendekeye amaresitora yonyine.
Bisa nk’aho abantu bifuzaga gusohoka gusa kugira ngo bashake icyo kunywa.
Mu tubari dutandukanye kugurisha inzoga byazemutseho 6,6 ku ijana mu kwezi, aho ibiribwa byagabanutseho gatatu ku ijana."
Paul Newman, ukorera isosiyete ukora ubusesenguzi mu by’imyidagaduro no kwakira abashyitsi ya RSM, yagize ati: "Iyo mibare ikomeza kugenda ihindagurika nk’uko twabibonye guhera mu mpera za Mata.
Imitererere n’ibindi bigira ingaruka ku bikorwa bihuza abantu benshi n’ibya siporo bikomeza kuba ari byo ahanini bituma habaho ihindagurika ry’ubucuruzi bw’ibigurwa bitajyanwa mu rugo.
Ntabwo bitangaje kuko amasosiyete afite za resitora akomeza kugorwa, nubwo ubucuruzi byagabanutseho 4,8 ku ijana mu mwaka birashoboka ko mu buryo bwihariye byababaza bikiyongera ku gitutu cy’ibiguzi kiriho.
Impeshyi ishyushye cyane ntabwo yakabaye yaraje mu gihe kidakwiriye ku masosiyete afite resitora kandi igihe ni cyo kizabitubwira niba ubushyuhe buri mu rugero twabonye muri Kanama buzaduha akaruhuko twari dutegereje."
Igiteranyo cy’ibyagurishijwe mu turabari n’amaresitora, harimo ibyafunguwe bishya, byari 2,7 ku ijana muri Nyakanga, bikaba bigaragaza ukugenda gahoro ko gufungura utubari n’amaresitora bifite amazina.
Urwego rushinzwe gukurikirana ibyagurishijwe ruzwi nka Coffer Peach Tracker rukurikirana utubari n’amaresitora rukusanya rukanasesengura amakuru y’imikorere y’amasosiyete 47 akora ubwo bucuruzi, mu gihe aho byose byinjiza miriyari 9 z’amapawundi kandi bikaba ari ibipimo ngenderwaho muri urwo rwego.
Umwe mu bana batanu afite konti z’ibanga ku mbuga mpuzambaga aho bihisha ababyeyi babo
Umwe mu bana batanu, bamwe muri bo bafite imyaka mike igera kuri 11, bafite konti z’ibanga ku mbuga mpuzambaga aho bihisha ababyeyi n’abarimu babo nk’uko ubushakashatsi bubigaragaza
Ubushakashatsi bwakorewe ku banyeshuri biga mu mashuri yisumbuye bangana na 20 000 bwagaragaje ko hari ubwiyongera bwa paji za "Instagram zitari ukuri"
Ayo makuru agaragaza ubwoba bw’ibijyanye n’ibitsina biri gutangazwa
Makumyabiri ku ijana by’abanyeshuri bavuze ko bafite konti "isanzwe" bereka ababyeyi
Umwana umwe muri batantu, ufite imyaka mike igera kuri 11, bari gushyiraho konti z’imbuga mpuzambaga bagira ibanga bakazihisha abantu bakuru.
Ubushakashatsi bwakorewe ku banyeshuri biga mu mashuri yisumbuye bagera kuri 20 000 bwagaragaje ko hari ubwiyongera bukabije bwa konti za "Instagram zitari ukuri", aho baba bashaka kuvuga ku rubuga rwa Instagram rufasha guhererekanya amafoto.
Ayo makuru agaragaza ubwoba bw’ibijyanye n’ibitsina biri gutangazwa.
Makumyabiri ku ijana by’abanyeshuri bavuze ko bakoresha neza nta bintu bibi bashyira kuri konti "isanzwe" bereka ababyeyi, mu gihe bafite izindi zo mu ibanga.
Umwe mu babyeyi yaguye ku buryo butunguranye kuri site y’ibanga y’umukobwa we w’imyaka 13 asangaho uwo mwangavu ari gusaba abandi ko "bamufata ku ngufu."
Ubushakashatsi bwakozwe n’ikigo cya Digital Awareness UK n’ihuriro ry’abayobozi b’abagore b’ibigo by’amashuri rizwi nka Headmasters" and Headmistresses" Conference (HMC) by’amashuri yigenga, bwabonye ko 40 ku ijana by’abana bafite imyaka kuva kuri 11 kugera kuri 18 bari bafite imyirondoro ibiri, aho igice cy’abo bemeye ko bagira konti z’ibanga.
Umuyobozi wa HMC, Mike Buchanan, yagize ati: "Birababaje cyane kubona abangavu n’ingimbi bari gushukwa bagashyiraho urubuga rwo kuri interineti aho ababyeyi n’abarimu badashobora kubabona."
Eilidh Doyle ni we "uzavuganira abakinnyi" mu nama y’abakinnyi bo muri Ekose
Eilidh Doyle yatorewe kujya mu nama y’abakinnyi bo muri Ekose nk’umuyobozi mukuru utari nshingwabikorwa mu kanama kayoboye mu nama rusange ngarukamwaka.
Doyle ni umukinnyi w’umunyabigwi cyane ukomoka muri Ekose kandi umuyobozi w’akanama witwa Ian Beattie akaba yarasobanuye ko icyo cyemezo ari amahirwe ku bayobozi ba siporo yo kungukira mu bunararibonye bwagutse bwo ku rwego mpuzamahanga mu myaka mirongo ishize.
Beattie ati: "Eilidh yubashywe cyane mu muryango w’abakinnyi bo muri Ekose, Ubwongereza ndetse no ku isi kandi tukaba tuzi neza ko abakinnyi bo muri Ekose bashobora kungukira cyane mu kumuzana muri ako kanama."
Doyle yagize ati: "Nshimishijwe no kuba ijwi ry’abakinnyi kandi ndizera ko nshobora mu by’ukuri gutanga umusanzu no gufasha kuyobora siporo muri Ekose."

Itangazo ryamamaza rya pompe z’amashereka rigereranya ababyeyi n’inka ryatumye abantu batanga ibitekerezo bitandukanye kuri interineti
Sosiyete ikora pompe z’amashereka zatumye abantu batanga ibitekerezo bitandukanye kuri interineti nyuma y’aho itangazo ryamamaza ryageranyije abagore bonsa n’inka ziri gukamwa.
Kugira ngo hatangizwe icyavuzwe ko ari "ipompe y’amashereka idasohora urusaku ya mbere ku isi," sosiyete ikora ibikoresho by’ikoranabuhanga ya Elvie yasohoye itangazo ryamamaza riri mu bwoko bwa videwo y’umuziki ryavugishije abantu benshi kugira ngo ryerekane ubwisanzure ipompo nshya iha abagore bashaka kwigaragaza.
Ababyeyi ba nyabo bane babyinira mu kiraro kirimo ubwatsi bw’inka mu ndirimbo irimo amagambo agira ati: "Yego, ndikama, ariko ntabwo ushobora kumbonana umurizo" kandi "Mu gihe utari wabibonye ntabwo ari amacebe, ahubwo ni amabere yanjye."
Inyikirizo igira iti: "Yapompe asohoke, yapompe asohoke, ndi kugaburira impinja, yapompe asohoke, yapompe asohoke, ndi gukama abagore banjye."
Icyakora, iryo tangazo ryamamaza, ryashyizwe ahagaragara kuri paji ya Facebook ya sosiyete, yatumye habaho kutumvikana kuri interineti.
Aho yarembwe n’abantu 77 000 maze hatangwa ibihumbi by’ibitekerezo, vidwo yakiriwe n’abayireba ku buryo butandukanye, aho benshi bavuga ko ishyira ku karubanda "ibibi" bibera mu ruganda rw’ibikomoka ku mata.
"Ni icyemezo kidahwitse cyo gukoresha inka mu kwamamaza iki gicuruzwa.
Umwe ati: “Kimwe nkatwe zikeneye gutwita kugira ngo zibyare maze zitange amata, keretse niba abana bazo bibwa ku munsi zibabyariyeho."
Ipompo y’amashereka yakozwe na Elvie ikwira neza ku buryo itagaragara mu isutiye y’umubyeyi wonsa (Elvie/Umubyeyi)
Undi yatanze igitekerezo agira ati: "Birumvikana cyane ko biteye ihungabana ku babyeyi n’impinja zabo.
Ariko ni ko bimeze kubera iki batakoresha iryo tangazo ryamamaza ipomo z’amashereka zigenewe ababyeyi bafata umwanzuro wo kugumana impinja zabo?"
Undi yongeraho ati: "Iryo ni itangazo ryamamaza ryarenze umurongo."
Abandi bavuganiye iryo tangazo, aho umugore umwe yemeye ko yasanze iyo ndirimbo "isekeje."
"Ndatekereza ko iki ari igitekerezo cyiza.
Nakabaye narafashe imwe iyo nza kuba nkonsa.
Gupompa byatumye numva meza neza nk’inka.
Itangazo ryamamaza ririmo ubusazi buke ariko narifashe uko rimeze.
Umwe yandika agira ati: “Iki ni igicuruzwa cy’ubwenge."
Undi yatanze igitekerezo agira ati: "Iri tangazo ryamamaza rirasheje aho rigenewe ababyeyi bakama amashereka (akenshi aho bakorera akazi cyangwa mu bwiherero) bakaba bumva bameze nk’"inka."
Ntabwo ari itangazo rishimagiza cyangwa ricira urubanza uruganda rw’ibikomoka ku mata."
Ku musozo wa videwo itsinda ry’abagore rigaragaza ko ryari riri kubyina rifite amapompo atagaragara yacengejwe mu masutiye yabo.
Igitekerezo cyagendeweho muri ubwo bukangurambaga gishingiye ku gitekerezo cy’abagore benshi bakoresha ipompo y’amashereka bavuga ko bumva bameze nk’inka.
Icyakora, ipompo yakozwe n’uruganda rwa Elvie, nta rusaka na ruke isohora, nta migozi cyangwa uduhombo kandi ikwira neza mu isutiye y’umugore wonsa, bigaha umugore ubwisanzure bwo kugenda, gufata impinja zabo ndetse no kujya hanze bari gukama amashereka.
Ana Balarin, umufatanyabikorwa ndetse n’ushinzwe imbonezamikurire y’umwana muto mu kigo cya Mother yatanze igitekerezo agira ati: "Ipompo yakozwe na Elvie ni igicuruzwa cyazanye impinduka kikaba kigomba gushyirwa ku isoko mu buryo budasanzwe.
Mu gushaka kugereranya abagore bari gukora ibyo bashaka n’inka zikamwa, twifuzaga kugaragaza gukama amashereka n’inzitizi zabyo, ari na ko tubyerekana mu buryo bwo gususurutsa n’uburyo bujyanye mu bwisanzure butangaje ipompo izazana.
Si bwo bwa mbere ipompo ya Elvie yavuzwe cyane mu itangazamakuru.
Mu cyumweru cyahariwe imideri i Londere, umubyeyi w’abana babiri yasaga nk’aho ari kwerekana imideri akimbagira yakozwe n’umuhanzi w’imideri witwa Marta Jakubowski ariho arakoresha icyo gicuruzwa.
Abana b’abimukira amagana bajyanywe bucecetse mu nkambi ku mupaka wa Texas
Umubare w’abana b’abimukira bafunzwe wariyongereye cyane nubwo abambuka umupaka buri kwezi batigeze bahinduka cyane, k ruhande rumwe bitewe n’amagambo akomeye n’ingamba zazanywe n’ubutegetsi bwa Trump bwatumye bigorana kurushaho guha abana ababishingira.
Ubusanzwe, abenshi mu bishingizi na bo baba bari abaimukira batagira ibyangombwa kandi bakagira ubwoba bw’uko bashobora gushyira mu byago ubushobozi bwabwo bwo kuguma mu gihugu baramutse baje gusaba ko bahabwa umwana.
Ibyo byago byariyongeye muri Kamena, ubwo inzego za leta zatangazaga ko abashaka kwishingira abo bana n’abandi bantu bakuru bo mu rugo rwabo bagomba gutanga ibikumwe kandi ayo makuru agomba gusangizwa inzego zishinzwe abimukira.
Icyumweru gishize, Matthew Albence, umuyobozi wo mu nzego zo hejuru ukorana n’Urwego rushinzwe abimukira na gasutamo, yatanze ubuhamya imbere ya kongere avuga ko icyo kigo cyafashe abantu mirongo basabye ko bishingira abana batarageza imyaka y’ubukure badaherekejwe n’umuntu mukuru.
Ikigo cyaje kwemeza ko 70 ku ijana by’abo bafashwe batari barigeze bagira ikindi cyaha bakora.
"Hafi 80 ku ijana by’abantu bashaka kuba abishingizi cyangwa abo mu rugo rw’abishingizi bari hano mu gihugu ku buryo butemewe n’amategeko kandi igice kinini cyabo ni abimukira bakoze ibyaha.
Bwana Albence ati: “Rero, dukomeje gukurikirana abo bantu."
Mu gushaka uburyo abana bakorerwa dosiye vuba kurushaho, abayobozi batangije amategeko mashya asaba ko bamwe muri bo bajyanwa mu rukiko mu gihe cy’ukwezi bamaze gufatwa, aho kujyanwa nyuma y’iminsi 60, bikaba ari byo byari bisanzweho hakurikijwe abakora mu bigo byakira abimukira.
Abenshi bagaragara hakoreshejwe kubahamagara kuri videwo murebana, aho kugaragara bahibereye, kugira ngo basabe umucamanza uca imanza z’abimukira ngo barebe ko babona uburyo bwo gutura bwemewe n’amategeko.
Abafatwa ko batujuje ibisabwa ku buryo bakoroherezwa bazahita basubizwa mu gihugu baturutsemo.
Uko abana bakomeza kumara igihe kinini muri kasho, ni ko bishoboka cyane ko bahangayika bakaniheba, bigatuma bagira umujinya uvanze n’amahane no kugerageza gucika, hakurikijwe abakozi bakora mu bigo bicumbikira abimukira na raporo zagaragajwe zivuye muri sisitemu mu mezi make ashize.
Ababakorera ubuvugizi bavuga ko izo mpungenge zigaragazwa mu kigo kinini nka Tornillo, aho hari ibimenyetso by’uko umwana ari kugorwa bika byarushaho kwirengagizwa kubera uko kingana.
Bongeraho ko kwimura abana bakajya mahema nta kubaha igihe gihagije cyo kwiteugra mu rwego rw’amarangamutima no gusezera ku nshuti bishobora gutuma bagira ihungabana benshi bari kurwana na ryo.
Siriya ibwira Amerika, Ubufaransa na Turikiya ko 'ingabo zigaruriye uduce' zigomba guhita zidusubiza
Avugira mu Nama rusange y’Umuryango w’abibumbye, Minisitiri w’ububanyi n’amahanga ari we Walid al-Moualem yanasabye ko impunzi zo muri Siriya zigaruka mu rugo, nubwo intambara iri mu gihugu imaze imyaka umunani kuri ubu ngubu.
Moualem, uri na Minisitiri w’intebe wungirije, yavuze ko ingabo z’amahanga zari ku butaka bwa Siriya ku buryo butemewe n’amategeko zitwaje ko ziri kurwanya iterabwoba” kandi ko zizitabwaho uko bikwiye.”
Abwira inteko rusange ko: "Izo ngabo zigomba gusubirayo ako kanya kandi nta yandi mananiza."
Moualem yashimangiye ko "intambara yo guhashya iterabwoba iri hafi kurangira" muri Siriya, aho abantu barenga 360 000 bapfuye kuva mu 2011, n’amamiriyoni arenga akaba yarakuwe mu byayo.
Yavuze ko Damascus izakomeza "kurwana iyi ntambara ntagatifu kugeza uduce twose twa Siriya twirukanywemo" imitwe y’iterabwoba "n’abanyamahanga bari mu gihugu bitemewe."
Amerika ifite ingabo zigera ku 2 000 muri Siriya, ahanini zigamije guha amahugurwa no kugira inama ingabo z’abakurude n’abarabu b’abanyasiriya bikuye kuri Perezida Bashar al-Assad.
Ubufaransa bufite ingabo zirenga 1 000 ku butaka mu gice cy’igihugu cyashegeshwe n’intambara.
Ku kibazo cy’impanzi, Moualem yavuze ko ibisabwa byari bikwiye kugira ngo bagaruke kandi ko anenga "bimwe mu bihugu byo mu burengerazuba bw’isi" kubera "gutuma abantu bashya ubwoba" bigatuma impunzi ziguma mu mahanga.
Ati: "Twahamagariye imiryango mpuzamahanga n’imiryango itanga ubutabazi koroshya uko bagaruka."
"Bari guhindura politiki icyakabaye ari ikibazo kijyanye no gutabara abantu gusa."
Amerika n’Umuryango w’ubumwe bw’Uburayi byaburiye ko hashobora kutabaho inkunga yo kongera kubaka Siriya kugeza habayeho amasezerano hagati ya Assad n’abatavuga rumwe na we kugira ngo intambara isozwe.
Abadipolomate mu Muryango w’Abibumbye bavuga ko amasezerano aheruka hagati y’Uburusiya na Turikiya agamije gushyiraho zone y’ubuhumekero mu gihe kirimo cyanen ingabo za Idlib bikaba byarashyizeho amahirwe yo guhatira ko habaho ibiganiro bya politiki.
Amasezerano y’Uburusiya na Turikiya yaburijemo igitero simusiga cy’Uburusiya butera inkunga ingabo za Siriya ku ntara ituwemo n’abantu miriyoni eshatu.
Icyakora, Moualem yashimangiye ko amasezerano yashyizeho ku buryo bugaragara "amatariki ntarengwa" kandi agaragaza icyizere cy’uko ibikorwa by’ingabo bitibasira ingabo z’abajihadisite harimo abarwanyi b’umutwe w’iterabwoba wa ukorana na Al-Qaeda witwa Nusra Front, na wo "ukaba uzarandurwa."
Intumwa mu Muryango w’Abibumbye, Staffan de Mistura, yizera ko vuba hazaterana inama ya mbere kuri komite nshya igizwe na leta n’abatavuga rumwe na leta kugira ngo hakorwe umushinga w’itegeko nshinga rya Siriya nyuma y’intambara no gutegura uburyo amatora azakorwamo.
Moualem yashyizeho amabwiriza kuri leta ya Siriya kugira ngo yitabire komite, avuga ko akazi kakozwe n’akanama kagomba kwibanda cyane ku "gusuzuma ingingo ziri mu itegeko nshinga riri gukurikizwa," no kubaburira ko hashobora kuzamo kirogoya.
Kuberai ki Trump azatsindira manda ya kabiri
Hakurikijwe inyurabwenge, Bwana Trump ni we watsinda amatora yo mu 2020, keretse abirebera hafi b’abaliberare bashobora kuba bizera, bakweguza perezida no kuba hari ibibazo bikomeye byaranze ubutegetsi bwe bukarangira imburagihe.
Nta gushidikanya ko "Ari nk’umukino wa nyuma ukomeye wa perezida wigeze ubaho!"
Kugezau bu, nta bimenyetso by’uko ababireba bigeze bananirwa.
Kuva mu 2014, amanota yatangwaga yikubye kabiri kurushaho bigerak uri 1,05 kuri CNN naho bikaba byarikubye bigera kuri miriyoni 1,6 kuri MSNBC.
Fox News ifite impuzandengo y’abayireba b’ibanze bangana na miriyoni 2,4, biyongeyeho 1,7 uhereye mu myaka ine ishize, hakurikijwe ibitangazwa n’ikigo cya Nielsen, naho ikiganiro cya MSNBC cyitwa "The Rachel Maddow Show" kikaba ari cyo kiza imbere kuri televiziyo aho kirebwa n’abantu miriyoni 3,5 mu gihe hatangazwa amakuru akomeye yo mu ijoro.

Amafaranga aturutse mu mahanga ari kwifashishwa cyane mu matora yo mu gihembwe hagati aho abahanganye barushanwa amajwi make cyane
Ntabwo bitangaje ko amatora agiye kuba ku nshuro ya 17 muri Pennsylvania arimo amafaranga menshi cyane, bitewe no guhindura uturere tukagira uburenganzira bwo kubona abajya muri kongere tukaba twarabonye abari muri kongere babiri bari guhatanira umwanya umwe.
Biherutse kongera kugaragaza imirongo y’umujyi wa Pittsburg bishyira uhagarariye abademokarate witwa Conor Lamb; watsindiye umwanya we mu kandi karere mu matora yihariye yabaye mu itumba.
Lamb ahanganye n’undi uri ku buyobozi, umurepubulikani witwa Keith Rothfus, kuri ubu uhagarariye akarere ka kera ka 12 ka Pennsylvania, kakaba gafatanye cyane n’akarere gashya ka 17.
Amakarita yongewe gushushanywa nyuma y’aho Urukiko rw’ikirenga rwa Pennsylvania rwafashe umwanzuro muri Mutarama ko uturere twa kera twahindaguwe ku buryo budakurikije Itegeko nshinga kugira ngo bihe amahirwe abarepubulikani.
Ihangana mu karere ka 17 ryatumye amafaranga yo kwiyamamaza aba ikibazo cy’ingume hagati y’amashyaka akomeye, Komite ishinzwe kwamamaza abademokarate bajya muri kongere (DCCC) na Komite y’igihugu ishinzwe kwamamaza abarepubulikani bajya muri kongere (NRCC).
Lamb yabaye izina rizwi muri Pennsylvania nyuma yo gutsinda arusha abo bahanganye amanota make mu matora yihariye yo muri Werurwe mu karere 18 ka kongere ya Pennsylvania.
Uwo mwanya wari ufitwe n’umurepubulikani akaba yari awumazeho imyaka icumi, naho Perezida Donald Trump yatsinze muri ako karere n’amanota 20.
Abasesenguzi b’ibya politiki bagaragaje ko abademokarate bashobora gutsinda bari imbere n’amanota make.
Amerika iratekereza ku guhana El Salvador kubera gushyigikira Ubushinwa, nyuma iza kubyihorera
Abadipolomate bamenye ko Repubulika y’abadominikani na Panama byamaze kwemera leta ya Beijing, byitaza leta ya Washington.
Bwana Trump yagiranye inama nziza na Perezida Juan Carlos Varela wa Panama muri Kamena 2017 aho anafite hoteri muri Panama kugeza abafatanyabikorwa birukanywe n’itsinda rishinzwe imicungire ry’umuryango witwa Trump Organization.
Abayobozi b’ishami rya leta bafashe icyemezo cyo gusaba ko abayobozi b’abanyamerika bagaruka bavuye mu butumwa bwa diporomasi muri El Salvador, Repubulika y’abadominikani na Panama nyuma y’"ibyemezo biherutse gufatwa ko bitazongera kwemera igihugu cya Tayiwani," Heather Nauert, umuvugizi w’urwego rwa leta yabivugiye mu ijambo yatanze mu ntangiriro z’uku kwezi.
Ariko ibihano byatekerejweho gusa ko byahabwa El Salvador, yahawe amafaranga agereranyije angana na miriyoni 140 z’amadorali y’Amerika nk’inkunga mu 2017, harimo kugenzura ibiyobyabwenge, ubufasha mu by’iterambere n’ubukungu.
Ibihano byasabwe, bikaba birimo kugabanya inkunga y’amafaranga no kugira abantu runaka bimwe viza, bikaba byari kubangamira bikomeye igihugu cyo muri Amerika yo hagati ndetse n’ibipimo by’ubushomeri n’ubwicanyi bigakomeza kuzamuka.
Nk’uko inama yahuzaga ibihugu yakomezaga, abayobozi b’Amerika ya ruguru n’iyo hagati basubitse inama yo ku rwego rwo hejuru yibandaga ku mutekano n’iterambere ry’ubukungu kugira ngo hakurikiranwe iby’inama bisa yabaye umwaka ushize yabonywe nk’intambwe yatewe mu kubuza abimukira kujya muri Amerika.
Ariko hagati muri Nzeli, abayobozi bo ku rwego rwo hejuru basobanuye neza ko bifuzaga ko inama ikomeza, bigahita bikuraho ibyatekerezwaga byose ku guha ibihano El Salvador.
Visi Perezida, Mike Pence, ubu yitezweho gutanga ijambo muri iyo nama, ubu iteganyijwe kuba hagati mu Ukwakira, bikaba ari ikimenyetso cy’imbaraga ubuyobozi bushyira mu nama, nk’uko abadiporomate babivuga.
Kandi intumwa eshatu z’abanyamerika zasubiye mucece muri El Salvador, Panama na Repubulika y’abadominikani aho nta butumwa bukomeye bushya cyangwai bihano byatanzwe na leta ya Washington.
Umuvugizi wa Perezidansi y’Amerika, Bwana Bolton, yanze kugira icyo avuga niba ikiganiro cyarasobanuwe n’abayobozi b’abanyamerika batatu, harimo abadiporomate b abiri, bameye kuganirana ibiganiro byo mu muhezo bifuje ko amazina yabo adatangazwa.
Ibyo bavuze byemejwe n’umusesenguzi wigenga ukorana bya hafi n’ubutegetsi kandi na we yasabye ko amazina ye adatangazwa.
Kwiga amateka
Umuntu ukurikiyeho mu gusezererwa mu kazi ashobora kuba ari umujyanama wihariye witwa, Robert Mueller, kubera raporo yatanze kuri Bwana Trump ko ashobora kuba ari kubangamira ubutabere, aho hari ibimenyetso bifatika mu makuru rusange.
Bwana Mueller yavuze ko ari guhindura iperereza ari gukora kugira ngo arebe niba abashinzwe kwiyamamaza kwa Bwana Trump bafitanye imikoranire n’Uburusiya mu gitero bwagabye ku matora yacu.
Igihe Kongere yaba ihinduriye aho ihagaze, Bwana Trump ashobora kwisanga ari kubazwa ibyo ashinjwa n’urwo rwego, mu gihe yitegura kongera gusubira imbere y’abatora kandi biranashoboka ko ari inteko y’inshuti ze.
Aho ni uguteganya cyane, kandi ntabwo mvuze ko ntatanga igitekerezo cy’uko ihirima Bwana Trump ritakwitegwa, cyangwa se uko afashwe mu Burayi.

Mu 1938, abayobozi b’abadage bari biteguye guhirika ku butegetsi Hitler, iyo abo mu burengerazuba bw’isi bari kuba barihagazeho maze bagashyigikira abacekovake i Munich.
Twarananiwe maze tubura amahirwe yo kubuza ko hamara imyaka myinshi abantu bishwa ariko byabayeho.
Uko amateka yagenze bishingira cyane kuri ibyo bikorwa bikomeye byagiye bibaho kandi urugendo rwa demokarasi rushobora gutizwa umurindi cyangwa gutinzwa.

Rosenstein yarari mu mazi abira kuva aho ikinyamakuru cyatangaje, umwaka ushize, ko yasabye ko hafatwa amajwi mu ibanga ya perezida ndetse no gukwiza ibihuha ko atabereye kuba perezida.
